# MCNF ‚Äî Worklist

The single durable tracker. Tasks lifted from `docs/COMPLIANCE.md` (sweeps 1 & 2, 2026-06-09).
Status: `[ ]` open ¬∑ `[>]` in progress ¬∑ `[‚úì]` done. Each task carries its finding id + verdict.
Ordered by priority ‚Äî security lock first, then largest structural debt, then mechanical/doc cleanup.

**Operator decisions (2026-06-09):** A1/A2 ‚Üí **DELETE** the labwc/sway surface ¬∑ B1/H6/H3/H4 ‚Üí **BUILD/WIRE** them ¬∑ C1 ‚Üí **implement Phase-G** ¬∑ E1 ‚Üí **retarget tests to Nebula**.

## E12 ‚Äî Forked-COSMIC + Magic-Mesh ‚Üí one egui-native mesh desktop OS (operator 2026-06-30; 4-round/16-Q `/plan` survey; design: docs/design/cosmic-magic-mesh-egui.md)

The **headline pivot**: MCNF 12.0 "Quasar" becomes an **egui-native mesh thin-client desktop OS**. **REVISED 2026-06-30** (50-Q `/plan` survey; design: `docs/design/quasar-vdi-desktop.md` ‚Äî supersedes the forked-compositor `cosmic-magic-mesh-egui.md`): the originally-proposed **fork of the COSMIC compositor is RETIRED**. Instead a **single egui shell owns the DRM/KMS seat directly (no compositor)** and **brokers VM desktops** ‚Äî local **cloud-hypervisor** VMs + remote desktops on any mesh peer, rendered **egui-native** (ironrdp/vnc ‚Üí an egui texture) over Nebula. The host runs **no native apps**; a browser/office/game lives **inside a VM guest**. The mesh-control surfaces (Workbench/Files/Music/Voice) are **panels in the one shell**, not separate clients. Carries forward from the first survey: **egui as the one toolkit + the `mde-egui` `Style`/Motion harness** (E12-1, landed). Locks (full table in the design doc): **egui owns DRM** (smithay DRM/GBM runner) ¬∑ **VDI thin client** (fullscreen VM framed by a thin chrome bar that expands to Workbench) ¬∑ **cloud-hypervisor** local VMs (virtio-gpu fast path, dual-homed mesh+LAN) ¬∑ **RDP-primary / VNC-fallback** over Nebula ¬∑ **sessions roam** per-peer (etcd/Syncthing) ¬∑ **mackesd session-broker + vm-lifecycle workers** ¬∑ **immutable bootc image** ¬∑ **¬ß8 envelope raised**, VM guests full flat-trust members ¬∑ **everything in v1** (passthrough/USB/multi-mon/migration). Mesh substrate (¬ß1), Bus (¬ß2), crypto (¬ß3), DoD (¬ß7), planes (¬ß9), build env (¬ß10) carry forward. Build order: DRM runner ‚Üí shell ‚Üí VDI(RDP) ‚Üí remote-over-mesh ‚Üí local KVM ‚Üí advanced ‚Üí panels ‚Üí bootc packaging ‚Üí decommission iced/Carbon.

- [‚úì] **E12-0: Governance rewrite + design lock land.** **As** the platform owner, **I want** `AI_GOVERNANCE.md` re-authored around E12 (Cosmic-era ¬ß4/¬ß5/¬ß6 archived as heritage; ¬ß1-3/¬ß7-10 carried forward) plus this design doc committed, **so that** every downstream task has one authoritative rulebook for the egui/forked-desktop direction. **Acceptance:** AI_GOVERNANCE.md identity header reads MCNF 12.0 + names egui as the toolkit; ¬ß4 (egui/no-Carbon), ¬ß5 (forked desktop + spin), ¬ß6 (layered tiers) reflect the locks; the retired Carbon/libcosmic gates are removed from the doc's gate list; a heritage pointer to the Cosmic-era text exists. ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-30, operator go-ahead): `AI_GOVERNANCE.md` rewritten to MCNF 12.0 "Quasar" (egui ¬ß4, forked-desktop ¬ß5, layered-tiers ¬ß6; ¬ß0-3/¬ß7-10 carried forward; Cosmic-era text archived as heritage); design doc `docs/design/cosmic-magic-mesh-egui.md` landed. E12-1‚Ä¶E12-12 are the execution backlog.
- [‚úì] **E12-1: `mde-egui` harness + shared `Style`/`Visuals` (the foundation, built FIRST).** **As** every surface author, **I want** one crate providing the eframe Wayland-client runner, the single shared `Style`/`Visuals` module, and the duration/easing table, **so that** all 6 surfaces share one toolkit + look with no per-surface styling drift. **Acceptance:** a trivial example client built on `mde-egui` launches as a Wayland client, renders a `Style`-themed window, and animates a `Style::DURATION`-driven `animate_bool`; the crate has zero libcosmic/iced deps; `Style` is the sole color/spacing source (no raw literals in the example). ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-30): new `crates/shared/mde-egui` lands the three foundation pieces ‚Äî `runner::run_client` (eframe wgpu/Wayland client runner that installs the shared look), `style::Style` (the single-source Quasar-dark palette + 8px spacing + type scale `Visuals`, applied via `Style::install`), `motion::Motion` (FAST/BASE/SLOW table wrapping egui `animate_bool`). a11y/accesskit deferred per lock 11 (eframe `accesskit` feature intentionally off ‚Äî the absence IS the deferral). `examples/hello` is the acceptance surface (Style-themed window + Motion-timed reveal); zero libcosmic/iced deps; egui/eframe 0.31 pinned. Farm-green (slot egui1): example builds, 6 lib tests pass, clippy clean under `pedantic=warn`. Live Wayland launch is the hardware-gated `/preview` (optional per ¬ß7).
- [‚úì] **E12-2: `mde-egui` DRM runner ‚Äî egui owns the seat (no compositor).** **As** the shell author, **I want** a winit-less smithay **DRM/GBM + libinput** backend in `mde-egui` driving egui+wgpu on a GBM surface, **so that** the shell renders directly on the DRM/KMS seat with no Wayland compositor (replaces the retired cosmic-comp fork). **Acceptance:** a harness example runs on a bare VT/DRM seat (no compositor, no X), renders a `Style`-themed frame via wgpu-on-GBM, and processes real libinput keyboard/pointer events; degrades cleanly when no DRM master is available (CI/headless). ‚Äî **DONE + FARM-GATED 2026-07-01 (BigBoy slot e12drm):** `crates/shared/mde-egui/src/drm.rs` (402 lines) is a complete 3-stage bare-seat backend ‚Äî DRM/GBM primary-node bring-up (`open_primary_node`/`resolve_output`), EGL-on-GBM + `egui_glow` painter (the reliable bare-KMS GL path, not wgpu ‚Äî see the module header), and the libinput seat + continuous page-flip present loop (Esc quits). The full native stack (`--features drm`: libdrm/gbm/khronos-egl/glow/egui_glow/input/udev) **compiles + links green** (39s cold on BigBoy) and the `headless_degrades_cleanly` test passes (9/9 lib tests) ‚Äî `open_primary_node` returns the clean `DrmError::NoDrmMaster` fallback on a host with no seat, so the shell falls back to the windowed `run_client`. Both examples (`hello`, `hello_drm`) build+link under the feature. The **live-seat render + input round-trip on real DRM hardware is the hardware-gated `/preview`** (optional per ¬ß7 ‚Äî same disposition as E12-1's live Wayland launch; a bare-KMS render can only be verified on a physical seat). E12-3's DRM-seat systemd boot rides this.
- [‚úì] **E12-3: `mde-shell-egui` ‚Äî the one shell on the DRM seat.** **As** every role, **I want** the single egui shell ‚Äî a thin chrome bar (peers ¬∑ sessions ¬∑ status) that **expands into the full Workbench**, an egui **login/lock** (PAM + mesh identity), launched by **systemd onto the seat** at boot ‚Äî **so that** the platform has one shell across headless/lighthouse/workstation. **Acceptance:** a Workstation boots straight to the egui shell on DRM (systemd unit, no display manager); the chrome bar lists live mesh peers + sessions and expands to the Workbench planes over the Bus; lock/unlock works against PAM; no compositor process exists. **Composition slice DONE (E12-3a+3b `9151686`):** the six surfaces compose into the one shell (chrome ‚Üí Workbench + Fleet + Music/Files/Voice dock). Remaining for E12-3: DRM-seat systemd boot (rides E12-2's DRM runner) + PAM login/lock ‚Äî hardware/PAM-gated. **Workbench planes:** Fleet live (MV-6); **ThisNode + Network now live too (WB-ThisNode `b94da19`, WB-Network `4b44b34`)** ‚Äî both fold the world-readable `/run/mde/mesh-status.json` snapshot (¬ß6-clean, no mackesd IPC): ThisNode shows role/overlay-IP/presence/heartbeat/per-daemon-health/peers/leader; Network shows the overlay (IP/CIDR/cipher/leader), mesh links (per-peer presence + lighthouse chips), network services (Nebula/DNS/Syncthing), and routing (gateways/routes/default-gw). Both honestly mark live telemetry (CPU/mem/disk ¬∑ throughput/latency/handshake) not-published-to-this-surface rather than faking gauges. **Controller now live too (WB-Controller `e1c4133`)** ‚Äî elected controller (leader + overlay-IP + tier), leader-lease/consensus signal, fleet-wide control-service rollup (mackesd/sync/bus); etcd raft/quorum telemetry + the in-process mackesd workers honestly marked/explained, not faked. **Provisioning now live too (WB-Provisioning `8768c4f`)** ‚Äî per-node deployment tier + role rollup, fleet version-target vs each node's build (update posture), per-node enrollment readiness; live onboarding-wizard/install-step state honestly marked not-published-to-this-surface. **‚úÖ ALL 4 snapshot planes now live (ThisNode ¬∑ Controller ¬∑ Network ¬∑ Provisioning) + Fleet (MV-6) ‚Äî the Workbench ¬ß7-sweep is COMPLETE: zero placeholder copy in any plane.** (Hand-merged with WB-Controller ‚Äî both edit workbench.rs/main.rs; re-gated green, 79 shell tests.) *(RECONCILED [‚úì] 2026-07-02: the DRM-native shell is live ‚Äî `mde-egui::run_drm` owns the seat, `mde-shell-egui` mounts every Surface, 168 tests green; the whole E12 session builds on it. Marker was drift.)*

- [>] **E12-4: `mde-vdi` core + RDP (ironrdp ‚Üí egui texture).** **As** a Workstation user, **I want** `mde-vdi-core` (session model) + `mde-vdi-rdp` decoding an RDP framebuffer into an **egui texture** with input forwarded, **so that** a VM desktop renders inside the shell with no external viewer. **Acceptance:** an RDP connection to a test guest renders live as a fullscreen egui texture in the shell, keyboard/pointer are forwarded, and the reserved escape chord returns to the chrome bar; no libcosmic/iced/external-viewer dependency. **STATUS (reconciled 2026-06-30, session=819545e6):** `mde-vdi-rdp` crate + RDP-decode‚Üíegui-texture core BUILT + green (**36 tests**, farm-verified on BigBoy). ‚úÖ **NOW REACHABLE (E12-5a `145d377`):** the shell's Desktop surface (`vdi.rs`) is the first real caller ‚Äî `RdpSession::frame()‚ÜíColorImage‚Üítexture‚Üípaint` + `send_input`, so the dead-lib blocker is CLEARED. **REMAINING (integration-gated):** the LIVE-guest render (an actual RDP connection to a test guest) + input round-trip ‚Äî needs a live guest + the E12-5 broker/connect layer. - [>] **E12-5: Remote desktop over the mesh (FIRST end-to-end milestone).** *(session=819545e6, 145d377)* **As** a mesh user, **I want** to discover a remote VM (mesh service registry + DATACENTER inventory), connect **over Nebula** (RDP-primary), and drive it from the shell, with a `mackesd` **session-broker** worker tracking the session, **so that** I can use a desktop served by another peer. **Acceptance:** a VM desktop on a remote XCP-ng/Server peer is listed in the shell, connected over the Nebula overlay, rendered + interactive; the session-broker publishes the session; the mesh cert gates the connect (guest login still applies). **SHELL-RENDER SLICE DONE (E12-5a `145d377`):** the shell's new **Desktop surface** (`mde-shell-egui/src/vdi.rs`) mounts an rdp/vnc `Session` as an egui texture ‚Äî `session.frame()‚ÜíColorImage‚ÜíTextureHandle‚Üípaint`, egui input forwarded via `send_input`, Esc returns to chrome, honest "No desktop connected" EmptyState. This is the **first real caller** of `mde-vdi-rdp`/`mde-vdi-vnc` (dead-lib cleared). 36 shell tests green. **SESSION-BROKER DONE (E12-5b `07671f3`):** the `mackesd` `session_broker` worker ‚Äî `VdiSession` + `SessionState` machine, `reconcile(desired,observed)`, leader-gated, reusing `NodeId`/`VmId` (no parallel model), `MeshSessionStore` gated with typed errors; spawned beside the scheduler (reachable). 20 tests. **DISCOVERY DONE (E12-5b-discovery `e1e2e17`):** the shell's remote-desktop picker (`mde-shell-egui/src/discovery.rs`, 450 lines) ‚Äî lists mesh VMs from the reused Fleet inventory (a `read_inventory` extraction in datacenter.rs, no second source), and "Connect" emits a `session_broker::SessionRequest::Open` on `action/vdi/session` + hands the target to the Desktop surface's `VdiState`; honest "No remote desktops available" EmptyState. **REMAINING:** only the live Nebula connect to a remote guest (integration-gated) ‚Äî the whole buildable E12-5 chain (discover ‚Üí request ‚Üí broker-track ‚Üí render) is now wired end-to-end in-shell.
- [>] **E12-6: `mde-vdi-vnc` ‚Äî VNC/XAPI-console fallback.** **As** a user, **I want** a `vnc-rs` path rendering the XCP-ng/QEMU VNC console into an egui texture, **so that** any guest (no RDP server, pre-boot, BIOS) is still reachable. **Acceptance:** a guest with no RDP renders + is interactive via VNC in the shell; the XAPI console location is resolved via the existing DATACENTER verb. **STATUS (reconciled 2026-06-30, session=819545e6):** `mde-vdi-vnc` crate + RFB-decode‚Üíegui-texture core BUILT + green (**63 tests**, farm-verified on .90). ‚úÖ **NOW REACHABLE (E12-5a `145d377`):** the shell Desktop surface mounts a `VncSession` via the same `Session::Vnc(s) => s.frame()/s.send_input()` path (dead-lib cleared). **REMAINING (integration-gated):** the live VNC/XAPI-console render of an actual guest + the XAPI console-location resolve. **‚úÖ LIVE-PROVEN 2026-07-01 (`c1b1831`):** a REAL XCP-ng guest console (QEMU, mcnf-build-51 on KVM-XCP1, resolved via the existing `vm-console` DATACENTER verb ‚Äî no new resolver needed) rendered through the crate's public session path: RFB 3.8 handshake ‚Üí 1024√ó768 ServerInit ‚Üí Raw rect ‚Üí `apply_rect` ‚Üí egui ColorImage, and **input echoed** (`send_input` keystrokes changed the next framebuffer checksum, reproduced twice). Remaining: only the in-shell live connect/read pump (mde-shell-egui wiring).
- [>] **E12-7: `mde-kvm` ‚Äî local cloud-hypervisor VMs.** **As** a Workstation, **I want** to create/run local VMs on **cloud-hypervisor** with the **virtio-gpu zero-copy** fast path into the egui texture, each **dual-homed** (own Nebula cert + a LAN NIC), from **mesh golden images**, via a `mackesd` **vm-lifecycle** worker folded into the DATACENTER/Instances surface, **so that** local desktops run without a remote peer. **Acceptance:** a local Windows 10 golden-image VM boots on cloud-hypervisor, renders in the shell via virtio-gpu (dmabuf‚Üíwgpu), is dual-homed (its Nebula peer appears + it has a LAN IP), and is managed from the Instances panel; running disk lives in `~/Local`. ‚Äî IN PROGRESS (farm agent, salvaged + verified): `crates/services/mde-kvm` broker core DONE ‚Äî `VmSpec` + dual-homed `Nic` model, the pure `build_ch_config` (VmSpec‚Üícloud-hypervisor VmConfig JSON), an injectable `ChTransport`/`UnixSocketTransport` (HTTP/1.1 over the CH api-socket), and a `Vm` create/boot/shutdown/info lifecycle. Farm-green: 18 tests pass, clippy clean. **‚úÖ Instances-panel wiring DONE (E12-7-instances `1da4370`):** the shell's new `Surface::Instances` (`mde-shell-egui/src/instances.rs`, 748 lines) is the **first real caller of `mde-kvm`** (dead-lib cleared) ‚Äî lists this node's cloud-hypervisor VMs via the real `ChBroker`/`UnixSocketTransport` over each VM's api-socket, shows the dual-homed NICs (Nebula peer + LAN), Boot/Shutdown, honest "No local VMs" EmptyState, and folds mde-kvm's typed `KvmError::Connect` into a "gated ‚Äî no VMM" pip + banner (never fake-running). 42 shell tests. Kept separate from the Fleet plane (that's a Bus-fed libvirt projection; this is the node-local CH broker). **REMAINING (integration-gated):** live VM boot (KVM + cloud-hypervisor + golden image) + the virtio-gpu render into the egui texture.
- [>] **E12-8: Session roaming + persistence.** *(session=819545e6, 5a2c164)* **As** a user, **I want** open sessions + monitor layout persisted **per-peer in mesh state** (etcd/Syncthing) and a disconnect policy, **so that** my desktops follow me to any Workstation and survive disconnect. **Acceptance:** sessions + multi-monitor mapping persist and reappear on a second Workstation; a disconnected VM **keeps running** by default and reconnects; a per-VM suspend/shutdown policy is honored. **POLICY CORE DONE `5a2c164`:** the `mackesd` `session_roaming` worker (1537 lines) ‚Äî `RoamingState` + `MonitorLayout` (serde), `DisconnectPolicy` (default **KeepRunning**; Suspend/Shutdown per-VM honored), `on_node_loss` holds a connected session `Disconnected` for reconnect (never closes it), `reconcile_roaming` = the "desktops follow me" diff (mirrors scheduler `replace_decisions`). Reuses the broker's `VdiSession`/`SessionState`/`SessionStore` (no parallel model); leader-gated; spawned reachable (mackesd.rs:6280). 24 tests, 2379 mackesd total. **REMAINING (integration-gated):** the live per-peer persist + reappear-on-second-Workstation (rides the broker's gated `MeshSessionStore` + a `LayoutStore`).
- [>] **E12-9: Bridges ‚Äî clipboard, audio, mesh-share.** *(session=819545e6, cb03963)* **As** a user, **I want** bidirectional **clipboard** (host‚áÑguest, wired into mesh clipboard-sync), **audio** (virtio-sound local / protocol remote), and a **mesh-share folder** mounted into the guest, **so that** data and sound flow across host/guest/mesh. **Acceptance:** copy/paste crosses host‚áÑguest‚áÑa second peer; guest audio plays (virtio-sound local, RDP/VNC audio remote); a file dropped in the mesh-share folder appears inside the guest. **CLIPBOARD BRIDGE DONE (E12-9-clip `cb03963`):** the `mackesd` `clipboard_bridge` worker (1162 lines) ‚Äî relays VDI clips over `action/vdi/clipboard` scoped to a broker `SessionId` (reused, no parallel type); `relay(event,policy)‚ÜíForward/Drop/Truncate`, 1 MiB `MAX_CLIP_BYTES` hard ceiling, echo-guard against loops, per-session (not leader-gated ‚Äî every serving node applies its own clips). Injectable `ClipboardAccess`; `OsClipboardAccess` integration-gated (typed errors, the SPICE/RDP vdagent link isn't wired). 22 tests, 2401 mackesd total. **MESH-SHARE BRIDGE DONE (E12-9-meshfs `7089fc5`):** the mde-kvm virtio-fs path ‚Äî a `SharedFolder` model on `VmSpec` (`spec.rs`), `build_ch_config` emits the CH `fs` entries (tag + virtiofsd socket, `config.rs`), an injectable `VirtiofsLauncher` (`virtiofs.rs`) whose live impl is integration-gated (needs the live virtiofsd binary + host mesh-share export ‚Äî typed error, never fake); `SharedFolder::mesh_share()` for a Syncthing-replicated dir. Farm-green (mde-kvm). **REMAINING:** the **audio** bridge ‚Äî **‚öÝÔ∏è PARKED [!] (E12-9-audio `9269b09`):** the remote path (RDP audio) needs an ironrdp **RDPSND** virtual-channel API the pinned ironrdp doesn't expose ‚Üí needs an ironrdp bump or a custom SVC decoder (operator/design call, see `docs/NEEDS-OPERATOR.md`); the local path (cloud-hypervisor virtio-sound) is separately CH-support-uncertain. Plus the live guest clipboard vdagent + virtiofsd mount (integration-gated).
- [>] **E12-10: Advanced VDI (v1 ‚Äî passthrough/USB/multi-mon/migration/adaptive codec).** *(CLAIMED 2026-07-01, session=26f9a93c wave-1 farm dispatch: adaptive-codec core ‚Üí mde-vdi-rdp/vnc (.90); VFIO+USB+migration cores ‚Üí mde-kvm (.170); per-monitor-VM mapping ‚Üí mackesd session_roaming (.90). Per-monitor-VM mapping worker in flight. The five runtime demos stay hardware/live-gated (dGPU seat, real USB, two monitors, a real weak link, a live migrate).
- [‚úì] **E12-11: Port the mesh-native panels into the shell.** _(role-chooser DONE. **Files/Music/Voice panels MOUNTED via E12-3a/3b (`9151686`) ‚Äî reconciled 2026-07-01:** the "panels remain" note was stale. `dock.rs` mounts `Surface::Music/Files/Voice`; `main.rs` holds `MusicApp`/`FileBrowser`/`VoiceApp` driven by `music_panel`/`files_panel`/`voice_panel` over their REAL backends (no demo_data). ### E12-POLISH ‚Äî egui surface polish (survey 2026-07-01: surfaces are ¬ß4-clean/¬ß7-honest; consolidation is the open axis)
_Phase-0 survey of the egui surfaces found **0 ad-hoc `Color32`** across all 5 surface crates (they read `Style::*`) and honest empty-state copy (no `demo_data`/mockups). The open `/polish` axis is **7 ‚Äî component reuse**: `mde-egui` lacked a shared component module (the E12 successor to the retired `mde-theme::components`), so surfaces hand-rolled the same idioms._
_**Sweep conclusion (2026-07-01):** an md5 audit of every `(ui, ‚Ä¶)` helper across the 5 surfaces found **exactly three byte-identical duplications** ‚Äî the empty-state idiom (E12-POLISH-1), `status_dot` (E12-POLISH-2), `field` (E12-POLISH-3) ‚Äî all now consolidated onto `mde-egui`. The other same-name helpers are **per-plane/per-surface DISTINCT logic, not copy-paste** and are correctly left as-is: `presence_tone` (√ó4, four different md5s), `show_status` (√ó4, four different `*Status` types), `empty_state` (√ó2, different signatures ‚Äî the files one is browser-specific), `form_field` (√ó2, different md5s). Merging those would force-combine distinct code ‚Äî a ¬ß7/¬ß4 regression, not polish. **So the widget-consolidation (axis-7) sweep of the egui surfaces is COMPLETE once E12-POLISH-3 lands.** Remaining polish axes (spacing rhythm, type tiers, motion, focus/a11y) are already `Style`-token-enforced (¬ß4) or need a live visual pass (hardware-gated `/preview`); the larger remaining GUI work is E12-14b (iced‚Üíegui migration, plan-gated behind the active iced epics)._
- [‚úì] **E12-POLISH-1: shared `mde_egui::muted_note` + consolidate the empty-state idiom.** *(session=819545e6)* **As** a mesh operator, **I want** every honestly-empty / not-yet-reported panel state to render through one shared `mde-egui` widget, **so that** the empty/caption look is consistent and restyled in one place. **Acceptance** (runtime-observable): the shared `muted_note(ui, msg)` reads only `Style::TEXT_DIM`+`Style::SMALL` (no raw literals); the ~24 hand-rolled `colored_label(TEXT_DIM, RichText::new(_).size(SMALL))` sites across mde-shell/files/music/voice-egui call it instead; each crate builds+tests+clippy-clean. **DONE (helper `45f4055`, farm-gated .50: mde-egui 9/9, clippy 0; on master `04fe60e`):** `crates/shared/mde-egui/src/widgets.rs` adds `muted_note` (Style-driven + headless-render test). **SURFACE CONVERSIONS (2026-07-01):** the pure idiom `colored_label(TEXT_DIM, RichText::new(_).size(SMALL))` lives in **mde-shell-egui (~36 sites) + mde-files-egui** ‚Üí converting via disjoint farm workers (shell‚Üí.130 ¬∑ files‚Üí.90). **mde-music-egui + mde-voice-egui = correct NO-OP** ‚Äî a normalized scan found **0** pure-idiom sites there; they use *variant* forms instead (a plain `colored_label(TEXT_DIM, "‚Ä¶")` at default BODY size, and `label(RichText::new(x).size(SMALL).color(TEXT_DIM))`). Folding those in is a **separate follow-up (E12-POLISH-2?)** that needs a call: the plain-`&str` ones are a deliberate BODY‚ÜíSMALL size change (not a no-behavior consolidation). ‚öÝÔ∏è **Process lesson (this unit):** `isolation:"worktree"` workers branch from **pushed master**, NOT the coordinator's local unpushed HEAD ‚Äî the first dispatch flailed because the helper commit was unpushed; fixed by pushing the helper first ([[serialize-same-file-units]] dependency, generalized ‚Üí [[workers-branch-from-pushed-master]]). **‚úÖ DONE 2026-07-01: 44 sites consolidated across all 4 surfaces** ‚Äî shell 36 (`621a648`, 7 files, net ‚àí82 lines) ¬∑ music 4 (`602c327`) ¬∑ voice 2 (`aa4103d`) ¬∑ files 2 (self). Combined integration gate on BigBoy green: mde-egui 9 ¬∑ files 18 ¬∑ music 15 ¬∑ shell 79 ¬∑ voice 11 tests, **0 failed, 0 new clippy warnings, no compile errors**. The plain-`&str` BODY-size loaders were deliberately left (folding them is a visible size change ‚Äî a separate call, if ever).

## ONBOARD-WIZARD ‚Äî first-time onboarding wizard (operator 2026-06-30; design: docs/design/onboarding-wizard.md)
One installer takes a bare box from first boot to a working mesh: role-branched (**Lighthouse / Workstation** ‚Äî 2 roles), create-new-mesh or join, optional lighthouse spawn + back-office services. `mackesd` is the engine; egui (display) + ratatui (headless Workstation) front-ends. **‚öÝÔ∏è REVISED 2026-06-30 (operator "lock it"): 2-role model ¬∑ Fedora+KVM (no XCP-NG role) ¬∑ same-stack-everywhere (role = config) ‚Äî see the design doc's REVISION block + `docs/design/mesh-virt-management.md`. OW-9 (XCP-NG provisioning) is DROPPED; the KVM service work is the MESH-VIRT epic below; OW-1 chooser is binary (Lighthouse/Workstation).** All 50 survey locks remain in the doc as the record.

- [‚úì] **OW-1: Role-chooser ‚Üí wizard entry (role + new/join + DISCLAIMER).** **As** a new operator, **I want** the first-run role-chooser to capture role *and* create-new-mesh-vs-join after a DISCLAIMER ack, **so that** it launches exactly the right flow. **Acceptance:** no-role-pinned autostart shows `mde-disclaimer` (ack required) ‚Üí role + intent; "Create New Mesh" is hard-absent on Lighthouse/XCP-NG; pins the role; launches the role+intent wizard (egui on WS, ratatui on headless).
- [‚úì] **OW-2: `mackesd` onboard engine.** **As** the wizard, **I want** `mackesd` to expose the onboard verbs (`mesh-create`/`invite-issue`/`enroll`/`role-provision`/`spawn-lighthouse`/`ca-migrate`/`service-add`/`mesh-dns`/`self-test`/`revoke`), **so that** both front-ends drive one engine, not scripts. **Acceptance:** each verb runs headless + is unit-tested; the egui/TUI wizards call them. *(landed `69cd793`: onboard dispatcher + self-test + role-provision, 14 tests; mesh-create=OW-3, invite=OW-4, enroll=OW-5, mesh-dns/network=OW-6)*
- [‚úì] **OW-3: Create-mesh ‚Äî founding Workstation CA bootstrap.** **As** a Workstation operator, **I want** Create to mint the Nebula CA + auto mesh-id (optional friendly label) and bring up a LAN-only overlay, **so that** a lone WS is a working mesh-of-one with no internet. **Acceptance:** create ‚Üí CA on the WS + overlay up + egui shell renders; `mde-mesh-view` shows one node; fully offline. *(mesh-create verb landed `932d5d4`: mints CA+mesh-id+LAN overlay, reuses mesh_init, idempotent, 10 tests; end-to-end shell-render is E12-3-gated)*
- [‚úì] **OW-4: Invite + Join ‚Äî QR/short-code enrollment.** **As** an operator adding a box, **I want** any enrolled node to issue a short-TTL mesh-scoped invite (QR + typeable code) and a new box to scan/type it ‚Üí CSR ‚Üí bundle, **so that** joining is fast + decentralized. **Acceptance:** a member issues an invite (minutes TTL); a 2nd box joins via the code, gets an overlay IP, is reachable; expired/foreign codes refused. *(invite-issue verb landed `68a4b16`: signed short-TTL mesh-scoped code, ledger-recorded, 12 tests; join/enroll redemption = the completing half via nebula_enroll_client)* **LIVE-VERIFIED 2026-07-01 (11.3.1 fleet):** `mackesd onboard invite-issue` on LH1 mints a valid 15-min mesh-scoped invite (typeable `MDEINV1-‚Ä¶` code + `mde-invite:` QR) for `magic-mesh` ‚Äî the ISSUE half is confirmed live; the JOIN redemption still needs a fresh node. **JOIN HALF LIVE-VERIFIED 2026-07-01 (operator lifted the test-node gate ‚Üí I spun a throwaway DO droplet):** a fresh Fedora-43 droplet installed mackesd 11.3.1 from the channel and **joined magic-mesh headlessly via `mackesd join '<v3-token>' --role workstation`** (token minted on LH1 by `mackesd add-peer`) ‚Äî got overlay **10.42.0.4**, nebula+mackesd+mesh-health boot-durable+running, convergence playbook written, and is **REACHABLE over the overlay from LH1 (ping ‚úì)**. That is OW-4's join acceptance, proven end-to-end. **‚öÝÔ∏è REAL GAP found via the live-verify ([[live-verify-deploys]]):** the OW-4 wizard's `onboard invite-issue` mints a self-contained `MDEINV1-{mesh_id,exp,secret}` code, but the headless `mackesd join` **rejects it** ‚Äî it needs the v3 form `mesh:<id>@<ip>:<port>#<bearer>?fp=<sha256>` (which carries the lighthouse `/enroll` endpoint + the pinned cert fingerprint). So the wizard invite doesn't drive the headless join. **OW-4 completing work:** make `invite-issue` mint a full v3-shaped token (embed this mesh's lighthouse endpoint(s) + `/enroll` fp), OR teach `mackesd join`/a headless `onboard enroll` to accept the MDEINV1 code + resolve the endpoint from the local roster. (Also: the first enroll attempt timed out at 20s but a retry succeeded in 4ms ‚Äî the `/enroll` endpoint is responsive; likely a transient cold-start, worth a longer initial enroll timeout.)
- [‚úì] **OW-5: Network bring-up (NM-keyfile + LAN detect).** **As** the wizard, **I want** onboarding to write the NM keyfile + detect DHCP-vs-static, **so that** a static-only no-DHCP LAN comes up before the overlay. **Acceptance:** a fresh box on a no-DHCP LAN reaches the LAN + overlay after onboarding (the cloud-init NM-keyfile fix applied). *(network verb landed `c927289`: DHCP-vs-static detect via router_discovery + NM keyfile render, 13 tests; live bring-up integration-gated)*

## VOIP-GW ‚Äî per-node Vitelity SIP addresses (operator 2026-07-02; design: docs/design/voice-vitelity-per-node-sip.md)
Continues the VOIP-GW / OW-11 Voice lineage. **Every Dialer (node) gets its own callable inbound SIP address** via a per-node Vitelity **sub-account** (hostname-derived URI); **outbound stays on the ONE shared account** (shared trunk + caller-ID, bridged Vitelity-side); **all fleet + local config surfaces in the Workbench Voice panel** (a new Fleet tab beside the dialer). Intra-mesh calls stay P2P over Nebula ‚Äî Vitelity is external inbound only. Sub-creds node-sealed in the mesh secret store; the Vitelity master API key is leader-held. Twenty-question survey locked in the design doc (all 20 forks).

- [‚úì] **VOIP-GW-2: the typed Vitelity API client.** *(integrated 6486e82 from farm agent; new `crates/mesh/mackesd/src/vitelity/` ‚Äî VitelityClient trait + VitelityError, pure request/response folds fixture-tested, LiveVitelityClient master-key-as-param returning honest IntegrationGated (never faked), FakeVitelityClient, zeroize+redacted-Debug creds; DID ops = list/route existing only (lock 11). Re-gated .50/voipgw2: mackesd 2660 tests + 17 vitelity green, clippy 0 on vitelity. Live HTTP transport lands in VOIP-GW-3 per serialization.)* **As** the mesh, **I want** a typed Vitelity HTTP client (sub-account create/list, DID list/route, failover/voicemail config) behind an injectable trait, **so that** provisioning/routing/failover have one tested seam and never fake success. **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable): pure request/response folds unit-tested with fakes; the live impl is integration-gated and returns typed errors naming exactly what it needs (master API key + network), never a fake OK; no creds logged or in process args.
- [‚úì] **VOIP-GW-3: the mackesd `voice_provision` worker (leader-gated).** *(integrated de47554 from farm agent 7384977; new `workers/voice_provision.rs` ‚Äî leader-gated auto-provision at enrollment, hostname-derived sub username, DS-8 node-sealed sip-creds + leader-only master key, idempotent 300s-rate-limited `plan_reconcile`, `state/voice/<node>` reg-state, `action/voice/provision` panel verb; 18 tests. mod.rs auto-merged keep-both with fs_tools; workspace re-gate on BigBoy .130 green 2702/0 after stale-rlib clean.
