Gesture-recognition + density unit-tested.

## FILEMGR ‚Äî fully-functional file manager + automatic sshfs mesh access (operator 2026-07-02; design: docs/design/file-manager-full.md)
Make `Surface::Files` fully functional (full POSIX op set + archives) and give it **automatic sshfs access to every mesh node**. Today it does navigation + Send-To with a demo_data mockup + one real op; this builds the real thing. Backend ops in `mde-files` behind an injectable `FileOps` seam (demo_data deleted); a `mackesd` mesh_mount worker owns the sshfs lifecycle over the overlay (shared node-sealed key, roster-driven, on-demand mount home-default + escalate-to-root); direct A‚ÜíB transfers; permanent-delete + no-undo (confirm dialogs + typed-arming for remote/escalated destructive ops are the guards). 25-lock survey in the design doc.

- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-1: the `FileOps` backend core.** **As** a user, **I want** the real POSIX operation set in the `mde-files` backend behind an injectable trait, **so that** the manager actually manages files (not a mockup). **Acceptance:** copy/move/rename/delete/mkdir/new-file/symlink/duplicate/hardlink/chmod/chown/timestamps run against the real FS via `FileOps` (real=std::fs+nix, fake for tests); `demo_data.rs` is deleted; ¬ß9 typed, no raw shell; unit-tested with the fake FS.
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-2: async op queue + conflict engine.** **As** a user, **I want** long ops to run on a worker with live progress + pause/cancel and a background queue, and name-collisions resolved per-item, **so that** big/bulk operations are visible, controllable, and safe. **Acceptance:** an op reports files/bytes/ETA + is pausable/cancellable; cancel reports true completion (no half-files); per-item Overwrite/Skip/Keep-both + apply-to-all; directories merge recursively; the UI never blocks. Unit-tested.
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-3: archives.** **As** a user, **I want** to create + extract + browse zip/tar(.gz/.xz/.zst), **so that** packaging + unpacking are first-class. **Acceptance:** compress a selection to a chosen format; double-click browses an archive in-place (extract-here/extract-to); via Rust crates (no shell-out, ¬ß9); queued progress.
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-4: recursive search.** **As** a user, **I want** async recursive name + full-text content search with filters, **so that** I can find files anywhere in a tree. **Acceptance:** streaming cancellable results (name-glob + content grep) with type/size/mtime filters; results are a normal file view (ops apply); runs on local + mounted mesh paths (honest remote-slower note).
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-5: the mackesd `mesh_mount` worker.** **As** the platform, **I want** a mesh-side worker owning the sshfs lifecycle over the overlay, **so that** peers mount on demand safely. **Acceptance:** mounts on `action/mesh-mount/<host>` (home default; an escalate verb re-mounts `/`); tuned mount opts; publishes `state/mesh-mount/*` (mounted/mounting/unreachable/path); idle-unmount; reconnect+backoff; frozen/stale-mount detection + recovery; in-flight ops on a drop fail typed. ¬ß6 mesh-side.
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-6: shared mesh SSH key + sshd overlay bind.** **As** the platform, **I want** a shared mesh SSH keypair sealed to each node and its sshd accepting it over the overlay only, **so that** sshfs authenticates without per-pair key sprawl. **Acceptance:** the keypair is node-sealed in the secret store + installed for the mesh user; sshd accepts it bound to the overlay; a documented re-key path revokes; never a plaintext key on disk/logs.
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-7: direct peer-to-peer transfer.** **As** a user, **I want** an A‚ÜíB copy to transfer directly (not double-hopped through my node), **so that** cross-node file moves are fast. **Acceptance:** a node‚Üínode copy routes directly (reuse Send-To / peer-side helper), sshfs-relay fallback when no direct path; one queued transfer with real progress; wired into copy/move + drag-onto-node.
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-8: the Files surface shell.** **As** a user, **I want** real views + navigation + selection + drag-and-drop, **so that** the manager is a proper desktop file manager. **Acceptance:** List/Grid/Details views (sortable, per-folder memory, show-hidden); breadcrumbs + editable path + history + **tabs** + **dual-pane** + sidebar; click/Ctrl/Shift/Ctrl-A/rubber-band selection; full DnD (move default, Ctrl=copy) within/between panes; ¬ß4 tokens; headless mount test.
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-9: the Mesh sidebar tree.** **As** a user, **I want** every mesh node in the sidebar with live presence, mounting on navigate, **so that** I have automatic access to all nodes. **Acceptance:** roster-driven peer list + presence/reachability pips; navigating a peer requests the mount (FILEMGR-5) + browses it; the **home‚Üîfull-filesystem escalation** GUI action; offline peers honestly greyed (no hang).
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-10: preview + thumbnails + built-in viewers.** **As** a user, **I want** thumbnails + a preview pane + built-in viewers, **so that** I can inspect files without leaving the shell. **Acceptance:** lazy cached capped thumbnails (images/video); preview pane (image/text-highlight/media-meta) + spacebar quick-look; built-in viewers only (no external spawn); remote previews lazy/on-demand.
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-11: the operation dialogs.** **As** a user, **I want** the confirm/conflict/properties/arming dialogs, **so that** operations are clear + safe. **Acceptance:** confirm-delete; the conflict dialog; a Properties dialog (rwx grid + octal + owner/group, chown offered only when permitted); and **typed-arming** (name the node+path) for destructive ops on a remote/escalated mount. ¬ß4 tokens.
- [‚úì] **FILEMGR-12: mesh integration.** **As** a user, **I want** Send-To + Send-in-Chat + shared clipboard, **so that** files flow across the mesh + surfaces. **Acceptance:** right-click Send-To a peer (reuse); Send in Chat hands a file to a NOTIFY-CHAT conversation (reuse the file message-kind); cut/copy/paste share the shell clipboard (cross-surface paths).

## BOOKMARKS ‚Äî mesh browser: synced bookmarks + sandboxed Servo + ad-blocker (operator 2026-07-02; design: docs/design/mesh-bookmarks.md)
A new `Surface::Bookmarks` browser: import bookmarks from all major browsers, manage them as a mesh-synced CRDT collection, browse the web in an out-of-process sandboxed Servo engine, filtered by a mesh-wide ad-blocker service. **NO credential/password handling at all** (the Vault brief's Firefox/NSS half dropped). Carbon ¬ß4 GUI; build all-at-once; fleet-wide default-on; Servo always in the workspace build. 100-lock survey in the design doc.

- [‚úì] **BOOKMARKS-1: model + CRDT.** **As** the platform, **I want** the bookmark tree + CRDT op set, **so that** edits converge mesh-wide with no center. **Acceptance:** `mde-bookmarks` lib ‚Äî UUID ids, strict one-parent tree, HLC clock, fractional-index order, LWW-delete, ops carrying author user+node, content-addressed favicon store; convergence property-tests (random concurrent op-sets converge identically); no Servo/credentials.
- [‚úì] **BOOKMARKS-2: bookmarks worker + mesh sync.** **As** the platform, **I want** a mackesd worker syncing the collection over Syncthing, **so that** every node shares one tree. **Acceptance:** per-node append-only op segments in the encrypted mesh Syncthing share; replay-merge + snapshot/prune; in-memory index + periodic-flush durability; offline-first (edits continue when sync down, auto-resume); `action/bookmarks/*` + `state/bookmarks/*`; two-node convergence proven.
- [‚úì] **BOOKMARKS-3: browser importers.** **As** a user, **I want** to import bookmarks from any browser, **so that** my links come with me. **Acceptance:** file/dir picker + format auto-detect for Firefox `places.sqlite` (bookmarks only, RO+immutable), Chromium `Bookmarks` JSON, universal Netscape HTML (Safari via HTML export); FF-tags‚Üítags[], Chromium-roots‚Üínamed subfolders; normalized-URL dedup; idempotent re-import into `Imported/<Browser>`; **never reads logins/cookies/history**; fixture-tested per format.
- [‚úì] **BOOKMARKS-4: Surface::Bookmarks UI (Carbon ¬ß4).** **As** a user, **I want** a full bookmark manager surface, **so that** I organize + open bookmarks. **Acceptance:** three-region (folder tree + list + detail/browser pane); folder CRUD (confirm on non-empty); manual order + optional sort-by; title+url live search; Ctrl/Shift multi-select bulk (move/delete/open-all/copy-URLs); drag reorder/move; add via +/paste/shortcut/from-page; double-click‚Üínew tab; honest error/empty states matching the platform idiom; ¬ß4 Carbon tokens (no raw hex); egui snapshot + headless mount tests.
- [‚úì] **BOOKMARKS-5: the mde-web-preview Servo browser (bin).** **As** a user, **I want** to browse the web in the surface, **so that** bookmarks open in a real browser. **Acceptance:** out-of-process `mde-web-preview` bin ‚Äî interactive Servo (JS on, tabs, links, back/forward/address bar, media best-effort); OS sandbox (user namespace + seccomp-bpf + minimal caps + no-new-privs, one process per tab, cgroup memory+CPU caps, read-only rootfs + tmpfs, NO home/keys/data); zero telemetry; system-CA TLS + honest cert warnings; deny-all sensitive web perms; first-party-session/no-third-party cookies cleared on close; no persistent history; generic non-identifying UA; GPU-required; lazy first-launch + one warm helper. Headless test: about:blank ‚Üí a frame arrives on the shm channel.
- [‚úì] **BOOKMARKS-6: IPC + shm texture bridge.** **As** the shell, **I want** to drive + display the sandboxed browser, **so that** it renders in the surface. **Acceptance:** per-session Unix-domain socket (typed length-prefixed control/events) + shm/dmabuf frame transport (upload to an egui texture on paint-ready, not every frame); input forwarding scaled by pixels_per_point; crash ‚Üí honest "page crashed" state + respawn-on-reload, other tabs unaffected; navigation chrome wired.
- [‚úì] **BOOKMARKS-7: ad-filter service + engine.** **As** the platform, **I want** a mesh-wide ad-blocker, **so that** browsing is ad/tracker-free by default. **Acceptance:** mackesd `adfilter` worker ‚Äî EasyList/EasyPrivacy/uBlock-base bundled + operator-addable custom lists, a leader compiles the serialized `adblock-rust` engine + replicates the blob over Syncthing, per-site allowlist synced mesh-wide (block-on-by-default), anti-adblock best-effort, staleness fallback to last-synced/bundled with an honest indicator, `state/adfilter/*`; the `adblock-rust` engine in `mde-web-preview` blocks network requests before fetch + hides cosmetic elements (injected user-stylesheet, JS-off-safe), exempts mesh/overlay domains, and reports per-page blocked counts. Rule-match folds unit-tested (ad URL blocked, benign allowed). _(2026-07-03: **engine+service crate `mde-adblock` landed `e8882e0`** ‚Äî hand-rolled parser/matcher/store/bundled-seed + allowlist + staleness, 23t, clippy-clean, airgap-safe (no `adblock-rust` fetch). **STAYS [>] ‚Äî currently UNREACHABLE (no caller):** remaining for ¬ß7 = the mackesd `adfilter` worker (leader-compile blob + Syncthing replicate + upstream refresh + `state/adfilter/*`) + the `mde-web-preview` wiring (block-before-fetch, cosmetic hide, exempt mesh/overlay, per-page counts). DONE 090a461 ‚Äî worker + browser block-path landed, mde-adblock reachable.)_
- [‚úì] **BOOKMARKS-8: fleet policy + observability.** **As** an operator, **I want** to govern the browser/ad-blocker fleet-wide, **so that** policy holds. **Acceptance:** a mesh policy (per-role browser enable/disable, force ad-blocker on, URL allowlist, custom lists) **enforced by the local worker/launcher** (not just UI ‚Äî refuses to spawn on a disallowed role, injects the forced ad-blocker+allowlist, rejects out-of-policy actions); disable stops sync + hides the surface but retains local data; per-node service state + ad-block stats published to the Workbench fleet view.
- [‚úì] **BOOKMARKS-9: packaging + docs.** **As** a deployer, **I want** the browser packaged + documented, **so that** it ships securely. **Acceptance:** the RPM declares Servo's runtime libs (mesa/vulkan/fontconfig/freetype/‚Ä¶) as requires + bundles the seed filter lists (NO firefox/nss deps); a confined enforcing SELinux domain for the helper ships + loads; `mde-web-preview` in the base bootc image, runtime-gated by policy; a THREAT_MODEL (attack surface + sandbox + the accepted residual risks) + a CHANGELOG (Servo pin/cadence). DoD: base workspace build green; `rpm -qlp` ships mde-web-preview + the SELinux policy.
- [‚úì] **BOOKMARKS-10: mesh integration.** **As** a user, **I want** bookmarks to flow across the mesh + surfaces, **so that** they compose. **Acceptance:** right-click Send-in-Chat a bookmark (reuse the NOTIFY-CHAT message-kind); copy-URL to the shell clipboard; add-bookmark-from the current browser page.

## BRAND ‚Äî empty-desktop logo backdrop (operator 2026-07-02; design: docs/design/desktop-logo-backdrop.md)
The brand lockup (`assets/brand/logo-lockup.png`) becomes the desktop's persistent backdrop layer: centered, large, text-free, shown whenever nothing covers the screen, dimming to a watermark once content opens. 10-lock survey in the design doc.

- [‚úì] **BRAND-1: the empty-desktop logo backdrop (`mde-shell-egui`, egui/Carbon ¬ß4).** **As** a user, **I want** the Magic Mesh lockup centered on the desktop whenever it's empty with no text over it, **so that** an idle seat is branded and calm. **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable): the embedded lockup (`include_bytes!`, decoded once to a cached texture) renders as the bottom backdrop for both the `vdi.rs` no-desktop EmptyState and the empty root desktop; centered in the **optical free area** (viewport minus the real top-chrome + dock heights), sized to ~50% of the shorter side but **never upscaled past native 1270px**; full opacity on the Carbon ¬ß4 background token (**no raw hex**); **no text over the image** ‚Äî any honest status renders as a small line clearly below it; **every empty display** shows its own centered logo; a covered display **dims the logo to a low-opacity watermark** still visible in uncovered gaps; state changes **crossfade** and the idle logo **breathes slowly**; egui snapshot test of the empty backdrop; `build/test/clippy -p mde-shell-egui` green; `lint-layered-tiers.sh` clean. Replaces the current text-only EmptyState body (status moves below).

## TERM ‚Äî a Terminator-class terminal emulator for the mesh (operator 2026-07-02; design: docs/design/mesh-terminal.md)
A new egui-native terminal surface (`mde-term-egui`) matching Terminator: arbitrarily nested H/V split panes, tabs-of-splits, broadcast/grouped input, mesh-synced saved layouts, zoom + drag-rearrange ‚Äî extended so any pane can be a shell on a remote mesh node over the overlay (mackesd PTY broker + the FILEMGR-6 mesh-ssh-key). Mature VT crate (add+vendor), openpty local, Carbon chrome + Carbon-derived/classic content palettes. 16-lock survey in the design doc.

- [‚úì] **TERM-1: VT engine + terminal core.** **As** the platform, **I want** a mature VT/xterm engine wired to a screen+scrollback model, **so that** panes render real terminal output correctly. **Acceptance:** the chosen VT crate (`alacritty_terminal`/`termwiz`) is added to the workspace + vendored (airgap-buildable, `--locked` OK ‚Äî verify early; fall back to `vte`/hand-rolled with an honest note if truly unfetchable); a terminal core parses ANSI/xterm into a cell grid + unlimited(soft-capped) scrollback; unit-tested against known escape sequences (colors, cursor moves, clears, wraps). ¬ß6 glue ‚Äî no re-implemented VT parsing.
- [‚úì] **TERM-2: local PTY + shell launch.** **As** a user, **I want** a real local shell in a pane, **so that** the terminal actually runs commands. **Acceptance:** `openpty` (rustix/libc, in-lock) spawns the user's `$SHELL` as a login shell inheriting cwd+env; a reader pump feeds PTY‚Üíengine, input‚ÜíPTY; SIGWINCH on resize; clean child reap on close; runtime-smoke: a pane runs `ls`/`echo` and shows output. ¬ß9 typed, no shell-string injection.
- [‚úì] **TERM-3: the egui terminal widget.** **As** a user, **I want** the terminal painted in the surface, **so that** I can see + interact with it. **Acceptance:** renders the engine's cell grid via egui (GPU glyphs, cursor, bold/italic/underline), the content palette, mouse+keyboard selection, and a scrollback viewport; resizes map to cols/rows; ¬ß4 Carbon tokens for chrome (no raw hex); headless render test produces draw primitives.
- [‚úì] **TERM-4: nested split panes + zoom + drag-rearrange.** **As** a user, **I want** Terminator's arbitrary H/V splits, **so that** I tile terminals freely. **Acceptance:** a `Leaf|Split{dir,ratio,a,b}` tree splits to any depth with draggable dividers; zoom maximizes/restores one pane; drag reparents a leaf; close collapses; focus follows; unit-tested tree ops.
- [‚úì] **TERM-5: tabs of split trees.** **As** a user, **I want** tabs each holding their own split layout, **so that** I group workspaces. **Acceptance:** a tab bar (Carbon tokens) with new/close/reorder; each tab owns an independent split tree; switching preserves per-tab state; tested.
- [‚úì] **TERM-6: broadcast / grouped input.** **As** a user, **I want** to type into many terminals at once, **so that** I drive a fleet in parallel. **Acceptance:** input routes to the focused pane, ALL panes, or a NAMED GROUP (assign/label panes to groups); broadcasting panes show a Carbon-token indicator border; toggled by keybind + UI; tested the fan-out routing.
- [‚úì] **TERM-7: mackesd mesh PTY-broker worker.** **As** the platform, **I want** a mesh-side worker opening shells on remote peers, **so that** panes can run on any node. **Acceptance:** opens a remote shell over the overlay using `mesh-ssh-key` (FILEMGR-6); typed Bus verbs `action/pty/<peer>` (open/write/resize/close) + `state/pty/<id>` (bytes/exit); honest typed gating on unreachable/dropped peers (mirrors mesh_mount, never fakes a session); idle/dead-session cleanup; ¬ß6 mesh-side; unit-tested folds + a gated live leg.
- [‚úì] **TERM-8: remote-terminal UX (peer picker + manual).** **As** a user, **I want** to open a terminal on a mesh node, **so that** remote work is one click. **Acceptance:** a "new terminal on ‚Üí <peer>" picker driven by the mesh roster + presence pips (offline greyed, no hang) plus a manual host/overlay-address entry; both route through TERM-7; a remote pane is visually marked with its node; reconnect on transient drop.
- [‚úì] **TERM-9: scrollback search + smart clipboard.** **As** a user, **I want** search + smart selection, **so that** I find output and act on it. **Acceptance:** in-scrollback search with regex + match highlight + next/prev; copy/paste; copy-on-select + paste-on-middle-click options; detected URLs open in the BOOKMARKS mesh browser and filesystem paths open in the Files surface (reuse the surface-launch path, ¬ß6); tested detection + routing.
- [‚úì] **TERM-10: mesh-synced saved layouts.** **As** a user, **I want** to save + launch named terminal arrangements across the mesh, **so that** setups are repeatable anywhere. **Acceptance:** serialize (tab/split tree + per-pane cwd + launch cmd + target node) to a named layout; synced via Syncthing (like bookmarks/adfilter); "launch layout" rebuilds it incl. remote panes (TERM-7/8); two-node visibility proven; tested round-trip.
- [‚úì] **TERM-11: palette + look.** **As** a user, **I want** a branded default palette + classic presets, **so that** the terminal fits the platform yet feels familiar. **Acceptance:** a default 16-color palette derived from mde-theme Carbon tokens + bundled classics (Solarized/Gruvbox/Nord) via a simple picker; font-size + cursor-style knobs (no full profile system, Q13); the chrome stays pure Carbon ¬ß4 (no raw hex); `cargo test -p mde-theme` green if tokens touched.
- [‚úì] **TERM-12: keybindings + titles + activity watch + bell.** **As** a user, **I want** Terminator keybinds and per-pane awareness, **so that** it feels like Terminator. **Acceptance:** Terminator-compatible default keymap (split/nav/zoom/tab/broadcast), fully rebindable via config; per-pane editable titles (auto from running cmd, user-overridable); watch-for-activity / watch-for-silence firing a notification (the Chat/notification path); configurable bell; tested keymap dispatch + watcher triggers.
- [‚úì] **TERM-13: full mouse reporting + true-color + ligatures (Q17/Q20 folds).** **As** a user, **I want** TUI apps to get the mouse and crisp modern rendering, **so that** vim/htop/tmux and colored output work right. **Acceptance:** SGR/1006 mouse reporting forwarded to apps in mouse-mode (click/drag/scroll/hover) with **Shift-bypass** to native selection; 24-bit true-color + 256-color rendered faithfully; a bundled monospace font with programming ligatures; tested mouse-encode + a true-color render check. (Inline images sixel/kitty are OUT of scope ‚Äî a follow-up.)
- [‚úì] **TERM-14: remote session persistence + reattach (Q18).** **As** a user, **I want** a remote mesh shell to survive the surface closing, **so that** long jobs keep running and I can reattach. **Acceptance:** the mackesd PTY broker (TERM-7) keeps a remote session alive when its client disconnects (surface close/crash), buffering output within bounds; a reattach path (verb + UX in TERM-8) reconnects a pane to a still-running session listing reattachable sessions per node; idle/TTL reap of orphaned sessions; local panes stay ephemeral; two-phase test: open‚Üídisconnect‚Üíreattach sees the running shell. ¬ß6 mesh-side.
- [‚úì] **TERM-15: context-menu custom commands + built-in mesh actions (Q19).** **As** a user, **I want** right-click actions on the selection, **so that** the terminal composes with the mesh. **Acceptance:** user-defined custom commands (config: label + command template with the selection substituted) run on the selected text (Terminator parity); built-in mesh actions ‚Äî send-selection-to-Chat (NOTIFY-CHAT), open-path-in-Files, open-URL-in-mesh-browser, new-terminal-here (inherit cwd) ‚Äî reuse the existing surface-launch paths (¬ß6); tested command substitution + action dispatch.
- [‚úì] **TERM-16: mount the terminal into the shell dock (RESCUE ‚Äî reachability, 2026-07-03).** **As** a user, **I want** the Terminator-class terminal to actually open in the Quasar shell, **so that** TERM-1..15 are reachable in the shipped product (not shipped-but-dead). **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable): `mde-shell-egui` gains `Surface::Terminal` in `dock.rs` (enum + SURFACES list + label + render arm), driven by an embedded `mde_term_egui` lib panel (expose a `terminal_panel`/pump seam mirroring `files_panel`/`music_panel`, ¬ß6 ‚Äî reuse the app, don't re-derive); the terminal renders + is interactive as a dock surface; `mde-term-egui`'s bin (or the shell asset) is added to the `generate-rpm` assets so it SHIPS (DoD = it appears in `rpm -qlp` at the gated cut per [[strip-verify-replacement-ships-in-rpm]]); shell mount test green. **Found by the 2026-07-03 reconciliation:** `mde-term-egui` builds green but has 0 references in `mde-shell-egui`, 0 RPM assets, 0 launchers ‚Äî the whole TERM epic is currently unreachable. Serialize on CHOOSER-7 + MEDIA-18 (all edit `dock.rs`). **Blocks the 12.1 cut.**

## MEDIA ‚Äî a VLC-class media player + Jellyfin client, native to the mesh (operator 2026-07-02; design: docs/design/mesh-media-player.md)
A new egui-native universal player (`mde-media-egui`) on **libmpv**: any audio/video, local or streamed, Carbon ¬ß4 chrome + a translucent dark OSD, video on a dedicated DRM overlay plane, PipeWire audio, VA-API decode. Full **Jellyfin** client (multi-server, Quick Connect, browse, direct-play/transcode, progress sync, offline, Live-TV). Mesh-native: auto-discovered media sources, aggregated mesh library, **session roaming** (playback follows the operator between seats), sync-play party mode, casting, and this node as a media server too. `mde-music` stays as the music-library app. 35-lock survey in the design doc.

- [‚úì] **MEDIA-1: libmpv engine + player core.** **As** the platform, **I want** a mature engine wrapped in a player core, **so that** any format plays correctly. **Acceptance:** the libmpv binding is added + vendored (airgap-verify early, `--locked`; honest fallback note if unfetchable); a `Player` wraps mpv (load/play/pause/seek/stop, position/duration/state events, track enumeration); state machine unit-tested against a fake mpv seam; real-clip smoke on the farm when `libmpv` present, else honest-gated. ¬ß6 glue.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-2: DRM overlay video plane.** **As** a user, **I want** smooth video, **so that** playback is crisp + low-power. **Acceptance:** mpv video scans out on a HW overlay plane beneath the egui shell, composited with the shell's DRM ownership (no tearing/z-fight); egui chrome/OSD draws above; plane resize/position track the player pane; seam-tested; honest-gated where no plane is available (render-to-texture fallback documented).
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-3: PipeWire audio + processing.** **As** a user, **I want** great audio, **so that** sound is rich + level. **Acceptance:** mpv audio ‚Üí PipeWire (seat audio); graphic EQ + audio filters + loudness normalization/ReplayGain + gapless, via the mpv af-graph; config folds unit-tested.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-4: VA-API decode + video adjustments.** **As** a user, **I want** HW decode + geometry control. **Acceptance:** VA-API decode with software fallback; aspect/zoom/crop/rotate/deinterlace + filters; config folds tested; honest fallback when no VA-API.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-5: subtitles + multi-track.** **As** a user, **I want** subtitles + track choice. **Acceptance:** embedded + external (.srt/.ass) with ASS styling/positioning/delay; OpenSubtitles online fetch by hash (egress, fail-soft); full audio/subtitle/video track selection with language labels; fixture-tested.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-6: playlists + advanced controls.** **As** a user, **I want** queues + fine control. **Acceptance:** save/load playlists, queue, shuffle, repeat, gapless; speed, A/V-sync offsets, chapters, frame-step, snapshot, A-B loop; queue + control model unit-tested.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-7: local library + resume.** **As** a user, **I want** a browsable library that remembers me. **Acceptance:** index chosen folders (+ mesh mounts) from embedded metadata + local artwork with online TMDB/TVDB scrape (egress, fail-soft); per-title resume + continue-watching + watch history; index/scan + resume store tested.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-8: the mde-media-egui surface shell (Carbon ¬ß4).** **As** a user, **I want** a full media app. **Acceptance:** Sources + Library browse + Player + Queue + PiP mini-player + auto-hide OSD; immersive fullscreen; platform-native rebindable keymap; Carbon chrome (no raw hex) + a translucent dark media OSD over video; egui snapshot + headless mount tests.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-9: Jellyfin client core.** **As** a user, **I want** to connect to Jellyfin. **Acceptance:** `reqwest`+serde client ‚Äî multi-server, Quick Connect + username/password login (saved), full browse (shows‚Üíseasons‚Üíepisodes, movies, music, collections, genres, artwork, Continue-Watching/Next-Up); fixture-tested against recorded API responses.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-10: Jellyfin playback + sync.** **As** a user, **I want** Jellyfin titles to play + sync. **Acceptance:** direct-play/direct-stream vs server-transcode (HLS) negotiation from the libmpv capability set; report progress + resume-across-devices + mark-played; cross-library search + filters + sort; Live-TV/DVR + music; negotiation + progress folds tested.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-11: Jellyfin offline + users.** **As** a user, **I want** offline + profiles. **Acceptance:** download titles to a managed local cache for offline playback; multiple user profiles + switching per server; cache lifecycle + user-switch tested.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-12: network streams + yt-dlp.** **As** a user, **I want** to play stream URLs + web videos. **Acceptance:** open direct stream URLs (http/hls/rtsp/mms) + resolve web-page videos via a bundled yt-dlp; URL detection + the yt-dlp seam tested (honest-gated when the tool is absent).
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-13: capture devices.** **As** a user, **I want** to watch capture inputs. **Acceptance:** v4l2 / TV-tuner / capture-card input as a playable source; enumerate + open a device; honest-gated when no device present.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-14: mackesd mesh media-discovery service.** **As** a user, **I want** every mesh media source listed. **Acceptance:** auto-discover mesh nodes serving media ‚Äî Jellyfin, DLNA/UPnP, this-player-as-server, mesh file shares ‚Äî via mDNS + the mesh registry (reuse `mesh_media.rs`/`mdns_relay`); publish `state/media/sources` with reachability; discovery folds unit-tested. ¬ß6 mesh-side.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-15: mackesd mesh media server + DLNA + aggregation.** **As** a user, **I want** to share + see all mesh media in one place. **Acceptance:** share this node's chosen folders as a mesh media source (peers' MEDIA-14 finds it) + a DLNA/UPnP server; aggregate peers' shared media into one mesh library view (MEDIA-8 consumes); share manifest + aggregation merge tested. ¬ß6.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-16: session roaming.** **As** an operator, **I want** my playback to follow me between seats. **Acceptance:** a session record (title/position/queue/tracks/state) bound to the mesh identity + synced (Syncthing/etcd, like bookmarks); login at a new seat offers resume-where-paused + releases the old seat (single owned lease, no double-play); two-seat test: play‚Üíswitch‚Üíresume continues. ¬ß6 mesh-side.
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-17: sync-play party mode + casting.** **As** a user, **I want** to watch together + throw playback. **Acceptance:** a shared session several seats join where play/pause/seek propagate in sync; cast to a mesh node, a DLNA/UPnP renderer, or a Chromecast; propagation folds tested + a gated live cast leg (mirrors mesh_mount gating).
- [‚úì] **MEDIA-18: mount the media player into the shell dock (RESCUE ‚Äî reachability, 2026-07-03).** **As** a user, **I want** the VLC-class media player to actually open in the Quasar shell, **so that** MEDIA-1..17 are reachable in the shipped product (not shipped-but-dead). **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable): `mde-shell-egui` gains `Surface::Media` in `dock.rs` (enum + SURFACES list + label + render arm), driven by an embedded `mde_media_egui` lib panel (expose a `media_panel`/pump seam mirroring `files_panel`, ¬ß6 ‚Äî reuse the app, don't re-derive); the player renders + drives `mde_media_core` as a dock surface; `mde-media-egui` is added to the `generate-rpm` assets so it SHIPS (DoD = `rpm -qlp` shows it at the gated cut per [[strip-verify-replacement-ships-in-rpm]]); shell mount test green. **Found by the 2026-07-03 reconciliation:** `mde-media-egui` "compiles green, ships/launches nowhere" ‚Äî 0 references in `mde-shell-egui`, 0 RPM assets, 0 launchers. Serialize on CHOOSER-7 + TERM-16 (all edit `dock.rs`). **Blocks the 12.1 cut.**

## CHOOSER ‚Äî the Desktop Chooser for every discovered display source (operator 2026-07-02; design: docs/design/desktop-chooser.md)
A `mde-shell-egui` surface that aggregates every discovered desktop ‚Äî remote mesh-peer desktops, local KVM/cloud-hypervisor consoles, RDP/VNC/Spice endpoints ‚Äî into one live card grid (grouped by node, protocol badges, live thumbnails), auto-popping on new discovery over the BRAND-1 backdrop, and drives the VDI attach path (vdi.rs + mde-vdi-rdp/-vnc + a new mde-vdi-spice). Always-ask protocol; mesh-SSO + sealed external creds; full local-KVM lifecycle; per-connection fullscreen/windowed + multi-monitor; mesh-synced favorites. 15-lock survey in the design doc.

- [‚úì] **CHOOSER-1: mackesd desktop-source discovery aggregator.** **As** the platform, **I want** every desktop source discovered in one place, **so that** the Chooser can present them. **Acceptance:** collect from the mesh registry (peer-advertised desktops), mDNS (RDP/VNC/Spice on the LAN, reuse `mdns_relay`), and local KVM enumeration (`kvm.rs`/`vm_lifecycle`), + manual sources; publish `state/desktops/sources` (per-source node/protocols/reachability/OS/thumbnail-ref); discovery+merge folds unit-tested. ¬ß6 mesh-side.
- [‚úì] **CHOOSER-2: the Chooser surface (`mde-shell-egui`, Carbon ¬ß4).** **As** a user, **I want** to see + pick discovered desktops, **so that** connecting is one click. **Acceptance:** a live card grid grouped by node/host with protocol badges + status pips, over the BRAND-1 backdrop when empty; auto-popups on a new-source event; renders `state/desktops/sources`; ¬ß4 tokens (no raw hex); egui snapshot + headless mount tests (empty, populated, offline-greyed).
- [‚úì] **CHOOSER-3: live thumbnails.** **As** a user, **I want** a preview of each desktop, **so that** I recognize it at a glance. **Acceptance:** periodic preview thumbnails ‚Äî mesh peers publish a small snapshot, local VMs snapshot the framebuffer, external endpoints a cheap probe ‚Äî graceful protocol/OS-icon fallback; bounded refresh + cache; source‚Üíthumbnail plumbing + fallback tested.
- [‚úì] **CHOOSER-4: connect flow (protocol picker + display options).** **As** a user, **I want** to control how I connect, **so that** it fits the source. **Acceptance:** on connect, always-ask the protocol when several are offered; fullscreen-or-windowed choice; multi-monitor span/single choice; route to `mde-vdi-rdp`/`-vnc`/`-spice` via a `vdi.rs` `ConnectRequest`; request-construction folds tested.
- [‚úì] **CHOOSER-5: `mde-vdi-spice` client crate (Spice‚Üíegui).** **As** a user, **I want** native Spice for local VMs, **so that** they're fast. **Acceptance:** a first-class Spice client rendered egui-native like the RDP/VNC crates; airgap-verify the Spice crate (add+vendor, honest VNC-fallback note if unfetchable); connects to a KVM VM's Spice console; headless: connect‚Üía frame arrives. New workspace-member crate.
- [‚úì] **CHOOSER-6: auth.** **As** a user, **I want** seamless mesh login + secure external creds, **so that** connecting is easy + safe. **Acceptance:** mesh-peer desktops authenticate with the node's mesh identity (SSO, no prompt); external RDP/VNC/Spice creds sealed in the secret store (reuse FILEMGR-6 seal/derive), prompted once; never a plaintext credential on disk/logs; seal/read + SSO path tested. _(2026-07-03: landed `ec718b2` ‚Äî auth.rs model + SSO (reuses `discovery::local_peer`, no prompt) + prompt-once UI + `CredentialStore` seal seam + log-safety (`Secret` redacts, no `Display`; no plaintext to Debug/logs), 221t, reachable (wired into chooser.rs/vdi.rs). **¬ß6-GATED FOLLOW-ON (mesh tier, NOT desktop):** the *live* external-cred seal into the mesh store ‚Äî FILEMGR-6's `SecretStore` (Argon2id+XChaCha20) lives inside the `mackesd` daemon behind `async-services`, which the desktop shell must not link (¬ß6); `MeshCredentialStore` honestly returns `SealOutcome::Gated` today. Needs a **mesh-side desktop-cred sealing worker** to back the seam so external creds persist across sessions ‚Äî tracked here for a mesh-tier unit.)_
- [‚úì] **CHOOSER-7: local-KVM lifecycle from cards.** **As** a user, **I want** to power local VMs from the Chooser, **so that** a stopped desktop is one click away. **Acceptance:** start/stop/pause a discovered local VM + open its console, driving the mackesd `vm_lifecycle` worker; the card reflects live power state; action dispatch + state reflection tested; honest-gated where no local hypervisor.
- [‚úì] **CHOOSER-8: card actions + find + states.** **As** a user, **I want** to manage + find desktops, **so that** the grid scales. **Acceptance:** per-card context menu (connect, favorite/pin, edit, remove manual, KVM power); search + filter (node/protocol/status/OS) + sort; offline/unreachable sources greyed with a reason + retry, never a blocking probe; filter/sort + the non-blocking offline model tested.
- [‚úì] **CHOOSER-9: mesh-synced favorites/recents/manual sources.** **As** an operator, **I want** my desktop list to follow me, **so that** every seat is the same. **Acceptance:** favorites, recents, and manual sources bound to the mesh identity + synced via Syncthing (like bookmarks); two-seat test: pin at one seat ‚Üí visible at another. ¬ß6 mesh-side.

## MESH-VIRT ‚Äî Fedora+KVM virt management, no center (operator 2026-06-30; design: docs/design/mesh-virt-management.md)
Replaces the XCP-NG toolstack with a **Fedora + KVM + Podman** stack driven by `mackesd` (the xapi-equivalent), no central orchestrator (#5 mesh-native; Incus the adopt-fallback, Nomad excluded on BUSL). The Datacenter interfaces drive the KVM services on each node. This is the KVM-equivalent of the deleted XCP-NG worker/catalog.

- [‚úì] **MV-1: `KVM_SERVICES` catalog + per-node service set.** **As** a node, **I want** the KVM stack (`qemu-kvm`/`libvirt` + sockets, `podman.socket`, NetworkManager, a metrics worker, optional `multipathd`) baked into the one image + a `KVM_SERVICES` catalog (replacing the removed `XCPNG_SERVICES`), **so that** every node carries the libvirt/Podman equivalent of the toolstack. **Acceptance:** the dnf set is in the image; `libvirtd`/`podman.socket` enabled; `KVM_SERVICES` lists the units; KVM modules load.
- [‚úì] **MV-2: `mackesd` kvm-host-health worker.** **As** an operator, **I want** a worker publishing `KVM_SERVICES` health to `event/kvm/services` (mirroring the removed xcpng-health), **so that** Datacenter panels show per-node KVM-stack health. **Acceptance:** reports each unit up/down + a host summary; injectable probe; unit-tested.
- [‚úì] **MV-3: `mackesd` vm-lifecycle worker over libvirt.** **As** the Datacenter UI, **I want** `mackesd` to create/start/stop/migrate VMs via libvirt (the `xapi`+`xenopsd`+`sm`+`xcp-networkd` equivalent; cloud-hypervisor kept for the VDI desktop fast-path), **so that** the Datacenter interfaces drive KVM. **Acceptance:** a VM is created/started/stopped via the worker; a libvirt storage pool + virtual network are managed; it appears in the mesh map.
- [‚úì] **MV-4: `mackesd` container worker over Podman.** **As** the Datacenter UI, **I want** `mackesd` to run/stop Podman containers on a chosen node, **so that** the layer covers containers too. **Acceptance:** a Podman service is launched/stopped via the worker + reachable by peers (behind the host's cert).
- [‚úì] **MV-5: No-center scheduler (#5) + Cockpit console.** **As** the mesh, **I want** desired-state + placement in the existing etcd/Syncthing so any node schedules with no center, with Cockpit (`cockpit-machines`/`cockpit-podman`) as the per-node console, **so that** "no fixed center" is structural. **Acceptance:** a VM/container scheduled from any node lands + survives that node's loss (placed workloads keep running); Cockpit reachable per node. *(MV-5a placement landed `91888d6`; MV-5b failover `7f2d369` landed ‚Üí MV-5 complete (60 tests); Cockpit per node via node-virt.yml (MV-1))*
- [‚úì] **MV-6: Datacenter/Fleet plane drives KVM ‚Äî `mde-shell-egui` (egui, `Plane::Fleet`), NOT the retired iced `mde-workbench`.** **As** an operator, **I want** the Datacenter/Instances panels to drive `mackesd`'s libvirt+Podman workers (not xapi), **so that** the UI manages the KVM stack. **Acceptance:** the panel lists nodes' VMs+containers from `event/kvm/services` + the lifecycle workers; create/start/stop works live, rendered through `Style`. *(MV-6 + MV-6b `d68613d`: VMs live-driven + container roster read-only; container lifecycle-drive = follow-up)*
- [!] **MV-7: Adopt-XCP-ng (day-2, optional).** *(session=819545e6, e50b693)* **As** an operator with existing XCP-ng iron, **I want** a day-2 "adopt hypervisor" action that enrolls + drives it via `xe`/tofu (as the live farm does), **so that** existing XCP-ng capacity joins the mesh without being a role. **Acceptance:** an existing XCP-ng host is adopted + serves VMs to the mesh; it is never produced by our installer. **CORE DONE `e50b693`:** the `mackesd adopt-xcp` verb ‚Äî pure `plan_adopt` ‚Üí ordered idempotent `AdoptStep`s (mint static-member token ‚Üí enroll dom0 as a static Nebula member ‚Üí register roster row ‚Üí attach + converge the XAPI toolstack via `xe`/`tofu`) or a retryable `Blocked`; injectable `Adopter` seam (`LiveAdopter` integration-gated, typed `IntegrationGated` errors ‚Äî never fake success); `--dry-run`. Reuses `invite::resolve_mesh_id` + `ca::bundle` + `peers`. Farm-green (11 tests, clippy-clean). **REMAINING (integration-gated, stays [>]):** the live enroll + xe/tofu drive against a real XCP-ng host (needs live SSH + the xen-xapi provider + host creds ‚Äî classifier-gated).

## DRAIN-ENGINE ‚Äî keep the build going until the worklist is clear (operator 2026-06-24; design: docs/design/autonomous-drain.md)
Methods so the autonomous drain can't be derailed by the mechanical failures that halted it (disk wedges 4√ó, sequential grinding, stalling on blockers). Locks: **Hybrid engine** (FARM-AUTO reconciler builds; AI supervises) ¬∑ **Hard enforcement** (local builds impossible) ¬∑ **Park + keep draining** (never stall on one item).
- [‚úì] **DRAIN-1: cargo-farm-guard ‚Äî make local builds impossible.** `install-helpers/cargo-farm-guard.sh` installs AS `cargo`; `build/test/check/clippy/run` exit 97 with a farm redirect, `fmt/metadata` pass through. **Acceptance:** a dev-host `cargo build` exits non-zero with the redirect; `xcp-build.sh` (farm) unaffected. *(verified standalone 2026-06-24: build‚Üí97.)*
- [‚úì] **DRAIN-2: disk-watchdog ‚Äî auto-heal disk pressure.** `install-helpers/disk-watchdog.sh` reclaims stray `target/` + aged logs when free `<` threshold; **active-safe** (never nukes a live agent's worktree). **Acceptance:** below-threshold free space triggers reclaim; a live agent's worktree survives.
- [‚úì] **DRAIN-3: install-drain-guardrails ‚Äî operator-run activator.** `install-helpers/install-drain-guardrails.sh {--install|--uninstall}` installs the guard + a 5-min watchdog systemd timer; reversible (real toolchain preserved as `cargo-real`). **Operator runs it** (self-installing persistence is not agent-authorized). **Acceptance:** `--install` makes the guard live + the timer active; `--uninstall` restores.
- [‚úì] **DRAIN-4: FARM-AUTO reconciler ‚Äî the no-AI mechanical build half.** A timer reads open units tagged `@farm:{crate,verify}`, builds the slice on the farm, opens a PR, flips the task to needs-review ‚Äî no AI tokens in the build loop (¬ß10 / build-platform.md). **Acceptance:** an `@farm`-tagged open unit produces a farm-green PR with zero AI tokens spent; red builds raise a triage task.
- [‚úì] **DRAIN-5: park-and-continue ‚Äî never stall on a blocker.** A unit hitting a live-infra/artifact/gate blocker becomes `[!]` + a `docs/NEEDS-OPERATOR.md` entry; the loop continues with the next unblocked unit. **Acceptance:** a blocked unit appears in NEEDS-OPERATOR.md and the loop advances ‚Äî zero whole-loop stalls attributable to one item. ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-25): `install-helpers/park-blocker.sh <ID> "<reason>"` flips the first open bullet for `<ID>` to `[!]`, annotates it `_(BLOCKED: ‚Ä¶ ‚Äî see NEEDS-OPERATOR.md)_`, surfaces it under "Parked by the drain loop" in `docs/NEEDS-OPERATOR.md`, and exits 0 so the loop continues. Idempotent; word-boundary id match (FAKE-1 ‚âÝ FAKE-10); not-found ‚Üí exit 1; self-tested green. (The prior NEEDS-OPERATOR "blocked: ¬ßC.4 absent" note was itself stale ‚Äî ¬ßC.4 exists ‚Äî now removed.)
- [‚úì] **DRAIN-6: coordinator pattern in /ship.** Encode: pre-flight disk-watchdog ‚Üí saturate N farm agents (disjoint crates, farm-only) ‚Üí on each completion merge+reclaim+relaunch (no batch-wait) ‚Üí park-don't-stall ‚Üí no-flinch. **Acceptance:** with the loop running, N agents stay in flight until the open+unblocked queue is empty; a completed agent is merged+replaced within one tick. ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-25): `install-helpers/drain-coordinator.sh {plan|slots|next|preflight}` encodes the tick (preflight `disk-watchdog.sh` ‚Üí free-slot compute over the REAL `.50/.90/.130` topology, caps 2/2/3 ‚Üí next N open-unblocked unit ids); the ship skill gained a "coordinator loop (DRAIN-5/6/7)" section wiring drain-coordinator + park-blocker + assert-own-worktree with the rearm-don't-batch-wait + park-don't-stall + no-flinch discipline, and its stale `.50/.51/.52` topology table is corrected to `.50/.90/.130`. `slots` verified live (free 2/1/3 ‚Üí 6).
- [‚úì] **DRAIN-7: worktree-isolation discipline.** A subagent strayed into the shared `calm-ray-dcr8` worktree + its work was wiped (2026-06-24). Agents must operate ONLY in their assigned isolated worktree. **Acceptance:** an agent's STEP-0 verifies it is in its own worktree (not the shared one) and refuses to edit/reset the shared checkout. ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-25): `install-helpers/assert-own-worktree.sh` is the agent STEP-0 guard ‚Äî REFUSES (exit 3) the shared `calm-ray-dcr8`/primary checkout, PASSES (exit 0) only from an isolated worktree; `--coordinator` asserts the inverse. Verified: refuse-from-shared, pass-from-isolated (incl. a real `wf_*` worktree), coordinator-from-shared. The ship skill mandates it as every isolated subagent's STEP-0.

## INCIDENT ‚Äî mde-bus broker resilience (BROKER-RESILIENCE-1, diagnosed live 2026-06-25)
A missing/skipped `ntfy` broker (`<overlay_ip>:8443`) was design-"non-fatal" but FATAL in practice: mackesd kept publishing to the unreachable `:8443` (every publish persisted to the `/run/mde-bus` spool, which grew unbounded ‚Äî observed boot-readiness 25M + audit 19M + compute 13M ‚âà 77M of a 190M tmpfs) and the broker-unreachable path starved the 60 s systemd watchdog ‚Üí `status=6/ABRT` ~every 3 min (NRestarts climbing on both lighthouses). The broker client was `reqwest::Client::new()` with NO timeout.
- [‚úì] **BROKER-RESILIENCE-1: a skipped/unreachable broker is truly non-fatal.** Four-part fix: **(1)** the outbound-publish reqwest client now has a CONNECT (3 s) + overall REQUEST (5 s) timeout via a shared `hooks::publisher::broker_client()` used by both the webhook listener and the `mde-bus publish` CLI, so a publish to a dead broker fails FAST instead of hanging ~60 s. **(2)** when `broker::evaluate_prereqs` returns `Skip`, the daemon binds the webhook listener in a new persist-only mode (`ListenerConfig::persist_only_for_overlay_ip`) ‚Äî it still ingests + persists + audits but skips the doomed outbound POST entirely (mirrors `--no-broker`), so a known-absent broker drives no outbound retries. **(3)** a conservative per-topic `/run` cap (`TOPIC_RUN_CAP_BYTES` = 8 MiB + 20k-entry backstop) now bounds EVERY non-audit topic to its most-recent window every retention pass (the analogue of the existing `audit/*` cap), so a down broker can never fill the tmpfs. **(4)** verified the sd_notify watchdog ping rides its own 250 ms timer in mackesd, sharing no task with any broker/spool call. **Acceptance:** a publish to a dead broker returns within the timeout (not ~60 s); a skipped-broker daemon persists without retrying outbound; the spool stays bounded under sustained no-broker publishes. *(build + clippy + new tests GREEN on the farm, slot `brokerfix`.)*
- [‚úì] **BROKER-RESILIENCE-2 / WATCHDOG-2: the watchdog ping was STILL being starved ‚Äî real root cause + fix (11.0.11, 2026-06-27).** BR-1 part (4)'s claim ("the ping rides its own 250 ms timer, sharing no task with any broker/spool call ‚Üí can't be starved") was **false in practice**: both production lighthouses kept watchdog-aborting every ~90 s for ~40 h (lh1 1355 / lh2 1348 `status=6/ABRT`), across 11.0.8‚Üí11.0.10, which blocked every enrollment (`:4243` only up between crashes). The ping rode `tokio::time::sleep` **on the runtime**, and on a **1-vCPU droplet** `new_multi_thread` defaults to a SINGLE worker that also owns the **tokio time driver**; when that worker reaches a blocking bridge (`substrate::peers::block_on` ‚Üí `block_in_place` for an etcd round-trip) the time driver **freezes**, the sleep never fires, and systemd SIGABRTs a healthy daemon. A missing broker reliably triggered it via extra `block_in_place` churn. Fix: **(a)** floor the runtime at 4 worker threads even on 1 vCPU (`bin/mackesd.rs`), so a second worker keeps timers alive while another blocks; **(b)** move the heartbeat to a **dedicated OS thread** gated on an async liveness beacon the serve loop stamps every 250 ms (`sd_notify::watchdog_should_ping`) ‚Äî kernel-scheduled (unstarvable) yet still reflects true liveness (a genuine wedge stops the beat ‚Üí ping withheld ‚Üí systemd restarts). Released as signed **11.0.11** (RSA-4096 d0921c73 verifies on F43) ‚Üí GitHub Release + gh-pages dnf channel (fedora-43/44). **Acceptance:** lh1/lh2 stop crash-looping after upgrade (NRestarts stops climbing, zero new ABRT, `:4243` stays up) ‚Äî the live deploy/verify is the remaining step (operator-gated channel `dnf upgrade`). *(farm: 7/7 lib tests incl. new beacon tests, clippy+fmt clean, `cargo check --bin` exit 0.)*
- [‚úì] **BROKER-RESILIENCE-3: the broker is now turn-key PRESENT on a fresh lighthouse, not just non-fatal when absent.** BR-1/2 made a missing `ntfy` broker survivable; this makes it actually get installed at provision time. The chain was already wired (RPM vendors the pinned `ntfy_2.24.0` tarball at `/usr/share/magic-mesh/vendor/`; `mesh-install-ntfy` is shipped + bundled-first/offline-capable + idempotent; post_install `enable`s `mesh-broker-setup.service`), but the oneshot is only `enable`d ‚Äî NOT `--now` (deliberately, so the dnf transaction never blocks on `network-online.target`). So on a freshly provisioned lighthouse that never reboots, there was no broker until the first reboot. Fix: both lighthouse cloud-inits (`do-lighthouse-cloudinit.sh` found-path + `do-lighthouse-join-cloudinit.sh` join-path) now `systemctl start --no-block` the three first-boot fetch oneshots (`mesh-broker-setup` / `mesh-netdata-setup` / `mesh-shell-setup`) after the daemon comes up ‚Äî post-boot, network up, idempotent, non-stalling. **Acceptance:** a just-provisioned lighthouse has `/usr/bin/ntfy` (and netdata + starship) without a reboot; re-running is a no-op. *(`bash -n` clean on both scripts; pure cloud-init template change, no compile.)*

## LIGHTHOUSE-MIGRATION ‚Äî 3 new lighthouses, retire old 2, move Eagle (DONE 2026-06-27)
Goal: "Create 3 new Lighthouses, Delete the existing 2, move Eagle to the new Lighthouses." **COMPLETE + live-verified.** Live topology is now Eagle (10.42.0.2) + **nyc3 (10.42.0.4) / fra1 (10.42.0.5) / sfo3 (10.42.0.6)**; old lh1 (167.71.247.150) + mcnf-lh2 (68.183.55.253) droplets deleted; etcd = 4 healthy voters; Eagle's roster dials only .4/.5/.6; cross-mesh connectivity verified. Three turn-key code gaps were found+fixed live and shipped (signed, gh-pages dnf channel):
- [‚úì] **11.0.11 WATCHDOG-2** ‚Äî the watchdog crash-loop (see INCIDENT above).
- [‚úì] **11.0.12 LIGHTHOUSE-ENROLL-SELF-CERT** ‚Äî a joined lighthouse self-generates its `/enroll` endpoint cert at startup (CA key present + cert absent), so `:4243` binds and it can SERVE enrollment, not just sign. Proven: a new node enrolled against nyc3.
- [‚úì] **11.0.13 MULTI-LH-IP-ALLOC** ‚Äî overlay-IP allocation now consults the global etcd directory (`allocate_overlay_ip_excluding`), not just the local cert-store, so a joined lighthouse no longer hands a new node a colliding `.1`. Proven: re-test node via nyc3 got 10.42.0.7 (unique).
### Follow-ups (turn-key sharp edges found during the migration)
- [‚úì] **MIG-1: `mackesd remove-peer` must delete the etcd `/mesh/peers/<host>` directory key.** It removes the etcd MEMBER + revokes + bans, but leaves the directory row, so the roster reconcile kept re-adding the dead node until the key was `etcdctl del`'d by hand. Decommission must drop the directory entry too.
- [‚úì] **MIG-2: atomic cross-lighthouse overlay-IP allocation.** _(shipped 11.0.14, d6e6f20)_ 11.0.13 reads the directory at sign time (closes the systematic collision), but two lighthouses signing in the SAME instant can still race (the parallel sfo3+fra1 provision hit a `(overlay_ip,epoch)` UNIQUE collision). Make allocation atomic via an etcd CAS/lease, or serialize signing per mesh.
- [‚úì] **MIG-3: provision the CA-backup passphrase on a joined lighthouse.** _(DONE, integrated a862854: `cmd_join`'s lighthouse path now calls `provision_ca_backup_passphrase_if_lighthouse` ‚Äî a new `ca::backup_provision` module mints a fresh 256-bit CSPRNG passphrase, seals it host-bound via `systemd-creds encrypt --with-key=auto` (TPM/host-key, NOT mesh-replicated) to `/etc/mackesd/backup-passphrase.cred` 0600 + writes the `LoadCredentialEncrypted` drop-in, so the upcoming mackesd restart surfaces it at `$CREDENTIALS_DIRECTORY/backup-passphrase` where `nebula_ca_backup` reads ‚Üí SEC-7/ENT-11 clears. Generated-on-joiner (secret never leaves the box, never logged), idempotent, no-op for Server/Workstation. 8 new tests; mackesd 1239 lib tests green. **Live-boot confirmation of the cleared warning is the remaining check (systemd-creds round-trip only exercises on a real host).** The off-fleet CA backup PUSH stays operator-run (classifier-blocked) ‚Äî that's the separate DR line below.)_ A joined lighthouse holds the CA key but had no backup passphrase credential ‚Üí `SEC-7/ENT-11: the CA is UNBACKED-UP` error each boot.
- [‚úì] **MIG-4: provision a sequential lighthouse-add (no parallel) or fix MIG-2 first.** _(resolved by MIG-2 ‚Äî atomic alloc landed, so the sequential-only constraint is lifted)_ `do-lighthouse-join.sh` runs must be sequential until MIG-2 lands (parallel runs collide on IP allocation).

## FARM-AUTOSCALE ‚Äî demand-driven elastic build farm (operator 2026-06-24; design: docs/design/farm-autoscale.md)
Tofu auto-scaling + full lifecycle of VM **and** POD resources: each dom0 runs EITHER one hardware-maxing big build VM OR several small VMs/agent pods, created/destroyed by tofu to fit the live build queue ‚Äî best on-demand hardware use. Locks: **demand-driven** (the @farm queue is the signal) ¬∑ **FARM-AUTO reconciler orchestrates** (no AI in the loop) ¬∑ **warm pool, scale-to-zero + snapshot-reset** ¬∑ **mutually-exclusive shapes per dom0, demand wins**.
- [‚úì] **FA-1: tofu shape model.** **As** the farm, **I want** a per-dom0 `shape` var (`big`/`small`/`off`) + `small_count` driving `infra/tofu/build-vms.tf`, **so that** `tofu apply` provisions one hardware-maxing big VM, N standard small VMs, or nothing. **Acceptance:** `shape=big` on BigBoy provisions ~10vCPU/26GiB `mcnf-build-big-52`; `shape=small,count=2` provisions 2 standard VMs; `shape=off` destroys them (scale-to-zero); idempotent re-apply.
- [‚úì] **FA-2: golden `clean` snapshot + fast reset.** **As** the autoscaler, **I want** each toolchained build VM to carry a post-toolchain `clean` snapshot and a `farm-vm reset <vm>` that `xe snapshot-revert`s it, **so that** inter-job state returns to baseline without a full re-clone. **Acceptance:** a build dirties the VM, `reset` reverts to clean (toolchain + sccache priming intact, job state gone), verified on a reset drill.
- [‚úì] **FA-3: the farm-autoscaler reconcile step (no AI).** **As** the FARM-AUTO reconciler, **I want** a step that reads the `@farm` queue, classifies each pending job big/small, computes the desired per-dom0 shape, writes the tofu vars, and `tofu apply`s ‚Äî scaling to zero when idle, **so that** the farm matches demand with zero AI tokens. **Acceptance:** a queued whole-workspace build ‚Üí big VM provisioned + the build runs + scaled down after; many per-crate jobs ‚Üí small√óN provisioned + run in parallel + scaled to zero; no AI tokens spent.
- [‚úì] **FA-4: mutual-exclusion drain/preempt + hysteresis.** **As** a dom0, **I want** to run EITHER big OR small (never both), switching only after draining current jobs, with a min-dwell debounce, **so that** shape changes don't thrash against tofu's ~minutes apply latency. **Acceptance:** a big job queued while smalls run ‚Üí smalls drain, then destroy+provision big; a dom0 never hosts big+small simultaneously; no flip within the dwell window.
- [‚úì] **FA-5: POD-level scaling.** **As** the autoscaler, **I want** to cap agent/build podman pods per VM to its vCPU/RAM budget and fold pod demand into the shape choice, **so that** many queued agent pods provision small√óN rather than starving one big VM. **Acceptance:** pod count per VM never exceeds its core budget; a pod-heavy queue biases the dom0 toward the small shape.
- [‚úì] **FA-6: route builds/agents by shape.** **As** a build job, **I want** `xcp-build.sh` + the drain coordinator to target the autoscaler-provisioned VM matching my shape (big‚ÜíBigBoy's big VM, small‚Üíthe small pool), **so that** jobs land on the right elastic resource. **Acceptance:** a whole-workspace build routes to the big VM; per-crate builds spread across the small pool; routing degrades to BigBoy if the autoscaler is paused.
- [‚úì] **FA-7: lifecycle observability.** **As** an operator, **I want** the autoscaler to log every create/destroy + publish the live farm topology (per-dom0 shape + utilization) to a CLI/Workbench surface, **so that** on-demand use is auditable. **Acceptance:** each scale event is logged with the reason; `farm topology` (CLI + panel) shows current shapes, running VMs, and per-dom0 utilization.

## ENTERPRISE FIT-AND-FINISH (2026-06-11) ‚Äî toward an enterprise-class deliverable

Lifted from a 5-pass parallel fit-and-finish evaluation (reliability ¬∑ security ¬∑ observability ¬∑ packaging/release ¬∑ quality/UX) for an enterprise deliverable **within the stated ‚â§8-peer flat-trust envelope** (¬ß8 ‚Äî NOT a zero-trust/hyperscale product). `EFF-#` ids. P1 = blocks a credible enterprise/production cut.

> **DRAIN STATUS (2026-06-12):** the tractable EFF backlog is drained ‚Äî ~30 items closed this session (EFF-1..17, 19..23, 25..28, 32, 33, 35, 36, 39..44, 46..49) plus the AUD2/AUD3 audit-fix sets and 6 audit cycles (converged CLEAN). **ZERO EFF items remain open ‚Äî the ENTERPRISE FIT-AND-FINISH program is fully drained** (49 items closed/resolved). The only remaining tracker content is the PEERS feature epic (feature backlog, not fit-and-finish). EFF-18 (resolved: operator chose to keep the correct serial CI) and EFF-31 (resolved: hard coverage gate at 84.84%/80) are now closed. The PEERS epic below is feature backlog, not fit-and-finish. Resuming the GUI items is a deliberate next step, not a quick drain.

### P1 ‚Äî blockers for a production cut

- [‚úì] **EFF-1 ¬∑ SEC ¬∑ FileXfer Send-To path traversal (target).** `ipc/files.rs:265` joins the `peer:<target>` selector raw into `inbox_root(target)` ‚Äî `peer:../../etc` escapes the QNM root (`create_dir_all` + write anywhere mackesd can). Reject `target` with `/`,`..`,`\0`,non-`[A-Za-z0-9._-]`; assert the resolved dest is under `<qnm>/inbox/`. *(Regression from AUD-1 this session.)*
- [‚úì] **EFF-2 ¬∑ SEC ¬∑ FileXfer Send-To arbitrary-file read (sources).** `ipc/files.rs:290` copies caller-supplied absolute `sources` verbatim ‚Üí a Bus writer can exfil `/etc/shadow`/keys into a peer's replicated inbox. Confine sources to an allowlisted root (operator home / declared share); refuse symlinks + paths outside it. ‚Äî DONE: `FileXfer` gained a `share_root` (defaults to the operator home, canonicalized; `with_share_root` override). `allowed_source()` canonicalizes each source (resolving symlinks + `..`), requires a regular file, and refuses anything not `starts_with(share_root)` ‚Äî refused sources are skipped + warn-logged + counted in the reply's `refused` field. Two regression tests: a source outside the root is refused while an in-root one delivers, and a symlink-under-root ‚Üí outside is refused.
- [‚úì] **EFF-3 ¬∑ SEC ¬∑ FileXfer rollback path traversal.** `ipc/files.rs:338` removes files from `inbox_root(target).join(host).join(f)` off forgeable outbox rows. Same target/basename validation + canonicalize-and-contain before `remove_file`.
- [‚úì] **EFF-4 ¬∑ REL ¬∑ Supervisor doesn't restart on worker PANIC.** `workers/mod.rs:481` matches only `Ok/Err`; a panicking `run()` becomes a logged `JoinError`, never restarted. Wrap each `worker.run()` so a panic ‚Üí restartable `Err` (feed the back-off/breaker).
- [‚úì] **EFF-5 ¬∑ REL ¬∑ Worker-loop `Mutex.lock().expect()` poisons ‚Üí permanently kills the worker** (compute_expose/firewall_monitor/compute_registry/peer_join). With EFF-4 this silently downs workers. Use poison-tolerant locks (`PoisonError::into_inner`) or `parking_lot`.
- [‚úì] **EFF-6 ¬∑ REL ¬∑ `mackesd healthz` GUI refresh has no timeout** (`panels/mesh_control.rs:606`) ‚Äî a hung daemon spins the panel forever. Run with a timeout wrapper + render "healthz timed out".
- [‚úì] **EFF-7 ¬∑ REL ¬∑ Bus responder threads have no restart + reply closures no `catch_unwind`** (`bin/mackesd.rs:6146`, `ipc/files.rs:64`) ‚Äî one panicking request downs Fleet.Files/Settings/file surfaces for the session. Wrap reply dispatch in `catch_unwind` ‚Üí `err()` body.
- [‚úì] **EFF-8 ¬∑ OPS ¬∑ `healthz` returns a hardcoded `HealthReport::empty()`** (`bin/mackesd.rs:1500`, `ipc/shell.rs:102`) ‚Äî never live state (leader/node-count/applied-revision all unset). Populate from the store via one shared fn used by CLI + IPC. *(Highest-value ops gap.)* ‚Äî DONE: `HealthReport::from_store(conn)` populates real node_count + healthy/degraded/unreachable buckets + audit_chain_intact (Break‚Üífalse, Empty/Intact‚Üítrue); wired into CLI `Cmd::Healthz` + `ShellService::build_healthz` (both open the store per call, fall back to `empty()` if no store). Remainder: `is_leader`/`applied_revision` stay defaulted pending leader-lease + applied-revision query plumbing.
- [‚úì] **EFF-9 ¬∑ OPS ¬∑ Prometheus textfile exporter built but never written.** `metrics::write_textfile` has zero callers. Add a periodic worker snapshotting control-plane counters (revisions, drift, reconcile failures, breaker trips, peer health, cert-days). ‚Äî DONE: new `metrics_exporter` worker (Lighthouse-tier, 30s cadence) snapshots store-derivable gauges (mesh node-health buckets, audit-chain-intact, applied-migration count) via `snapshot_counters(conn)` reusing `HealthReport::from_store` (single source of truth with healthz), atomically writes `<textfile_collector>/mackesd.prom`. Remainder (follow-ups appending to the same file): runtime in-process counters (drift/reconcile-failures/breaker-trips) need a shared process registry the workers increment; cert days-remaining is EFF-11.
- [‚úì] **EFF-10 ¬∑ OPS ¬∑ Structured-logging plane logs human text, not the documented JSON.** `bin/mackesd.rs:1469` uses `fmt()` not `.json()`; `LogContext`/correlation-id unused. Switch the subscriber to JSON (env/flag-gated for TTY) + a span layer for the fields.
- [‚úì] **EFF-11 ¬∑ OPS ¬∑ No certificate-expiry monitoring/alert.** Certs store `expire_at` but nothing computes days-remaining; a ‚â§8 mesh silently loses every cert at turnover. Add a periodic check ‚Üí `healthz`/metrics/alert under a threshold. ‚Äî DONE: new `ca::expiry` module probes the **CA cert** (the real cliff ‚Äî peer certs are epoch-lifetime sentinel `0` by design, so per-peer expiry was a non-target) via `nebula-cert print -json` ‚Üí `details.notAfter` ‚Üí days-remaining (pure `parse_not_after_unix` is unit-tested). Wired into the `metrics_exporter` worker: each tick emits `mackesd_ca_cert_days_remaining` (clamped ‚â•0) + `mackesd_ca_cert_expiry_warning` (1 at/under the 30-day threshold) and logs a warn under threshold (the alert). Remainder: surfacing days-remaining on `healthz`/HealthReport would need `from_store` to take the CA path + run the subprocess (it's store-only today) ‚Äî Prometheus alert-rule on the metric covers the operational need; the healthz field is a thin follow-up.
- [‚úì] **EFF-12 ¬∑ OPS ¬∑ systemd units have no sandboxing.** `packaging/systemd/*.service` set only `NoNewPrivileges`. Add `ProtectSystem=strict`, `ProtectHome`, `PrivateTmp`, `ReadWritePaths`/`StateDirectory`, `RestrictAddressFamilies`, `MemoryMax`/`CPUQuota`, `LockPersonality`.
- [‚úì] **EFF-13 ¬∑ PKG ¬∑ RPM license contradicts the workspace license + copyleft deps.** generate-rpm `license = "proprietary"` vs workspace `GPL-3.0-or-later` + MPL/GPL pop-os deps. Reconcile the license string; add root `LICENSE`/`COPYING` + a `NOTICE` for bundled deps.
- [‚úì] **EFF-14 ¬∑ PKG ¬∑ No RPM scriptlets** ‚Äî daemon never enabled, no `systemctl daemon-reload`, no icon/desktop cache, no `/etc/mackesd` dir. Add `post_install`/`preun`/`post_uninstall` (daemon-reload + role-policy enable + `gtk-update-icon-cache` + `update-desktop-database`).
- [‚úì] **EFF-15 ¬∑ PKG ¬∑ `mackesd.service` won't start without the encrypted credential** (`LoadCredentialEncrypted=‚Ä¶/backup-passphrase.cred`, never created) ‚Äî fresh install = dead unit. Make the credential optional (Condition/wrapper) + create `/etc/mackesd` (0700) in a scriptlet.
- [‚úì] **EFF-16 ¬∑ PKG ¬∑ No supply-chain gating.** ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12): `deny.toml` (advisories deny-level w/ unmaintained=workspace-only; license allow-list scoped to what the tree ships, per-crate exceptions for rsip's X11-swapped text, clarifies for the license-field-less pop-os git crates; bans deny openssl/native-tls per ¬ß3, multiple-versions warn pending EFF-34; sources locked to crates.io + the pinned pop-os tree). Validated GREEN locally (cargo-deny 0.19.8: advisories/bans/licenses/sources all ok) so the new `supply-chain` CI job is a HARD gate; it also emits a CycloneDX SBOM artifact (cargo-cyclonedx). Bonus hardening en route: migrated mackes-nebula-https-tunnel off unmaintained `rustls-pemfile` (RUSTSEC-2025-0134) onto rustls-pki-types' PemObject; added the missing `license` field to 5 workspace crates; RUSTSEC-2023-0071 (rsa Marvin) ignored with written justification (keygen-only usage, no remote timing oracle ‚Äî ring does wire sign/verify).
- [‚úì] **EFF-17 ¬∑ PKG ¬∑ `magic-mesh-release` repo RPM referenced but never defined** (`packaging/repo/magic-mesh.repo:11`) ‚Äî so `dnf install <url>` leaves no repo for upgrades + the `gpgkey=` URL has no key. Define the release sub-package shipping the `.repo` + committed `RPM-GPG-KEY-magic-mesh`. ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12): generated the project signing key (Ed25519, 2y expiry; private key in the operator's `~/.gnupg`, revocation cert in `openpgp-revocs.d`); committed the public key at `packaging/repo/RPM-GPG-KEY-magic-mesh`. One-RPM design (no sub-package): the main RPM now ships the `.repo` ‚Üí `/etc/yum.repos.d/` + the key ‚Üí `/etc/pki/rpm-gpg/`, so a one-shot install leaves a working gpgcheck'd upgrade channel. Signing the RPM itself stays operator-gated at /release; the gh-pages publish of the key matches the gpgkey URL when stood up.
- [‚úì] **EFF-18 ¬∑ QA ¬∑ `set_var` env-race forces serial mackesd CI.** ‚Äî RESOLVED (2026-06-12, operator decision: option 3 ‚Äî keep the serial flag). The `--test-threads=1` run is CORRECT and green; mackesd's ~61 `set_var`/`remove_var` test sites mutate process-global env, which races the parallel harness. This was a CI-SPEED optimization only, and both alternatives carry flakiness risk (inject-config = large production ripple; `serial_test` = must annotate every env *reader*, not just writers). Operator chose to accept the safe serial suite rather than trade correctness for speed. WON'T-DO unless mackesd test latency becomes a real CI pain point, at which point option 1 (inject config) is the path. The CI job comments already document the serial requirement + this rationale.
- [‚úì] **EFF-19 ¬∑ CLI ¬∑ `magic-fleet` is a hand-rolled CLI** ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12): full clap derive port (real `--help`/`-V`, typed flags, unknown-flag errors with usage; `--root=`/`--hostname=` syntax the fleet_reconcile worker shells stays accepted). `--json` added to apply/heal/converge/elect/reconcile emitting one stable outcome object ({verb, drift, ok, changed, failures, unreachable, converged}; error form {verb, error, converged:false}); exit codes unchanged. Smoked: help, bad-flag rejection, apply --json round-trip; 49 tests green.

### P2 ‚Äî enterprise ratchet

- [‚úì] **EFF-20 ¬∑ REL ¬∑ ~8 daemon workers shell out blocking, no timeout** (firewall_preset/mesh_dns/mesh_firewall/cups_sync/netassess/peer_cap/netdata_aggregator/ssh_pubkey_gossip) ‚Äî a hung child pins a runtime thread. Route through the existing `subprocess_tick` timeout helper. ‚Äî DONE: new `workers/proc.rs` with `output_with_timeout`/`status_with_timeout` (blocking, dependency-free poll+kill) for the sync `tick_once` helpers and `status_with_timeout_async` (tokio) for the already-async workers, all killing the child at a 15s deadline. Routed every shell-out in all 8 workers (firewall_preset √ó5, cups_sync central run_lpadmin/run_capture + systemctl/lpoptions/hostname, netassess run_stdout/binary_present/ping, mesh_firewall, mesh_dns, netdata_aggregator systemctl, peer_cap + ssh_pubkey_gossip async). A hung child is now bounded to the timeout instead of pinning forever. Helper has 5 tests (kills a `sleep 60` promptly, captures fast output, surfaces spawn failure, async variant). Minor follow-up hygiene: the sync `tick_once`es still run on the runtime thread (now bounded, not infinite) ‚Äî wrapping them in `spawn_blocking` would also keep a slow-but-not-hung child off the scheduler.
- [‚úì] **EFF-21 ¬∑ SEC ¬∑ Secrets via env-var + argv.** ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12): (1) **daemon env scrub** ‚Äî run_serve captures `MDE_BACKUP_PASSPHRASE` once at boot, hands it to the backup worker via `with_passphrase`, and `remove_var`s it immediately, so the dozens of worker subprocesses (nebula-cert, df, firewall-cmd‚Ä¶) never inherit the secret; the exporter's backup-posture gauge rides a boot-time flag OR the systemd-creds file instead of a per-tick env read. The creds path (ENT-11, never env-borne) is untouched and stays preferred. (2) **stdin intake** ‚Äî `ca export`/`ca import` gained `--passphrase-stdin` (import requires `--input` since its default bundle source is stdin); `enroll` gained `--passcode-stdin`/`--token-stdin` with full clap conflict rules; shared `read_secret_line` helper, empty-secret rejected. Argv/env forms remain as documented fallbacks with prefer-stdin help text. Smoked: stdin passcode read+validation, help text, conflict rejection. 1448 serial green.
- [‚úì] **EFF-22 ¬∑ SEC ¬∑ Netdata `:19999` web UI not confined to the overlay** (aggregator rewrites only `[stream]`). Set `[web] bind to = <overlay-ip>`/127.0.0.1 and/or land the firewalld rule (the open NET-plane item). ‚Äî DONE: generalized the conf rewriter to `rewrite_named_section` and added `build_web_block` ‚Äî the aggregator now also writes a `[web] bind to = 127.0.0.1 <overlay-ip>` block each tick (loopback-only pre-enrolment), so the dashboard never binds the default `0.0.0.0`/underlay. Also fixed a latent non-idempotency in the rewriter (it grew a blank line per pass ‚Üí would have churned a netdata reload every tick); the trailing blank run is now collapsed so an unchanged conf is a true no-op. Tests: web block confines to overlay+loopback / loopback-only, a stock `0.0.0.0` bind is rewritten away, and re-running is idempotent.
- [‚úì] **EFF-23 ¬∑ SEC ¬∑ No body-size cap on Bus responders** ‚Äî `from_str` on unbounded bodies; cap inbound length + `sources`/row counts before parse. ‚Äî DONE: shared `ipc::MAX_RPC_BODY_BYTES` (64 KiB) + `body_within_cap()` + `body_too_large_reply()`. Applied at every body-parsing responder loop (files generic `poll_once`, fleet, settings, jobs, directory lifecycle-result/lifecycle/wake) ‚Äî an over-cap body is refused with an `{"error":‚Ä¶}` envelope + warn, never reaching `from_str`. send-to also caps `sources` at 1024 rows. Tests: over-cap body suppressed + within-cap dispatched.
- [‚úì] **EFF-24 ¬∑ OPS ¬∑ No readiness probe / per-worker liveness.** ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12): supervisor maintains a shared `WorkerStatusMap` (alive / restarts / breaker_tripped / last_exit_ok, updated at every lifecycle transition incl. ENT-6 trips); `HealthReport` gains serde-defaulted `workers_alive/workers_total/breaker_tripped/ready`; the Bus healthz (daemon in-process) folds live worker status into `ready` = audit-intact AND all-alive AND no-trip, while the CLI's store-only view reports the store half. Tests: lifecycle/restart tracking, alive-while-running, readiness fold (dead worker or trip ‚áí not ready). Honest remainder: 'leader known' stays out of `ready` until the EFF-8 leader-lease plumbing lands.
- [‚úì] **EFF-25 ¬∑ OPS ¬∑ Wire or remove the dead alert layer.** `events.rs`/`AlertHook`/`dispatch_alerts` have no live callers; only `Reconcile` of 5 `EventKind`s is emitted. Wire it + emit the missing kinds, or delete + document Netdata+firewall_monitor as the only sources. ‚Äî DONE (wired, 2026-06-12): `MackesdConfig` gained `[[alert_hooks]]` (kind + command, fail-open TOML; typo'd kind drops the hook with a warn ‚Äî never widened to fire-on-everything; empty command skipped) + `alert_hooks()` resolving to `events::AlertHook`. `apply_repair_rows` now returns its emitted `Event`s and the reconcile tick fires `dispatch_alerts` post-commit (a rolled-back event can never alert). Tests: TOML‚Üíhook resolution incl. drop/skip cases. Remainder (honest): only `Reconcile` events are emitted today; emitting `ConfigChange`/`Auth`/`Lifecycle`/`AdminAction` at their natural sites flows through the same dispatch automatically.
- [‚úì] **EFF-26 ¬∑ OPS ¬∑ Headless alert path + disk/breaker/backup alerts.** ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12): (1) alert_relay now journals EVERY alert at its severity level (`target: mackesd::alert`, error/warn/info) unconditionally and FIRST ‚Äî on a headless Lighthouse/Server the journal is the alert surface; Bus-FDO/notify-send toasts are additive. (2) The metrics exporter gained the continuous checks, each a gauge + a `mackesd::alert`-target journal alert: worker liveness/breaker (`mackesd_workers_alive/total`, `mackesd_breaker_tripped`; trip = repeated crit ERROR), disk headroom per monitored fs via bounded `df` (`mackesd_disk_available_bytes{path}`; warn <10% free; QNM root + store fs wired), and backup posture (`mackesd_backup_passphrase_set`, `mackesd_backup_age_seconds`; warns on passphrase-unset, >48h staleness, and enabled-but-no-bundle). Operators alert off either the journal (`journalctl -t ‚Ä¶ mackesd::alert`) or the Prometheus series.
- [‚úì] **EFF-27 ¬∑ OPS ¬∑ No day-2 admin guide.** ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12): root `ADMIN.md` walks the full lifecycle (install/first-boot ‚Üí mesh-init + enroll ‚Üí backup provision incl. the unset-passphrase alert behavior ‚Üí observability table (healthz/doctor/journal-alerts/metrics/hooks) ‚Üí dnf + fleet upgrade ‚Üí fleet rollback + node exceptions ‚Üí state-restore/ca-import DR ‚Üí cert lifecycle (days-remaining cliff, rotate, decommission, passcode) ‚Üí troubleshoot), cross-linking every docs/help runbook. All cited commands verified against the live CLI. Ships in the RPM at /usr/share/magic-mesh/.
- [‚úì] **EFF-28 ¬∑ OPS ¬∑ DR path untested + manual.** ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12): (1) `mackesd state-restore --verify` ‚Äî dry-run that dearmors + unseals + reports the bundle (mesh id, exported_at, CA/peer counts, meshfs presence) and stops before ANY mutation; exit 0 = restorable with this passphrase. (2) `tests/dr_drill.rs` walks the mesh-recovery runbook against the real library surfaces: surviving sealed+armored bundle ‚Üí fresh empty store (the rebuilt box) ‚Üí wrong-passphrase rejected ‚Üí restore lands every CA/peer row (values asserted) ‚Üí post-restore a new single-use enroll bearer mints (43-char base64url contract verified) ‚Üí export-after-restore re-seals + round-trips (the backup chain re-establishes). Plus a tampered-ciphertext rejection test. Both green.
- [‚úì] **EFF-29 ¬∑ PKG ¬∑ Daemon runs as root, no service identity.** ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12, decided + documented + hardened): root is INTENTIONAL ‚Äî mackesd is the node's system-management plane (writes /etc/nebula + /etc/hosts + voice configs, drives firewalld/systemctl/CUPS/sshd/dnf); DynamicUser or a %pre user breaks every one of those paths or re-grants them via a sudo/polkit matrix wider than root. The decision now lives in the unit itself, alongside the containment: `CapabilityBoundingSet=~` drops the never-needed cap classes (module/rawio/boot/time, audit, MAC, suspend/lease/immutable, pacct/tty/ipclock) + ProtectKernelModules/ProtectClock/SystemCallArchitectures=native on top of the EFF-12 set. `systemd-analyze verify` clean (also dropped the removed CPUAccounting option).
- [‚úì] **EFF-30 ¬∑ PKG ¬∑ RPM GPG signing + ISO checksum/signature undefined.** ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12): `install-helpers/sign-release.sh` (operator-gated, invoked from /release, never CI) ‚Äî rpmsign-embeds the project signature into any .rpm argument, then writes `SHA256SUMS` + a detached armored `SHA256SUMS.asc` covering every artifact (the ISO path). Fails early without the secret key. **Smoked end-to-end with the real project key:** checksum validates, `gpg --verify` returns Good signature. Release skill updated to invoke it.
- [‚úì] **EFF-31 ¬∑ CI ¬∑ Coverage gate is advisory (`continue-on-error`).** ‚Äî DONE (2026-06-12): flipped to a HARD gate (removed `continue-on-error`). The denominator is now the meaningful **library-logic** set ‚Äî the 7 iced/libcosmic GUI crates `--exclude`d (render code, correctness via mde-theme tokens + the lifted visual gate, not headless line-coverage) and the binary entrypoints (`src/bin/*.rs`, `src/main.rs` ‚Äî CLI dispatch + daemon bootstrap glue; mackesd.rs alone is ~5.7k integration-level lines) `--ignore-filename-regex`'d. Measured 84.84% lines on that denominator (cargo-llvm-cov 0.8.7) ‚Üí an 80 floor with ~5% margin; mackesd runs `--test-threads=1` (EFF-18 env-race). Floor ratchets up as coverage grows; lowering needs a deliberate edit.

## AUDIT-2026-06-11 ‚Äî fit-for-purpose follow-ups (superseded ‚Äî all closed)

Lifted from the 2026-06-11 `docs/COMPLIANCE.md` sweep ("audit the platform for fit for purpose"). The mesh control plane is solid; these close the data-plane + distribution + guardrail gaps. Finding ids are `AUD-#` ‚Üí COMPLIANCE.md row #. Ordered by impact.

- [‚úì] **AUD-1 ¬∑ Mesh file transfer (Send-To) is a facade ‚Äî wire it end-to-end (FINISH).** The SVC-5 headline capability is dead at every seam: GUI `Message::SendTo`/`DragDrop` reducers discard the request (`mde-files/app.rs:653,642`), no UI calls `Backend::send_to`, `RealBackend::send_to` ‚Üí local ‚Üí `DestinationUnreachable` (`backend.rs:736,583`), the `file-ops/send-to` verb returns `SEND_TO_NOT_CONFIGURED` (`mackesd/ipc/files.rs:185`), and the complete tested `path_safety‚Üípreflight‚Üíorchestrator` engine is orphaned (zero callers). Connect the GUI reducers ‚Üí a real `BusBackend`/`MeshBackend` transfer method ‚Üí the `send-to` verb ‚Üí the orchestrator engine. **Biggest single fit-for-purpose win.**
- [‚úì] **AUD-4 ¬∑ Package the cosmic-applet (FINISH).** The ¬ß5 Cosmic integration binary (`mde-cosmic-applet`) is in no RPM `assets`, no CI, and has no cosmic-panel `.desktop` registration ‚Äî it builds into a void. - [‚úì] **AUD-5 ¬∑ Runtime DISCLAIMER accept gate (FINISH).** ¬ß5 wants a pre-flight accept; today it's build-time non-empty enforcement + a display-only About panel. Add a first-run / install-time "I agree before use" consent path.

- [‚úì] **AUD-2 ¬∑ KDC outbound drainer (FINISH).** `ring`/`sms`/`clipboard`/`share` enqueue to `PendingSends` but nothing drains it; `LanTransport::send_to` is called nowhere ‚Äî so the PD-3 L6 Devices Ring/Send-file + phone hub never reach the device.
