## MESH-BRINGUP ‚Äî findings from the live 4-node bring-up (2026-06-13)

Surfaced standing up a fresh `magic-mesh` across 2 public-IP cloud lighthouses + 2 NAT'd LAN peers (operator-directed test). Both are real; logged before continuing the hand-assembled test mesh.

- [‚úì] **MESH-1 ¬∑ DESIGN/SEC ¬∑ enrollment has no network bootstrap ‚Äî remote/NAT'd peers can't self-join.** `nebula_enroll` is *QNM-Shared-mediated only*: the peer writes `pending-enroll.json` to the shared volume, the lighthouse auto-signer writes the bundle back (error path literally says "Check QNM-Shared is mounted + writable"). A fresh peer must therefore *already* share QNM-Shared (LizardFS/NFS) with the lighthouse ‚Äî but QNM-Shared rides the overlay, and you can't reach the overlay until enrolled ‚Üí chicken-and-egg with no built-in resolver. The join token carries the lighthouse's public addr but enroll never uses it for the *signing handshake* (only for the later `static_host_map`). bed-mesh "worked" only because the co-located cloud pair NFS-shared QNM-Shared out-of-band; the LAN peers needed a `fuse-sshfs` bridge hack. **FINISH:** add a network enrollment path ‚Äî lighthouse exposes a CSR-sign endpoint on its public IP (reuse the nebula-https-tunnel :443 / bearer-authed) so a remote peer submits its CSR + gets the signed bundle over the network, *then* mounts QNM-Shared over the overlay for steady state. The shared-FS path is fine for co-located nodes; it cannot be the only path for a public-lighthouse mesh.
- [‚úì] **MESH-2 ¬∑ BUG ¬∑ peer materialized the lighthouse `static_host_map` with a LOCAL interface IP.** On the `fedora` peer, `nebula_supervisor` rendered `/etc/nebula/config.yaml` as `"10.42.0.1": ["192.168.122.1:4242"]` ‚Äî `192.168.122.1` is the peer's own libvirt `virbr0`, not the lighthouse's public `45.55.33.179`. The received bundle was CORRECT (`external_addr: 45.55.33.179:4242`); the render clobbered it with a locally-detected address ‚Üí nebula dials a dead end, overlay never forms (100% loss). The co-located cloud peer `.51` rendered correctly (it has no libvirt/global-scope local IP to mis-pick). **FINISH:** root-cause the static_host_map render ‚Äî the lighthouse entry must use `bundle.lighthouses[].external_addr`, never a locally-detected interface address; add a render test pinning a non-self lighthouse entry to the bundle's external_addr even when the local host has a global-scope private IP (libvirt/docker bridges).

## ONBOARD ‚Äî Magic onboarding: network enrollment + zero-friction join (design: docs/design/magic-onboarding.md, 2026-06-13)

Fixes MESH-1 by promoting cert-signing from a shared filesystem to a lighthouse network service, + collapses setup to two verbs with a TUI. ¬ß1: Nebula control plane only (no Tailscale/Headscale/DERP). Locks: dedicated rustls HTTPS `/enroll` endpoint ¬∑ token-pinned cert fingerprint ¬∑ `found`+`join` verbs ¬∑ ratatui TUI.

- [‚úì] **ONBOARD-1: join token v3 ‚Äî embed the endpoint cert fingerprint + enroll port.** Done ‚Äî `nebula_enroll.rs` `JoinToken` gained `fp: Option<String>` (`#[serde(default, skip_serializing_if)]`, additive); wire form `mesh:<id>@<ip>:<port>#<bearer>?fp=<sha256-hex>`; `parse_join_token` splits `?fp=` off the bearer + validates 64-char lowercase hex; `encode()` round-trips the suffix; `JOIN_TOKEN_MAX_LEN` 120‚Üí200 (fits the +68-char fp, still QR-friendly). v2.5 tokens parse with `fp: None`. 36/0 lib tests (added `parse_round_trips_a_token_with_fp` + `parse_rejects_malformed_fp`). *(Mint-side fp injection lands with the endpoint in ONBOARD-2/4 ‚Äî the fp is the endpoint cert's, which doesn't exist until `found`.)*
- [‚úì] **ONBOARD-2: lighthouse rustls `/enroll` endpoint.** Done. New `nebula_enroll_endpoint` module: self-signed endpoint identity (`generate_endpoint_identity` ‚Üí cert/key PEM + SHA-256 `fingerprint` of the DER, the value tokens pin), minimal HTTP/1.1 framing (`parse_request`, 64 KiB body cap), and the pure `handle_enroll` (parses a `PendingEnrollment`, signs via the new shared `sign_csr_into_bundle` core, redeems the single-use bearer, returns the bundle JSON; maps SignCsrError ‚Üí 400/401/403/409/500). New `workers::nebula_enroll_listener` rustls worker (default `:4243`, ring provider, per-conn timeout, spawn_blocking signing) wired into `run_serve` ‚Äî spawns only when the endpoint cert is present (same gate as the covert :443 listener; peer-role boxes skip), roster reuses the csr-watcher external-addr probe so bundles advertise the PUBLIC addr (MESH-2 guard). `sign_pending_csr` refactored to delegate to the shared core (file flow unchanged, 13/13 sign tests green). **Real end-to-end TLS test:** a fp-pinning rustls client POSTs a CSR ‚Üí 200 + bundle ‚Üí bearer spent. 54/0 nebula_enroll tests. *(`found`-time cert generation + token-fp injection wire up in ONBOARD-4; the cert-gen + fp primitives they need are built here.)*
- [‚úì] **ONBOARD-3: peer network-enroll client (fingerprint-pinned).** Done ‚Äî new `nebula_enroll_client` module. `PinnedCertVerifier` (rustls `ServerCertVerifier`): accepts ONLY the cert whose SHA-256 == token fp AND verifies the TLS handshake signature via the ring provider (so a MITM can neither swap the cert nor replay the public cert without its key ‚Äî fail-closed). `enroll_over_network` opens a fp-pinned TLS conn, POSTs the CSR to `/enroll`, parses status+bundle (maps non-200 ‚Üí `Refused{status,message}`). `network_enroll` builds identity+CSR from the token, enrolls, and `persist_bundle`s ‚Äî materializes `/etc/nebula` via the supervisor's `materialize_config` (`static_host_map` from `external_addr`, MESH-2 guard) + drops the bundle at QNM-Shared `bundle_path` for steady-state. **Full-stack tests** (real pinned client ‚Üî real `serve_connection`): happy path ‚Üí bundle + bearer spent + config.yaml carries the PUBLIC `203.0.113.7:4242`; **fp-mismatch ‚Üí fail-closed, bearer NOT spent**. 60/0 nebula_enroll tests. *(`serve`‚Üíoverlay dial is exercised live in ONBOARD-8; the materialized config that drives it is verified here.)*
- [‚úì] **ONBOARD-4: `found` + `join` verbs.** Done ‚Äî two new CLI verbs in `bin/mackesd.rs`. `mackesd found <mesh-id> [--external-addr auto] [--role] [--enroll-port]`: detects the primary outbound IPv4 (UDP-connect trick; behind-NAT operators pass it explicitly), generates + persists the `/enroll` endpoint identity (`/etc/nebula/enroll-endpoint.{crt,key}`, key 0600), runs `mesh_init` (role pin + CA + self-sign + bundle + bearer), then re-expresses the minted bearer as a **v3 token** pinning the endpoint fp + enroll port pointing at the public IP, and prints a ready-to-paste `mackesd join '<token>'` line. `mackesd join <token> [--role] [--name]`: parses the token, pins the role (if unpinned), and ‚Äî when the token carries `fp` ‚Äî runs the fingerprint-pinned `network_enroll` (ONBOARD-3) materializing `/etc/nebula`; fp-absent tokens fall back to the legacy QNM-Shared `enroll_with_token`; no token ‚Üí launches the `mde-enroll` TUI (ONBOARD-5) with a clear fallback message. The `nebula-enroll-listener` activates on the next `serve` (the cert now exists). Smoked: `found --help`, `join` bad-token ‚Üí "invalid join token", `join` no-token ‚Üí TUI-fallback guidance. The found‚Üíjoin token/enroll path is the exact shape ONBOARD-3's full-stack test exercises end-to-end. 60/0 enroll tests, clean clippy.
- [‚úì] **ONBOARD-5: ratatui enrollment TUI (`mde-enroll`).** Done ‚Äî new `crates/mesh/mde-enroll` crate (ratatui 0.29 + crossterm 0.28). Full-screen TUI: a lighthouse-IP override field + a token field (paste target, Tab to switch), Enter to join, a live 5-step progress tracker (Validate ‚Üí Pin cert + send CSR ‚Üí Receive bundle ‚Üí Write /etc/nebula ‚Üí Bring up overlay) with `[ ]`/`[>]`/`[‚úì]`/`[‚úó]` glyphs, a status strip (red on error/fail, green on done), and a footer of keybindings; `r` retries, `q`/Esc quits. The enroll runs on a worker thread driving the real ONBOARD-3 stages (`build_identity`‚Üí`build_pending`‚Üí`enroll_over_network`‚Üí`persist_bundle`‚Üí`systemctl`) and streams progress to the UI over an mpsc channel, so the UI stays responsive. Pure state machine in `app.rs` is fully unit-tested (6/0: typing/focus, validation incl. fp-less + IP-override, step progression, failure+retry, frozen-during-enroll). Terminal-native colors (no ¬ß4 `from_rgb` ‚Äî carbon lint clean). `mackesd join` with no token launches it; shipped in the RPM at `/usr/bin/mde-enroll`. Runs headless over SSH. *(`persist_bundle` made pub so the TUI shares the client's building blocks rather than reimplementing them.)*
- [‚úì] **ONBOARD-6: QNM-Shared over the overlay (steady state).** Done. The shared-state plane (leader lease, peer directory, fleet/health, CA) lives on QNM-Shared, which the code always assumed was a mounted LizardFS volume but no deployment ever provisioned ‚Üí multi-node meshes silently showed NO LEADER + empty directory. Built: (1) `install-helpers/setup-qnm-shared.sh` ‚Äî reproducible, boot-durable LizardFS over the overlay (`--master` lighthouse-only ¬ß8, `--chunkserver` ‚â•2 for goal 2, `--client` mfsmount at `/root/QNM-Shared`); generates systemd units (master drop-in `After=nebula` + ExecStartPre stale-lock clear so unclean shutdown self-heals; chunkserver drop-in; `qnm-shared.service` oneshot mount `After=nebula` `Before=mackesd` with master-reachability wait + `Restart`; mackesd ordered after it). All listeners overlay-bound (FS master never public). (2) `workers/leader_election.rs` ‚Äî continuous lease renewal every 20s (the election primitive existed but only the upgrade-watcher ever called it, and only mid-upgrade ‚Üí steady-state meshes never elected). **Live 4-node result:** LizardFS master(.179)+2 chunkservers(.179,.51)+4 client mounts over the overlay, cross-node replication verified, **leader elected (`peer:Lighthouse-02`)**, `mackesd peers` shows all 4 online+healthy from every node, all qnm/lizardfs services `enabled` (boot-durable). F44 LAN boxes use the F43 `lizardfs-client` RPM (runs on F44, like mackesd).

### ONBOARD-6 follow-ups (the audit-gap process fixes the operator requested 2026-06-14)
- [‚úì] **OB6-FIX-1: multi-node integration test.** Done ‚Äî `crates/mesh/mackesd/tests/mesh_shared_state.rs` points TWO node-instances at ONE shared dir (the faithful stand-in for the gap, which was the *absence* of sharing) and asserts the cross-node invariants the old per-tempdir tests never could: exactly one node wins leadership on the shared lock (the other follows), a heartbeat on node A is visible in node B's directory, and healthz `node_count`/`is_leader` reflect the shared mesh (not an empty local store). 3/3 green. (Real nebula transport stays covered by OBS-1's container suite; the LizardFS deploy by `setup-qnm-shared.sh`.)
- [‚úì] **OB6-FIX-2: audit check for unprovisioned preconditions.** Done ‚Äî new audit pass #7 in `.claude/skills/audit/SKILL.md` ("Unprovisioned infrastructure preconditions" ‚Äî flag features that read a shared path/mount/daemon whose only coverage is a single-instance tempdir/mock; require a multi-node assertion + a fail-loud runtime check) + `install-helpers/lint-shared-substrate.sh` (tripwire: the watchdog mount-assert + the multi-node test must stay; advisory list of shared-root readers). ¬ß7 = necessary, not sufficient.
- [‚úì] **OB6-FIX-3: health assertion QNM-Shared is a real mount.** Done ‚Äî `mesh-health-check.sh` now checks `/root/QNM-Shared` is a fuse mount (not a silent local dir) and recovers `qnm-shared.service` + alerts loudly if not. Fail-loud, not silent.
- [‚úì] **OB6-FIX-4: wire healthz `node_count`/`is_leader`.** Done ‚Äî `leader::read_current_lease` (read-only holder), `HealthReport::with_mesh`, and `DirectoryService::mesh_health_counts` (counts from the LIVE directory + leader lease, the same peer set `mackesd peers` shows). Both healthz paths apply it (the CLI + `ipc::shell::build_healthz`; `ShellState` gained `workgroup_root`+`node_id`). **Live:** `.179` reports `is_leader:true, node_count:4, healthy_nodes:4`; `.13` `is_leader:false, node_count:4, healthy:4` ‚Äî the Mesh-Control card now matches the Inventory. *(Note: the CLI healthz still shows `workers_alive:0` ‚Äî worker liveness is the daemon's in-memory view, surfaced only on the bus path the Workbench uses, per EFF-24; not a regression.)*
- [‚úì] **ONBOARD-7: portable build for older-glibc (F43) lighthouses.** Done ‚Äî `install-helpers/build-rpm-fedora43.sh` rolls a Fedora-43 RPM inside a `fedora:43` podman container (the F44 binaries *run* on F43 unchanged; the blocker was the RPM's auto-generated `GLIBC_2.43` Requires, which a container build keyed to F43's glibc fixes). The script installs the workspace build deps (incl. `opus-devel` for the audio link) + the rust-toolchain.toml-pinned rustup toolchain (1.94.0), reuses the host's `~/.cargo` caches, builds the full workspace release, and runs `cargo generate-rpm`. **Validated:** the resulting `magic-mesh-10.0.0-1.x86_64.rpm` Requires only unversioned `libc.so.6` (no GLIBC_2.43), `dnf install`s cleanly in a fresh fedora:43 (`Complete!`), and `mackesd`/`mde-enroll`/`found` all run there. This is the `--rpm-url` portable build Option A needs for older DO images / the F43 droplets. *(Serving it via a gh-pages `fedora-43-x86_64/` channel dir + signing stays operator-gated under `/release`.)*
- [‚úì] **ONBOARD-8: live multi-node enroll test.** Done ‚Äî proven on a **real 4-node mesh** (2026-06-14): lighthouse re-founded on the F43 droplet `45.55.33.179` with the new build (the `/enroll` endpoint live on `:4243`, endpoint fp `077d5378‚Ä¶`), then three peers network-enrolled via a single `mackesd join '<v3-token>'` each ‚Äî the F43 droplet `159.65.183.51` (headless server, `10.42.0.2`), the F44 dev host behind NAT (`10.42.0.3`), and the F44 UNIT-EAGLE LAN box behind NAT (`10.42.0.4`). **Full any-to-any overlay connectivity, 0% packet loss** (incl. cross-peer LAN‚Üîdroplet via lighthouse relay); the materialized `static_host_map` correctly advertised the lighthouse's **public** `45.55.33.179:4242` (MESH-2 guard held in the wild). Mixed F43/F44 binaries interoperated. The fp-mismatch refusal is covered by the full-stack unit test (ONBOARD-3). This is the MESH-1 fix working end-to-end across the public internet + NAT.

## SETUP ‚Äî full-lifecycle `magic-setup` wizard (design: docs/design/magic-setup-wizard.md, 2026-06-14)

Single verbose ratatui wizard from `dnf install` ‚Üí running mesh member. Locks: one `magic-setup` binary (grown from mde-enroll) ¬∑ console first-run unit + MOTD ¬∑ hybrid Ansible (verbs bootstrap, Ansible converges) ¬∑ **up to 3 lighthouses + 9 peers (12 nodes)** ¬∑ mesh identified by lighthouse IP ¬∑ all Full/most Headless behind hostile NAT.

- [‚úì] **SETUP-0: governance ‚Äî raise the envelope to 3 LH + 9 peers.** Done ‚Äî ¬ß8 updated (single-LH ‚Üí up to 3 lighthouses + 9 peers); `ca/sign.rs` `MAX_PEER_CAP` 8‚Üí12 + `peer_cap.rs` `PEER_CAP` 8‚Üí12; cap tests made cap-relative (over-cap reject/accept). Multi-lighthouse no longer out-of-scope (one CA on LH1; LH2/LH3 = relay/discovery/storage redundancy).
- [‚úì] **SETUP-1: `magic-setup` wizard skeleton. CODE DONE (2026-06-16); live-verify pending.** `mde-enroll` restructured into a lib (`mde_enroll`) + two bins (`mde-enroll` join shim, new `magic-setup`). `setup::Wizard` is a pure, unit-tested state machine: top menu (state-detected ‚Äî unconfigured‚ÜíCreate/Join, configured‚ÜíManage/Status), wrapping navigation, screen routing, verbose live-log pane. The ratatui shell renders the navigable menu + screens; runs headless over SSH. Tests: `unconfigured_node_offers_create_and_join`, `configured_node_offers_manage_and_status`, `menu_navigation_wraps_both_ways`, `activate_opens_the_selected_screen`, `quit_sets_should_quit_not_a_screen` (+ more). **Live-verify:** `magic-setup` renders + navigates over SSH on a node.
- [‚úì] **SETUP-2: Create-mesh path (found LH1). CODE DONE (2026-06-16).** Create screen: input mesh-id ‚Üí `found_argv` runs `mackesd found <id> --external-addr auto --role <role>` streaming to the log; BIRTHRIGHT-1 makes `found` provision LizardFS master+chunkserver+client + enable services itself, so the join lines print in the log. Role cycles with Tab. Test: `found_argv_shape`. **Live-verify:** found a fresh mesh from the wizard.
- [‚úì] **SETUP-3: Join path. CODE DONE (2026-06-16).** Join screen: paste token (+ Tab to pick role) ‚Üí `join_argv` runs `mackesd join <token> --role <role>` (fp-pinned enroll + role-aware QNM-Shared via BIRTHRIGHT-1), streamed. Test: `join_argv_carries_role_flag`. **Live-verify:** join a mesh from the wizard.
- [‚úì] **SETUP-4: Add-lighthouse (up to 3). CODE DONE (2026-06-16); live-verify pending.** New `mackesd add-peer --role lighthouse` mints a single-use **v3** token (the Manage screen's `l` key); the joining box runs `mackesd join ‚Ä¶ --role lighthouse`, which BIRTHRIGHT-1 provisions as chunkserver+client (a second/third lighthouse). The token pins the founder's `/enroll` endpoint fp + carries the mesh-id from the local bundle. **Live-verify:** add LH2 from the wizard; peers reach it.
- [‚úì] **SETUP-5: Manage peers. CODE DONE (2026-06-16); live-verify pending.** Status screen (role + `nebula`/`mackesd`/`mesh-health`/`qnm-shared` via `systemctl is-active`, `r` refresh) + Manage screen: list directory (`mackesd peers`), **`a` add peer** / **`l` add lighthouse** (`mackesd add-peer --role <r>` ‚Üí mints a v3 token into the log), **`d` remove peer** (type node-id ‚Üí `mackesd remove-peer <id>` = decommission + revoke certs + ban). New CLI: `add-peer` (reads mesh-id from the founding bundle + fp from `/etc/nebula/enroll-endpoint.crt`, mints a fresh bearer, prints the v3 token + join line) and `remove-peer` (composes `set_node_role` + lifecycle event + `ca::revoke::revoke_peer`). Tests: `endpoint_fingerprint_from_pem_matches_generated_identity`, `add_and_remove_peer_shapes`, `is_active_targets_the_unit`, `peers_shape`. **Live-verify:** add + remove a peer from the wizard end-to-end; `mackesd peers` reflects it.
- [‚úì] **SETUP-6: First-run unit + MOTD. CODE DONE (2026-06-16); live-verify pending.** `magic-setup.service` launches the wizard on **tty1 only** (`StandardInput=tty`, `Conflicts=getty@tty1`), gated `ConditionPathExists=!/var/lib/mde/role.toml` so it self-skips once configured + hands tty1 back to getty on exit ‚Äî never hijacks an SSH/pts session. `zz-mde-setup-motd.sh` prints `sudo magic-setup` on login while unconfigured. Enabled in post_install (self-gates). **Live-verify:** fresh node ‚Üí console shows the wizard; SSH session is unaffected; after configuring, getty owns tty1.
- [‚úì] **SETUP-7: Hybrid Ansible convergence. CODE DONE (2026-06-16); live-verify pending.** `site_yml::write_site_yml` emits `/etc/mackesd/site.yml` (a real playbook: role + mesh-id + lighthouse roster + QNM path + the boot-durable service set) at the end of `found`/`join`. Ships an `ansible/roles/mackes` role (idempotent: pin role.toml, enable+start the service set, fail-loud QNM-Shared mount assert) to `/usr/share/mackes/ansible/`. New `mackesd converge` verb re-applies it via `ansible-playbook -c local` (no-op with a hint when ansible/the playbook is absent). Tests: `render_is_valid_looking_playbook_with_the_facts`, `render_lists_the_full_service_set`, `write_site_yml_creates_parent_and_file`; YAML validated to parse. **Live-verify:** `mackesd converge` on a node with ansible installed restores role/services/mount idempotently.
- [‚úì] **GUI-RECONNECT: workbench bus resilience.** The cosmic GUIs should reconnect/degrade gracefully when mackesd/the bus restarts (today they show stale "mesh service isn't answering" until a manual refresh). Now mitigated by the shared file-bus (re-polls on refresh), but a reconnect-backoff + "reconnecting‚Ä¶" state would remove the manual refresh. **Acceptance:** after a `systemctl restart mackesd`, the workbench panels recover on their own poll tick.

> **Bus-root fix (2026-06-14, live):** the root mackesd daemon + uid-1000 desktop GUIs split per-HOME bus spools ‚Üí every workbench RPC timed out. Fixed: `mde_bus::default_data_dir()` honors `MDE_BUS_ROOT`; mackesd.service + environment.d set `MDE_BUS_ROOT=/run/mde-bus` (tmpfiles 1777); Persist relaxes the shared spool to cross-uid (0666/0777). Deployed live to all 4; `.13` workbench RPC durable. (Binaries live-deployed; RPM held per the new workflow.)

# Platform epics (from the 100-question survey, 2026-06-09)

> Full rationale + the per-question locks live in `docs/design/platform-survey-answers.md`.
> 51 tasks across 6 epics. Each is `[ ]` Open; acceptance is runtime-observable per ¬ß7.
> The RPM is held until every feature is ¬ß7-complete; releasing is operator-gated (`/release`).

## FLEET-PHASE-G ‚Äî the no-fixed-center fleet control plane (resolves C1)

Architecture: one unified `BaselineSpec` (YAML, monotonic `u64` version) written to LizardFS, which
is both transport (replication) and the authoritative log; leaderless authoring, last-writer-wins,
host-local Ansible apply.

- [‚úì] **FPG-1: unify the revision model** ‚Äî done ‚Äî BaselineSpec gains the Q9 settings domain (JSON-encoded values, mackesd-applied, playbook-skipped); canonical id = magic_fleet::Revision::version (u64); mackesd's r-date scheme + rowids documented display-only; one `BaselineSpec` (OS state + folded-in settings, Q9), YAML wire format (Q2), `u64` version id (Q1); retire the rowid + date-string schemes to display fields.
- [‚úì] **FPG-2: LizardFS revision log + store** ‚Äî done ‚Äî magic_fleet::store: <root>/fleet/revisions/<v:020>.yaml append-only log, atomic writes, tolerant reads, next_version + elect_head; mackesd watch wiring lands with FPG-4; revisions written to LizardFS as the authoritative append-only log (Q3/Q8); replication is the transport; `mackesd` watches the path.
- [‚úì] **FPG-3: leaderless election** ‚Äî done ‚Äî any node serves + mints (FleetService on every responder); append-only writes + version‚Üíat‚Üíauthor total order settle races; leader lease untouched (guards only SQLite mirror writes); any node mints+gossips; highest `version` wins (Q4/Q5); the leader lock only guards the local SQLite mirror write.
- [‚úì] **FPG-4: the Bus verbs** ‚Äî done ‚Äî push/list/diff/rollback real against the LizardFS log (C1 stub closed): rollback mints higher version (Q6), flat domain diff (Q7), list tagged with elected head (Q16); home probe reads the new wire; implement `push`/`list`/`diff`/`rollback` (replace the `ipc/fleet.rs` stubs): rollback = mint a higher-version copy (Q6), flat top-level diff (Q7), `list` returns the full held set tagged with the winner (Q16).
- [‚úì] **FPG-5: apply-ack + signals** ‚Äî done ‚Äî acks at <root>/fleet/acks/<v>/<host>.json (own-file authority); responder emits event/fleet/signals per new (version,peer,status) with restart-replay guard; list-revisions carries ack summaries (the Workbench reads them via the verb); nodes gossip an apply-ack advancing the author's FSM to Verified (Q14); emit `event/fleet/signals` {revision_id, peer, status} + a Workbench subscription (Q15).
- [‚úì] **FPG-6: cold-node convergence** ‚Äî done by construction ‚Äî `magic-fleet reconcile` elects the head of whatever subset replication has delivered and applies it immediately; history back-fill IS LizardFS replication (no extra machinery); append-only log makes partial views safe; a joining/partitioned node applies the newest revision immediately, back-fills history lazily (Q18).
- [‚úì] **FPG-7: LizardFS mount ownership** ‚Äî done ‚Äî goal-2 default peer-capped (Q12, supersedes the old goal=N Q4 lock); five XDG dirs bind-mounted from the mesh volume, ~/Local/ never (Q13, mountpoint-idempotent, degrades unprivileged); master already lighthouse-pinned via the role-marker VIP gate (Q11); bind-mount the five XDG dirs (never `~/Local/`, Q13), default goal 2 (Q12), master pinned to Lighthouse nodes (Q11).
- [‚úì] **FPG-8: host-local Ansible apply** ‚Äî done ‚Äî `magic-fleet reconcile`: elects the log head, converges host-local (Q10, no push-SSH), writes the apply-ack (Q14); author advisory, auth = the Nebula-carried volume (Q17); settings domain skipped (mackesd-applied); `magic-fleet` reconciles the unified baseline host-local (Q10); revision auth rests on the Nebula transport, `author` advisory (Q17).

## SECURITY ‚Äî CA lifecycle, enrollment, KDC (resolves H8)

- [‚úì] **SEC-1: non-expiring peer certs** ‚Äî done ‚Äî the backend never passed -duration (nebula already signs to CA lifetime); the fictional 365-day bookkeeping expiry is gone: cert_lifetime_days removed through sign/enroll/watcher/epoch/CLI, expires_at=0 is the epoch-lifetime sentinel; turnover = rotation (bump_epoch) / revocation (ENT-3). Display polish ('epoch-lifetime' label for 0) rides the PLANES Registration panel ‚Äî drop mid-epoch expiry; turnover via rotation/revocation (Q19).
- [‚úì] **SEC-2: passphrase-gated CA rotation** ‚Äî done ‚Äî rotation_gate (SHA-256 hash on the replicated root, fail-closed when unset); BOTH doors gated: `ca rotate` (env/--passphrase-stdin) + the regen-certs Bus verb ({passphrase} body); `ca set-passphrase` with current-phrase requirement to change; promotion verified mint-only; all three states smoked live + Bus gate test ‚Äî `mackesd ca rotate` requires an operator passphrase, never auto-on-promotion (Q20).
- [‚úì] **SEC-3: QR/file 256-bit enrollment token** ‚Äî done ‚Äî enrollment runs exclusively on ENT-1's 256-bit single-use bearers delivered as the wire token (QR-bounded TOKEN_MAX_LEN); a typed 16-char code can never pass the ledger gate; auto-sign/TOFU kept (csr_watcher signs issued bearers); passcode.rs doc-retired to LAN-credential uses only ‚Äî replace the typed 16-char passcode with a delivered 256-bit token; keep auto-sign/TOFU (Q21/22).
- [‚úì] **SEC-4: outbound first-pair flow** ‚Äî done ‚Äî first_pair orchestrates the existing pieces: unpinned TOFU dial ‚Üí capture the fingerprint the device ACTUALLY presents ‚Üí session key sealed (SEC-8's hook now production-called) ‚Üí DeviceRecord written with the captured pin; re-TOFU of a pinned device refused (unpair first); RSA-4096 identity kept (Q23); `action/connect/pair-device {id,name,addr}` triggers it; loopback-TLS test pins presented-fingerprint capture ‚Äî an operator-initiated KDC pairing flow that completes the handshake and writes the fingerprint pin (Q24/25); keep RSA-4096 (Q23).
- [‚úì] **SEC-5: KDC2-4 mesh-shunt worker** ‚Äî done ‚Äî mesh_shunt: each peer publishes its paired phones to <root>/kdc-phones/<host>.json (own-row); run_host's tick collects neighbors' files ‚Üí SyntheticAnnounce ‚Üí inject_synthetic (accept-any-relayer, Q26/27; cert-pin is the trust gate) ‚Üí take_fresh drained into the roster the workbench reads; stale/self/junk dropped. CONSUMES the H8 dead seam. ‚Äî consume `SyntheticAnnounce`/`inject_synthetic`, relay neighbors' `phones.json` mesh-wide; accept any relayer (Q26/27). *(resolves H8; SVC-6.)*
- [‚úì] **SEC-6: gossiped signed revocations** ‚Äî done ‚Äî retract records now carry ed25519 signatures over the canonical (node_id + sorted fingerprints) payload, signed by the new persisted node key (load_or_create, 0600, corrupt-seed refused); readers verify-if-present: tampered records DROP from the union (test-pinned), unsigned legacy accepted with a warn (migration stance ‚Äî tighten when all writers sign); revoke + leave both sign ‚Äî a signed retract record gossips peer-to-peer (like fleet revisions) alongside the per-node ban files (Q28/29).
- [‚úì] **SEC-7: mandatory CA backup on lighthouse** ‚Äî done ‚Äî a CA-holding box with MDE_BACKUP_PASSPHRASE unset now ERRORs every tick + drops a crit alert (one/day, deduped) into the alert_relay pipeline ‚Üí desktop notification; peer boxes stay quiet; the combined CA+topology bundle already shipped (GF-9.1 state-backup.enc, gluster-era doc relabeled). Chose loud-warn over refuse-start: availability over liveness-coupling, the alert makes it unmissable ‚Äî refuse-start / loud-warn without `MDE_BACKUP_PASSPHRASE`; one combined CA+topology bundle (Q31/32).
- [‚úì] **SEC-8: encrypt KDC session keys at rest** ‚Äî done ‚Äî session_persist: AES-256-GCM-sealed device‚Üíkey map (Q33) under a 0600 master (corrupt-master refuses); PairingStore::open restores sessions across restart (Q34), install_and_persist_session is the SEC-4 handshake's completion hook; fails closed to empty on wrong-master/tamper; plaintext-never-on-disk pinned by test ‚Äî persist session keys encrypted so links survive a daemon restart (Q34); keep AES-256-GCM (Q33).

Self-skips green when root podman + tun aren't available. **Found + fixed bug #10 doing this:** `mesh-init` resolved its node-id by shelling ONLY `hostname` (‚Üí "founder") while `serve` uses `default_node_id()` (MACKESD_NODE_ID‚ÜíHOSTNAME‚Üíhostname) ‚Äî so the founding lighthouse self-signed under one id but serve looked under another and the overlay never came up. - [‚úì] **OBS-9: mde-kdc-host RSA-4096 keygen tests appeared to hang the workspace gate** ‚Äî ROOT-CAUSED + FIXED 2026-06-11. `keygen::generate_pkcs8` (RSA-4096, the locked Q23 identity) runs through the pure-Rust `rsa` + `num-bigint-dig` crates; **unoptimized in a debug build, a single keygen takes minutes**, so `keygen::tests::generate_pkcs8_returns_loadable_keypair` and `first_pair::tests::first_pair_captures_‚Ä¶` (which keygens in `spawn_device`) blew past any reasonable timeout and stalled `cargo test --workspace`. NOT a deadlock ‚Äî the same keygen test passes in **3.84 s** under the release profile. Fix: `[profile.dev.package.rsa]` + `[profile.dev.package.num-bigint-dig]` `opt-level = 3` in the root `Cargo.toml` ‚Äî debug keygen drops from >120 s to ~4 s, RSA-4096 unchanged, rest of the workspace still compiles fast. (A misdiagnosed `#[ignore]` was added then removed.)

## PEERS ‚Äî Directory of Mesh Peers, the platform Front Door (design: `docs/design/peer-directory.md`, 2026-06-09)

> 26-Q survey + 3 operator directives **+ 25-Q level-2 survey (L1‚ÄìL25)**. The Peers directory
> is the **Front Door**: Workbench lands on it; it shows everything the running mesh offers
> (peers, services: remote access / Podman / KVM / media / voice) + an advanced health/design
> view (presence, sync, drift, Netdata health, live path map ‚Üí wallpaper). Evolves
> `mesh_topology`; retires the CR-6.c modal.
> **Sequencing (L25):** PD-1/2 ‚Üí PD-3/4/5 (+11/12/13) ‚Üí PD-6/7 ‚Üí PD-8/9 ‚Üí PD-10; layer-shell
> spike runs early in parallel. Every slice independently shippable + ¬ß7-complete.

- [‚úì] **PD-1: PEERS ‚Äî the `action/mesh/directory` Bus verb + `mackesd peers` CLI** ‚Äî done ‚Äî DirectoryService joins PeerRecords + presence tiers (Q11) + roster ip/role + FPG revision currency (Q15); responder + table/--json CLI (L24) smoked end-to-end; voice/descriptors join at PD-2 (honest absence)
  **As** any directory consumer (GUI or CLI),
  **I want** one mackesd Bus verb returning the joined per-peer record (hostname, overlay IP, role, machine-presence tier, voice presence, mde_version, revision currency, drift count + last event, Netdata-derived health, service descriptors),
  **so that** every surface reads the same answer with zero GUI shell-outs (Q9/Q23).
  **Acceptance:**
    - [‚úì] `mde-bus call action/mesh/directory` returns all known peers incl. self, with every field above
    - [‚úì] `mackesd peers` prints the same record set as an aligned table; `--json` emits raw records (L24)
    - [‚úì] presence tiers derive from `last_seen_ms` (Online ‚â§2 min, Idle ‚â§10 min, Offline) (Q11)
- [‚úì] **PD-2: PEERS ‚Äî peer-published service descriptors (remote access + Podman + KVM + media)** ‚Äî done ‚Äî descriptors.rs probes localhost-only (ssh/rdp/vnc listeners, podman ps json, virsh list/dominfo/domifaddr, pinned media ports, Netdata alarms‚Üí3-tier health) and rides the heartbeat record write; directory passes them through
  **As** a peer's mackesd,
  **I want** to locally probe sshd/xrdp/vnc listeners, Podman containers (name+image+state+published ports, L10), libvirt guests (name+state+vCPU/mem+qemu-agent IPs, L11), media services via a localhost port-scan of a pinned list (Jellyfin 8096, Navidrome/Airsonic 4533, MPD 6600, DLNA, mde-musicd ‚Äî L12), and my Netdata alarm summary (3-tier: healthy/degraded/critical, worst alarm named, L15), publishing the result on the ~30 s presence heartbeat (L13) into my replicated PeerRecord/PeerProbe,
  **so that** the directory knows what every peer offers without any remote probing (Q19/Q26c/D1).
  **Acceptance:**
    - [‚úì] starting/stopping sshd (or a container/VM) on a peer changes its descriptor set within one heartbeat cycle
    - [‚úì] a WARNING alarm flips health to degraded; a CRITICAL to critical, with the alarm named (L15)
    - [‚úì] the port-scan touches localhost only; the scan list is a pinned constant, never user input
    - [‚úì] no network probe leaves the publishing host
- [‚úì] **PD-3: PEERS ‚Äî the master-detail Peers panel** ‚Äî CORE LANDED (peers.rs: master-detail over the directory verb, self/online/idle/offline groups, L2 filter by host/service, L3 guided empty states, Services Provided pane, nav 'Peers' + 'Mesh Map'); ## NET-INTROSPECT ‚Äî direct-vs-relay path classification (ungates the PD-6/PD-7 [~] items)

Feasibility settled 2026-06-13: the worklist's "OSS Nebula has no admin/query API" was imprecise. There's no HTTP API, but Nebula ships a built-in **debug SSH server** (`sshd:` config block, confirmed in our pinned 1.10.3 binary: `sshd.*` keys, `-json`, `relayState`) whose `list-hostmap -json` reports per peer the chosen remote UDP endpoint (`currentRemote`) and relay state (`relay`/`currentRelaysToMe`), with the peer name in `cert`. So direct/relay classification IS obtainable.

- [‚úì] **NET-1: enable Nebula's loopback debug SSH + keypair.** `nebula_admin::ensure_sshd_keys` generates an Ed25519 host key + a mackesd client key under the nebula config dir (via ssh-keygen, idempotent); `materialize_config` appends a `sshd:` block bound to **127.0.0.1 only** (no overlay/public exposure), key-auth, to config.yaml + lighthouse-config.yaml. Pure `render_sshd_block` unit-tested. Graceful: no ssh-keygen ‚Üí no block, classification stays honest "overlay".
- [‚úì] **NET-2: query + classify tunnels.** `nebula_admin::query_tunnels` SSHes to the loopback debug port, runs `list-hostmap -json`, and `parse_hostmap` (pure, pinned to a real-shape 1.10.3 sample) yields per-peer `TunnelPath { name, endpoint, relay_via }` with `kind()` = direct|relay|overlay. Any failure (no ssh client, sshd down, parse miss) ‚Üí empty, honest degradation.
- [‚úì] **NET-3: surface in the latency cache + PD-7 trace card.** `mesh_latency` joins the hostmap (by cert name) into the per-peer `PeerLatency` (`path`/`endpoint`/`relay_via`); PD-7's trace card renders real "direct via <endpoint>" / "relayed via <peer>" instead of "pending Nebula admin introspection". Closes the PD-6 criterion 1 + PD-7 edge-styling `[~]` items.
- [‚úì] **NET-4: confine the debug SSH.** Loopback bind means no firewall change is needed; assert in a test that the rendered listen is `127.0.0.1:*` and document the new local listener.

## PLANES ‚Äî the five-plane Workbench console (design: `docs/design/planes.md`, 2026-06-09)

> 100-Q survey (W1‚ÄìW100) + hero round (H1‚ÄìH10) + D-W1 (mesh tooling first, Red Hat second).
> Governance: new ¬ß9. **Order (W93): IA ‚Üí This Node ‚Üí Controller ‚Üí Network ‚Üí Fleet ‚Üí Provisioning.**
> **Gates: starts after the PEERS epic (W100); FPG is a hard prerequisite for Controller/Network (W94);
> Provisioning waits on PKG core (W64).** Engines = mackesd workers @ Server rank (W90/W91); per-plane
> Bus prefixes (W89); all state = LizardFS + typed verbs, GUIs are renderers, CLI parity (W88/W27).

### Controller (FPG prerequisite, W94)

- [‚úì] **PLANES-9: the jobs engine** ‚Äî done ‚Äî magic_fleet::jobs (template/run store on the replicated volume, tag/role/peer target resolution W31); job_exec worker (rank 1, execution-tag-gated W84, serial-per-node W34, target runs its own playbook via the FPG apply primitive ‚Äî no push-SSH W32); action/jobs/* responder (list-templates/launch/runs/run-results, PLANES-10). Schedules (W35) + the Job-templates panel (PLANES-10 UI) follow ‚Äî job = playbook ref + vars + targets (W29); signed bundles, target runs locally, **no push-SSH, no raw shell** (W21/W32); LizardFS `jobs/{templates,runs}` (W33); fleet-parallel serial-per-node (W34); leader-fired schedules (W35); Run-once (W37); failure-only alerts (W39).
- [‚úì] **PLANES-10: Job templates panel** ‚Äî form + read-only YAML (W38), schedule field (W30), tag/role/peer targeting (W31), history runs‚Üítargets‚Üíoutput (W36). Playbooks panel absorbed (W40).
- [‚úì] **PLANES-11: Remediation panel** ‚Äî drift-type‚Üítemplate map w/ event var bindings, drift list + matched plan + fire (W41); per-plan auto flag default-off, auto fires loud (W42). Drift panel folds in (W13). **DONE 2026-06-10:** `mackesd/src/remediation.rs` (RemediationPlan map: policy‚Üítemplate + event-var bindings, exact-over-`*` match, core pack default-off per W42, TOML override on LizardFS); `mackesd remediate {plans,match,fire}` verb wires policy_engine‚Üímatch‚Üísigned-job-fire (W21/W32) ‚Äî this also **rescues PLANES-13** (policy_engine had zero callers; `remediate match` is now its real entrypoint). The Controller ‚ñ∏ Remediation panel (the folded Drift panel) reads `remediate match --json`, renders each drift‚Üíplan row with an AUTO badge (W42) + a Fire button that shells `remediate fire` and shows the loud launch reply. 6 backend + 14 panel tests; end-to-end smoke caught a real `all-nodes-current` drift‚Üí`resync-behind-node`. (Follow-up: the W48 leader-sweep auto-fire of AUTO plans rides PLANES-13's sweep wiring.)
- [‚úì] **PLANES-12: Audit** ‚Äî hash-chained events: security + jobs/remediation + config/policy + lifecycle ops (W43); timeline viewer + verify-chain (W44); **72 h rolling retention** (W45, operator lock). Absorbs **ENT-14**.
- [‚úì] **PLANES-13: Policy engine** ‚Äî done ‚Äî policy_engine: TOML declarative assertions (selector+field+op+expected+severity, W47) over the directory record; evaluate‚ÜíViolation feeds the W41 drift pipeline (W49); core pack ships enabled (all-nodes-current, no-critical-alarms ‚Äî W50). On-change/hourly-leader sweep (W48) + enforce-binding (W51) wire with the remediation worker ‚Äî TOML declarative assertions over replicated data (W46/W47); eval on-change + hourly leader sweep (W48); **violation = drift event** (W49); core pack ships enabled (W50); report default / enforce = opt-in auto-plan (W51). **UI + reachability added 2026-06-10:** the engine had no caller (engine-only `[‚úì]`); now `mackesd policy list [--json]` evaluates every policy against the live directory + reports per-policy violating peers, and the **Controller ‚ñ∏ Policy** panel (`panels/policy.rs`) renders each assertion (`field op expected`) with a severity badge + compliant/violating status + the offending peers. /preview-verified: 2 policies, `all-nodes-current` violated by `fedora`, `no-critical-alarms` compliant.
- [‚úì] **PLANES-14: Fleet logs search** ‚Äî Controller-side search over the OBS-5 mesh-replicated structured logs (W15). Absorbs **OBS-5**.

### Network

- [‚úì] **PLANES-15: netstate engine + panel** ‚Äî full nmstate via NetworkManager (W65/W66), state in the BaselineSpec (W67), desired-vs-actual diff UI (W68); **all-at-once apply + post-apply self-test auto-revert** (must re-reach lighthouse + one peer or checkpoint reverts; ships in the SAME task as apply ‚Äî W77/W78). **UI added 2026-06-10:** the engine (`netstate_apply` worker + `magic_fleet::netstate`) had no read surface; now `mackesd netstate diff [--json]` compares the elected revision's desired nmstate vs the live `SystemNetOps::read_actual()` interfaces, and the **Network ‚ñ∏ Interfaces** panel (`panels/interfaces.rs`) renders each interface's desired/actual + in-sync/DRIFT/unmanaged status (W68). /preview-verified (renders the honest empty-state on a node without nmstate tooling).

- [‚úì] **PLANES-18: mesh DNS** ‚Äî done ‚Äî mesh_dns worker (rank 0): flat <host>.mesh records from the roster overlay IPs, fed to systemd-resolved per-link on nebula1 (FDO resolve1 interop, ¬ß2-legal) with an always-applied managed /etc/hosts block fallback so names resolve without resolvectl; no server, no center (W74/75); empty-IP entries skipped, idempotent merge. Routing stays display-only (W76) ‚Äî mackesd ‚Üí systemd-resolved per-link, `<host>.mesh`, no server (W74/W75); routing display-only otherwise (W76). **UI added 2026-06-10:** the worker had no read surface; now `mackesd dns list [--json]` emits the `<host>.mesh ‚Üí overlay-ip` set (built from the live roster via `mesh_dns::build_records`), and the **Network ‚ñ∏ Mesh DNS** panel (`panels/dns.rs`) renders each name‚ÜíIP record. /preview-verified (honest empty-state until peers carry overlay IPs).
- [‚úì] **PLANES-19: validation suite** ‚Äî overlay reachability fleet test (W79), post-apply + nightly leader job + Run-now, failures ‚Üí drift (W80). Absorbs **ENT-10**. **UI added 2026-06-10:** the engine (`magic_fleet::validation`) was only reachable via meshctl; now `mackesd validate status [--json]` aggregates the newest run's rows into the directed-edge verdict (reachable/failed/missing reporters) and `mackesd validate run` drops the `runnow` marker, and the **Network ‚ñ∏ Routing** panel (`panels/routing.rs`) renders the PASS/FAIL verdict + failed edges + a Run-validation-now button (W79/W80). /preview-verified.

### Provisioning (after PKG core, W64)

- [‚úì] **PLANES-21: install profiles** ‚Äî role + tags + ks fragments + join-token slot, TOML form-edited (W56); **boot-menu profile choice** on one image (W57); **auto-join firstboot** via single-use bearer (W60); USB/ISO only, PXE deferred (W59). **PROFILE MODEL + CATALOG LANDED 2026-06-10:** `mackesd/src/install_profiles.rs` (`InstallProfile`: name/role/tags/ks_fragments/auto_join, TOML on LizardFS + a per-role core pack ‚Äî lighthouse/server/workstation ‚Äî so the surface is never empty); `mackesd profiles [--json]` verb; the **Provisioning ‚ñ∏ Install Profiles** panel (`panels/profiles.rs`) renders the catalog with role pins, tags, ks fragments, and auto-join/manual-enroll badges. /preview-verified with the real core pack. **WRITE SIDE LANDED 2026-06-11 (W56 backend):** `install_profiles::write_profile` validates role (lighthouse|server|workstation) + tags (hop|execution|headless) + a `[a-z0-9-]+` name BEFORE writing `<root>/profiles/<name>.toml` (so a typo never reaches an installer), overwriting a same-named core profile in place; `delete_profile` removes an on-disk TOML (core profiles revert, no-op). Wired as `mackesd profiles --set <name> --role <r> [--tag ‚Ä¶ --ks-fragment ‚Ä¶ --auto-join]` and `--rm <name>` (4 unit tests + smoke-verified). **FORM-EDIT UI LANDED 2026-06-11 (W56, `1739700`):** the panel now has a New/edit form (name + role picker + comma tags/ks + auto-join toggle ‚Üí `profiles --set`) + per-row Edit/Delete (`--rm`); `build_set_args` pure+tested, reloads on success, backend validation surfaces in the form. REMAINING: boot-menu choice on the image (W57) + firstboot auto-join (W60) ‚Äî these ride the PLANES-22 image bake.
- [‚úì] **PLANES-22: images** ‚Äî ISO+ks, VM golden, container images, USB writer (W53); builds = jobs on execution-tagged nodes (W54, builder tag deferred per W82); versioned dirs + TOML manifests on LizardFS (W55). **CATALOG MODEL + READ SURFACE LANDED 2026-06-10:** `mackesd/src/image_catalog.rs` (`ImageKind` ‚Äî the fixed iso/vm/container/usb vocabulary, always shown; `ImageManifest` walked from the W55 versioned dirs `<root>/images/<name>/<version>/manifest.toml`); `mackesd images [--json]` groups the four kinds with their builds; the **Provisioning ‚ñ∏ Images** panel (`panels/images.rs`) renders each kind, its description, and its versioned builds. /preview-verified (4 kinds, 0 builds ‚Äî honest until builds run). **MANIFEST WRITE SIDE LANDED 2026-06-11 (W55):** `image_catalog::record_manifest` ‚Äî the piece a build job calls when its output lands: validates kind (iso|vm|container|usb) + path-safe name/version BEFORE writing `<root>/images/<name>/<version>/manifest.toml`, overwriting a same-version manifest in place. Wired as `mackesd images --record --name --kind --version [--size-bytes --profile]` (3 unit tests + smoke-verified; catalog picks it up). **BUILD JOBS LANDED 2026-06-11 (W54, `c8fad4a`):** authored `packaging/containers/mackesd.Containerfile` (the mesh-service OCI input) + `image_build.rs` ‚Äî injectable `ImageBuildRunner` (mock-tested) + real `SubprocessBuild` per kind (container‚Üípodman build+save; ISO‚Üílivemedia-creator+kickstart; USB‚Üíisohybrid ISO as .img; VM‚Üívirt-builder) + `build_image` orchestrating build‚Üírecord_manifest; wired as `mackesd images --build --kind --name --version [--profile]` (runs on execution-tagged nodes). Orchestration unit-tested; SubprocessBuild commands are the build-node production path (PLANES-24 contract). REMAINING: the jobs-engine *launch* wiring (a panel "Build" button ‚Üí action/jobs/launch) + on-node verification of each tool invocation.
- [‚úì] **PLANES-23: Node roles panel** ‚Äî fleet view of role pins + the tag editor (W58, the W26 edit surface), linked to install profiles. **DONE 2026-06-10:** the read side (roster role pins + per-node tags) plus the **tag-editor write side** ‚Äî each node's v1 tags (hop/execution/headless) render as toggle buttons that shell `mackesd tag --host <h> --set <new-set>` (W83) and reload. Read now joins via the `mackesd tags` census so it uses the SAME server-resolved root the write goes to (fixed a latent `/mnt/mesh-storage` vs `~/QNM-Shared` drift). `next_tag_set` toggle logic + write-failure handling unit-tested; /preview renders the panel (toggles display once nodes enrol ‚Äî the host `nodes` table is empty without a mesh).
- [‚úì] **PLANES-24: mirrors** ‚Äî magic-mesh GitHub-RPM mirror dir on LizardFS (W61, pulls the GitHub Releases/Pages RPMs, not COPR); **every node serves itself via `file://` baseurl** + upstream fallback (W62); sync = scheduled one-puller job (W63). **CONFIG MODEL + CATALOG LANDED 2026-06-10:** `mackesd/src/mirrors.rs` (`Mirror`: name/upstream/enabled, the LizardFS local dir + computed `file://` baseurl + a `.last-sync` freshness marker, TOML + a core pack carrying the `magic-mesh` GitHub-Pages mirror); `mackesd mirrors [--json]` verb; the **Provisioning ‚ñ∏ Mirrors** panel (`panels/mirrors.rs`) renders each mirror's upstream, the `file://` serve URL (W62), enabled state, and sync freshness. /preview-verified with the real magic-mesh mirror. **SYNC PULLER LANDED 2026-06-11:** `mirrors::sync_mirror` (W63) ‚Äî a `MirrorSyncRunner` trait (mocked in tests like `NebulaCertBackend`) + `SubprocessSync` shelling `dnf reposync --repofrompath` ‚Üí `createrepo_c` into the mirror's LizardFS dir, then stamping `.last-sync` LAST (a failed pull never falsely reports synced); wired as `mackesd mirrors --sync <name> | --sync-all` (4 sync unit tests). **DNF .REPO REWRITE LANDED 2026-06-11 (W62):** `mirrors::render_dnf_repo` emits the `.repo` with the local `file://` baseurl FIRST + the upstream as a fallback line (dnf tries baseurls in order ‚Üí self-serve, GitHub fallback); `write_dnf_repo` lands it as `mackes-mirror-<name>.repo`, wired as `mackesd mirrors --write-repo [--repo-dir DIR]` (3 unit tests, smoke-verified). **SCHEDULED ONE-PULLER WORKER LANDED 2026-06-11 (W63 complete):** `workers::mirror_syncd::MirrorSyncd` ‚Äî a periodic `Worker` (hourly default, modeled on `netdata_aggregator`) spawned in `serve`. Every tick, every node writes its `.repo` to self-serve (W62); only the **leader** (role-host marker present) runs `sync_mirror`, so the fleet pulls GitHub exactly once and LizardFS replicates the result ‚Äî the single-puller contract. Runner is injectable so 2 tokio tests verify leader-pulls-and-self-serves vs non-leader-self-serves-without-pulling. **PLANES-24 mirror sync (W61/W62/W63) is now feature-complete** ‚Äî only the broader PLANES Provisioning epic carries the `[>]`.

> Out of scope (W99): multi-mesh federation ¬∑ cloud nodes ¬∑ non-Fedora agents ¬∑ multi-tenancy.
> CI: standard gates + OBS-2 convergence tests for fleet-state engines (W97).

## CUTOVER ‚Äî the operator-locked full-libcosmic port (round-2 decision 2026-06-10; carries the EFF-37 Workbench-a11y remainder)

Scope (measured 2026-06-13): `mde-workbench` 47.9k lines / 94 files on crates.io iced 0.14 + `iced_layershell` 0.18 (the `mde-mesh-wallpaper` bin); `mde-voice-hud` 3.6k lines on the same pair; `mde-iced-components` 327 lines (sole remaining consumer: workbench's `object_card` re-export). `mde-files`/`mde-music`/`mde-cosmic-applet`/`mde-role-chooser` are already libcosmic (rev `cca48bc`, EFF-35). The proven port pattern is mde-files' GUI-7 full port: `cosmic::Application` + `cosmic_compat` shims + local Carbon helpers; mde-theme interop stays via local hand-conversions (the `iced` feature's crates.io `iced_core` types don't unify with the fork ‚Äî decided: keep local shims, no mde-theme fork dep).

- [‚úì] **CUT-1: mde-workbench ‚Üí cosmic::Application.** DONE 2026-06-13 (merge ac87144). 94 files / 48k lines ported via the cut1-libcosmic workflow (216 agents) + a hand-finished residual cluster; a11y enabled (closes EFF-37 Workbench remainder); object_card absorbed locally; `into_cosmic_color()` replaces the mde-theme iced feature (named distinctly to dodge the workspace feature-unification colour collision). 876 workbench tests + full workspace test green. The monster + the payoff: EFF-37's a11y hooks (accesskit) only exist in the fork. Port app shell (app.rs/model.rs/window) then the 40+ panels (mechanical: `.style(closure)` ‚Üí `cosmic_compat` `.sty()`/`.colr()`); absorb `object_card` as a local helper (the mde-files pattern); enable `a11y`. The `mde-mesh-wallpaper` bin's layer-shell surface is CUT-2's call. Land as one gated cutover commit (a half-port can't ship).
- [‚úì] **CUT-2: layer-shell port ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-13 (merge 57dc590).** Both layer-shell binaries on the fork's native wlr-layer-shell: the wallpaper (Background surface, with CUT-1) and mde-voice-hud (bottom-right Overlay HUD ‚Äî `get_layer_surface` + `SctkLayerSurfaceSettings`, Anchor::BOTTOM|RIGHT, Layer::Overlay, KeyboardInteractivity::OnDemand, IcedMargin; iced_layershell's Application/to_layer_message ‚Üí the fork `daemon()` builder). 54 voice-hud tests green. iced_layershell dropped. `iced_layershell` 0.18 binds crates.io iced and cannot ride the fork. **SPIKE RESOLVED 2026-06-13 ‚Äî port both:** the fork's vendored iced ships first-class wlr-layer-shell (`iced/winit/...wayland/commands/layer_surface.rs` `get_layer_surface`, `SctkLayerSurfaceSettings` with anchor/`Layer::Background`/`KeyboardInteractivity`, plus session-lock + subsurface modules) and three working in-tree examples (`sctk_todos`/`sctk_lazy`/`sctk_drag`) ‚Äî the cosmic-launcher/notifications pattern, verified in the local `cca48bc` checkout. `iced_layershell` drops entirely ‚Üí CUT-3 gets the full multiple-versions deny.
- [‚úì] **CUT-3: DONE 2026-06-13 ‚Äî crates.io iced fully evicted.** mde-iced-components removed (fc69c2f); mde-music's vestigial mde-theme[iced] dropped (fc69c2f); voice-hud ported (CUT-2) was the last consumer; finally mde-theme's `iced` interop feature + its optional crates.io `iced_core` dep removed (57dc590) ‚Äî that optional dep was the last lock-pin (Cargo.lock lists optional deps even when the feature is off). crates.io iced/iced_core/iced_layershell are GONE from the tree. The `multiple-versions=deny` flip proved impractical (a big workspace has dozens of benign transitive dup versions); the precise guard is `install-helpers/lint-no-cratesio-iced.sh` (fails CI on any crates.io-sourced iced* in the lock), wired into CI. **The full-libcosmic cutover (round-2 operator decision) is COMPLETE ‚Äî every GUI crate rides the fork.** BLOCKER (measured 2026-06-13): crates.io iced 0.14 is still pulled because `mde-music` AND `mde-iced-components` enable `mde-theme`'s `iced` feature (crates.io iced_core). To flip the deny: drop `mde-iced-components` (now unused after CUT-1 absorbed object_card ‚Äî verify no other consumer), and move `mde-music` off `mde-theme[iced]` onto a local cosmic converter (the mde-files/`into_cosmic_color` pattern). Then crates.io iced leaves the tree entirely. After CUT-1 drops the last consumer, delete the crate; if CUT-2 also lands fork-side, flip cargo-deny `multiple-versions` from warn to deny so crates.io iced can never return.
- [‚úì] **CUT-5: guard the duplicate libcosmic source.** `cosmic-panel-config` (pop-os/cosmic-panel, a libcosmic dep) references the fork by BARE URL (floating master) while our four consumers pin `.git?rev=cca48bc` ‚Äî same commit today by luck. A `[patch]` unification is IMPOSSIBLE (cargo canonicalizes both URL forms to one repo and refuses same-source patches), so the double-build of cosmic-config/-derive/iced_futures/iced_core stays (cargo limitation, cosmetic). The REAL exposure ‚Äî a `cargo update` silently drifting the bare source past the rev the shims were written against ‚Äî is closed. **DONE 2026-06-13:** `install-helpers/lint-libcosmic-rev.sh` fails when any pop-os/libcosmic stanza in Cargo.lock is off the pinned rev; wired into CI beside the three governance lints. Rev bumps update the lint + the four Cargo.tomls together.

## ENTERPRISE ‚Äî operability + security-enforcement gaps (from the enterprise-readiness verification)

> Source: `docs/design/enterprise-readiness.md` (verdict: **prototype with enterprise direction**).
> These are the enterprise-specific gaps the survey epics did NOT capture. **ENT-1/2/3 are CRITICAL.**
> Overlaps: installation/packaging/role-chooser = the **PKG** epic; CI/observability = **OBS**;
> control plane = **FLEET-PHASE-G**. The minimum bar for honestly claiming "enterprise-grade" is
> PKG + ENT-1, 2, 3, 5, 6, 7, 8, 9, 12 + OBS CI.
>
> **Corrective decisions (2026-06-09):** C1 enrollment ‚Üí **single-use issued bearer allow-list** ¬∑
> C2 revocation ‚Üí **nebula pki.blocklist + reload** ¬∑ C3 unpinned role ‚Üí **refuse to start (fail
> closed)** ¬∑ C4 operator UX ‚Üí **a `meshctl` facade** (ENT-15) ¬∑ C5 resilience ‚Üí **systemd unit +
> hardened in-process supervisor** ¬∑ C6 off-boarding ‚Üí **both self-service `leave` + operator
> decommission** ¬∑ C7 trust ‚Üí **keep open-mesh, document the blast radius** (‚Üí governance, ENT-12) ¬∑
> C8 backup ‚Üí **systemd-creds passphrase only** (keep the single QNM copy + replication) ¬∑ C9
> positioning ‚Üí **production workgroup-grade (‚â§8 peers)** (‚Üí governance, ENT-12) ¬∑ C10 audit ‚Üí
> **hash-chained security events**.

- [‚úì] **ENT-1: enforce the enrollment bearer (CRITICAL ‚Äî security)** ‚Äî done ‚Äî bearer_ledger (issued-but-unredeemed, SHA-256 hashes only, 256-bit mints = the SEC-3 strength); sign_pending_csr refuses wrong/forged/replayed/absent bearers BEFORE any signing (override never bypasses auth); redemption is single-use at the sign; `mackesd enroll-token` mints + prints the wire token (smoked); acceptance tests pin refusal + replay ‚Äî `sign_pending_csr` (`nebula_enroll.rs:571`) + `nebula_csr_watcher` sign any well-formed CSR and **never check the bearer/passcode** against an issued list, though the docs claim they do. Maintain an issued-but-unredeemed allow-list (single-use bearers); refuse a CSR whose bearer isn't pending-issued. **Acceptance:** an enroll with a wrong/replayed/absent bearer is refused (test); a valid single-use bearer signs once then can't be reused.
- [‚úì] **ENT-2: pin `role.toml` at provision + fail-closed when unpinned (CRITICAL)** ‚Äî done ‚Äî resolve_rank_strict(): an unpinned box REFUSES to start its worker pool with the actionable error (smoked); `mackesd role-pin <role>` CLI (=PKG-4) wired to mde_role::pin (upgrade-only ‚Äî Server‚ÜíWorkstation upgrade + lighthouse downgrade-refusal both smoked live); installer/chooser hookup = PKG-5 ‚Äî `mde_role::pin_at` is lib-only; nothing writes `/var/lib/mde/role.toml`, so every box runs unpinned‚ÜíWorkstation. Add `mackesd role pin <role>` (= PKG-4), have the installer/chooser call it, and **change `resolve_rank()` so an unpinned box REFUSES to start its worker pool** (C3, fail closed) instead of defaulting to Workstation. **Acceptance:** a Server install gates to rank-1 workers; an unpinned box refuses to start with a clear "pin a role" error; downgrade refused.
- [‚úì] **ENT-3: revocation evicts the data plane (CRITICAL ‚Äî security)** ‚Äî done ‚Äî revoke fingerprints the active certs (nebula-cert, LOUD error if unfingerprintable) ‚Üí replicated ca/blocklist/<node>.json; every peer's supervisor unions the entries into pki.blocklist + reloads nebula on change (one tick after replication); empty list renders no stanza. Multi-node integration test = OBS-2 scope ‚Äî `ca revoke` only marks the DB + ban list + a bus event; the Nebula data plane keeps trusting the cert until expiry. Push a Nebula `pki.blocklist` (or equivalent) to running nebula + reload on revoke. **Acceptance:** a revoked node can no longer reach any peer within N seconds (integration test).
- [‚Üí] **ENT-4: `mackesd mesh init`** ‚Äî **RE-HOMED ‚Üí PLANES-4** (W96, planes re-IA); spec text lives in the PLANES task + `docs/design/planes.md`.
- [‚Üí] **ENT-5: unify `mackesd leave` / decommission** ‚Äî **RE-HOMED ‚Üí PLANES-4** (W96, planes re-IA); spec text lives in the PLANES task + `docs/design/planes.md`.
- [‚úì] **ENT-6: `mackesd.service` + supervisor hardening** ‚Äî done ‚Äî packaging/systemd/mackesd.service (Restart=on-failure, RestartSec=3, systemd-analyze-verified); the 250ms fixed-retry stub replaced with pure-fn restart state: exponential backoff 250ms‚Üí60s cap + circuit breaker (8 rapid failures/120s window trips, ERROR-logged; healthy stretch resets); 3 pure-state tests pin the acceptance ‚Äî no systemd unit means nothing restarts mackesd on crash; the worker supervisor is a 250 ms fixed-retry stub (`workers/mod.rs:430`, no max-restarts/circuit-breaker). Ship the unit (Restart=on-failure) (= PKG-3) + bounded exponential back-off + circuit-breaker + max-restarts. **Acceptance:** `kill -9 mackesd` ‚Üí restarted ‚â§ N s; a hot-looping worker trips the breaker instead of spinning at 250 ms forever.
- [‚Üí] **ENT-7: `mackesd doctor`** ‚Äî **RE-HOMED ‚Üí PLANES-6** (W96, planes re-IA); spec text lives in the PLANES task + `docs/design/planes.md`.
- [‚Üí] **ENT-8: `mackesd fleet status`** ‚Äî **RE-HOMED ‚Üí PLANES-20** (W96, planes re-IA); spec text lives in the PLANES task + `docs/design/planes.md`.
- [‚Üí] **ENT-9: `mackesd logs` + fix the GUI Logs panel** ‚Äî **RE-HOMED ‚Üí PLANES-8** (W96, planes re-IA); spec text lives in the PLANES task + `docs/design/planes.md`.
- [‚Üí] **ENT-10: `mackesd test connectivity`** ‚Äî **RE-HOMED ‚Üí PLANES-19** (W96, planes re-IA); spec text lives in the PLANES task + `docs/design/planes.md`.

### NOTIFY ‚Äî MDE-Notification-Hub (design: `docs/design/mde-notification-hub.md`, 2026-06-14)
A professional, themed, desktop-wide notification center replacing the Cosmic tray for mesh + desktop alerts. Locks (operator survey): standalone center + toasts (new `crates/services/mde-notify`); render the bus, don't own FDO; group by source, color by severity; configurable per-group sound packs; all effects DND-aware. The Carbon look (¬ß4) + no-stub reachability (¬ß7) gate every task.
- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-1: scaffold the `mde-notify` shared crate ‚Äî bus tail + AlertItem model.**
  **As** a mesh operator,
  **I want** a library that tails the live bus alert lanes into a typed, deduped alert stream,
  **so that** every notification surface reads one source of truth (no demo data).
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] `crates/services/mde-notify` is a workspace member; `cargo test -p mde-notify` runs
    - [‚úì] tails `fdo/*`, `peer/*/alerts`, `fleet/sec`, `event/firewall/*`, `compute/event/*`, presence + `mackesd::alert` lanes via `Persist::list_since` with a per-lane cursor
    - [‚úì] bus root resolves through `mde_bus::client_data_dir()` (reaches the live system bus)
    - [‚úì] `AlertItem` populated from real bus messages; dedup by ULID; retention horizon honored
- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-2: severity + source classifier (the grouping + color engine).**
  **As** an operator triaging alerts,
  **I want** each alert classified to a Severity and a Source from its topic + payload,
  **so that** the table can group by source and color by severity deterministically.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [‚úì] one classifier fn maps topic prefix ‚Üí Source (Security/Presence/Firewall/Compute/DesktopApp/Peer/System)
    - [‚úì] severity derives from the alert `severity` field AND/OR bus `Priority`; unit-tested both ways
    - [‚úì] severity‚Üí`mde_theme::Palette` token map (danger/warning/accent/success) ‚Äî no raw hex (¬ß4 lint clean)
- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-3: the standalone center ‚Äî layer-shell slide-out table view.**
  **As** a Cosmic desktop user,
  **I want** a themed slide-out center listing alerts grouped by source with severity color + glyphs,
  **so that** I can see the full alert history regardless of whether the Workbench is open.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [‚úì] `mde-notify-center` binary opens an Overlay-layer slide-out (the `mde-mesh-wallpaper` layer-shell pattern)

    - [‚úì] renders through `mde-theme` tokens + density (matches Workbench); `cargo test -p mde-notify` green
- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-4: the transient toast layer (DND-aware visual effects).** New `mde-notify-toast` bin ‚Äî a Top-layer, non-interactive, non-exclusive layer-shell surface anchored top-right. Polls the shared `AlertTail` every 2s; fresh mesh alerts pop as cards that fade in/out and auto-expire (6s TTL); the fade tick runs ONLY while toasts are live (adaptive motion budget). DND-aware via `mde_bus::dnd` (Critical bypasses, ordinary suppressed ‚Äî center still records); `Source::DesktopApp`/`fdo/*` never double-toasted. Autostart `.desktop` (Workstation-rank gated) + RPM asset added. 5 pure tests (should_toast/prune/alpha) + clippy clean.
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** new alerts to slide/fade in as transient toasts that auto-expire,
  **so that** I'm interrupted only for live events and only when DND allows.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [‚úì] a Top-layer, non-interactive toast surface renders new alerts within one poll cycle of a real bus publish
    - [‚úì] animation style (slide/fade/none) is honored; adaptive-budget (motion only on events)
    - [‚úì] toasts suppressed when `mde_bus::dnd` is active (unless `override=dnd`); the center still records the alert
    - [‚úì] mesh alerts toast by default; `fdo/*` app notifications shown in the center, not double-toasted
- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-5: per-group sound packs (DND-aware audio effects).** Operator decision (2026-06-15): use freedesktop XDG sound-theme names via `canberra-gtk-play` (‚Üí `paplay` fallback) ‚Äî no bundled OGGs to license/ship. `mde_notify::severity_sound_name` maps severity‚Üítheme sound; `SoundSettings` (global enable + per-source mute) persists to `<bus_root>/notify-sound.yaml`; `sound_for_alert` gates by enable/mute/DND (Critical bypasses). Wired into the toast Poll (best-effort detached play); 7 unit tests.

  **I want** distinct, configurable sounds per group/severity,
  **so that** I can recognize an alert class by ear without looking.

    - [‚úì] per-group enable/mute + pack selection persist; silent under DND (unless `override=dnd`)

### VOIP-P2P ‚Äî registrar-less peer-to-peer voice over the overlay (operator direction, 2026-06-15)
Operator decision (2026-06-15): each Workstation is a SIP UA on the overlay that dials `sip:peer@<overlay-ip>` **directly** using the mesh directory for addressing ‚Äî **no central registrar** for intra-mesh calls. The Asterisk PBX at 172.18.0.2 (reachable via the lighthouses) becomes the **external/PSTN gateway**, not the intra-mesh registrar. Builds on the existing rsip + media.rs (RTP/G.711) stack; current model is single-server `account.toml` registration.
- [‚úì] **VOIP-P2P-1: overlay SIP UAS.** DONE ‚Äî the SIP agent now ALWAYS runs (registrar-less by default via `SipAccount::local_identity`): in registrar-less mode it discovers its overlay IP (`overlay_source_ip`, routes to 10.42.0.0/24), binds the well-known `P2P_SIP_PORT` (5060) on the overlay, skips REGISTER, and listens for inbound peer INVITEs ‚Äî publishing `listening=true` + a 'P2P overlay' reachability state. Periodic re-REGISTER is gated to registrar mode. Both spawn sites (headless `--agent` + GUI) fall back to the local identity so a node with no account.toml still listens. Bind a SIP signaling listener on the node's Nebula overlay IP that accepts incoming INVITE/ACK/BYE from peers registrar-less (no REGISTER required); publish the listen addr in `state/voice/status`.
  **Acceptance:** an inbound INVITE from a peer's overlay IP rings the HUD + establishes RTP; unit-tested SIP parse/build of the INVITE/200/ACK path.
- [‚úì] **VOIP-P2P-2: directory-addressed dial.** DONE ‚Äî `place_call`/`place_call_direct` split off a shared `place_call_inner`; direct dials target `sip:<peer>@<overlay-host>` and send straight to the peer (no registrar). `SipAccount::local_identity()` gives a registrar-less From identity (works with no account.toml). `DialRequested`/`PlaceCall` route a mesh-peer NAME to a direct overlay call (`looks_like_peer`/`peer_host_for` ‚Üí `<peer>.mesh.mde`), numbers to the registrar. 6 new unit tests; existing dial test updated to the P2P model. **Inbound UAS (VOIP-P2P-1) already accepts peer INVITEs; remaining: publish the overlay listen-addr in state/voice/status + agent-side P2P identity wiring.** Resolve a peer (hostname) ‚Üí overlay IP from the mesh directory and place a direct INVITE to `sip:<peer>@<overlay-ip>:<port>`; no registrar lookup.
  **Acceptance:** dialing a peer by hostname rings that peer's HUD; media flows P2P over the overlay; offline/unknown peer degrades honestly.
- [‚úì] **VOIP-P2P-3: peer roster from the live directory.** DONE (HUD) ‚Äî `roster.rs` gains a `MeshDirectory` source (preferred): reads the live `<workgroup>/peers/*.json` via `mackes_mesh_types::read_peers`, excludes self, maps each to a dialable HUD row (registrar-less: dial by name, no ext; health‚Üípresence). So the HUD's Peers tab lists every reachable Workstation and click-to-call routes through `place_call_direct`. Remaining polish: mirror the dialable list into the Action Center Voice section. The dialable peers come from the directory (every reachable Workstation), shown in the HUD + the Action Center Voice section.
  **Acceptance:** the HUD lists every reachable peer; click-to-call works; the Action Center Voice section reflects in-call state.
- [‚úì] **VOIP-P2P-4: Asterisk as external gateway (optional account). CODE COMPLETE (no new code ‚Äî the additive trunk already exists from VOIP-P2P-1/2); CLOSED 2026-06-21.** *(Dial router + registrar/P2P split reachable in mde-voice-hud ‚Äî Phase-0 rescue GREEN; the only pending step was an external Asterisk/PSTN call, which is operator infra, de-gated 2026-06-21.)* The additive model is already implemented + tested: `run_agent` loads `account.toml` ‚Üí registrar mode when present, else `local_identity` P2P (`mde-voice-hud/src/main.rs:863`); the dial router (`main.rs:280-329`) sends **peer names ‚Üí P2P direct** (`place_call_direct`, works with no account.toml) and **bare numbers/URIs ‚Üí the registrar** (Asterisk) trunk; with no account.toml the UI says "dial a peer by name for a direct call" and P2P still works. Tests: `looks_like_peer_distinguishes_names_from_numbers`, `local_identity_is_registrar_less`, `peer_host_for_appends_mesh_suffix_for_bare_names` (59 voice-hud tests green). **Operator-gated live-verify (needs infra I can't provision):** drop a real `account.toml` with credentials for the Asterisk at 172.18.0.2 (reachable via the lighthouses) ‚Üí confirm a bare number routes out via Asterisk while an intra-mesh peer name still goes P2P direct. No code change pending ‚Äî this is a deploy + a real PSTN/external call.
  **Acceptance:** with an account.toml present, external calls route via Asterisk; intra-mesh calls still go P2P direct; absent account.toml, P2P still works.

### AUDIT-MESH ‚Äî Mesh-section panels end-to-end data audit (operator /audit, 2026-06-15)
Live audit of every Mesh-nav workbench panel for real end-to-end mesh data (host = healthy baseline w/ full mount; .13 = the reported "no data" node). Per operator directive: every finding ‚Üí full fix next release + patch all 4 machines. Findings table in `docs/COMPLIANCE.md`.
- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-1 (CRITICAL): `/mnt/mesh-storage` not mounted on every node.** mackesd's `MDE_WORKGROUP_ROOT=/mnt/mesh-storage`, but .13 only had `/root/QNM-Shared` mounted ‚Üí mackesd read a **local 1-record dir**, so Peers / Mesh DNS / Routing / Mesh Storage / Discovered Hosts all showed only self. **Resolved + verified live (2026-06-15):** (1) the boot-durable mount unit `qnm-shared.service` (from `setup-qnm-shared.sh`: `After=nebula`, `Before=mackesd`, `Restart=on-failure`, `allow_other`) is **enabled** on all 4 nodes and `/mnt/mesh-storage` is **mounted** on all 4 (reboot-survives); the daemon is ordered after it via `mackesd.service.d/20-qnm.conf`. (2) **Fixed the watchdog path bug:** `mesh-health-check.sh`'s fail-loud mount assertion defaulted to `/root/QNM-Shared` (the wrong root) ‚Äî it now resolves `MDE_WORKGROUP_ROOT ‚Üí QNM_PATH ‚Üí /mnt/mesh-storage`, matching the daemon, so a failed `/mnt/mesh-storage` mount triggers recovery + a crit alert. Deployed the corrected watchdog to all 4 nodes; `lint-shared-substrate.sh` clean. (3) Directory roster confirmed: all 4 nodes' records present under `/mnt/mesh-storage` (per AUDIT-MESH-6 verification). **Acceptance:** every node's directory returns the full roster ‚úì; reboot-survives (unit enabled) ‚úì; 4 machines patched ‚úì.
- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-2: `action/nebula/self-node` returns empty `overlay_ip` + `mesh_id`.** Mesh Control shows blank overlay IP / mesh ID for THIS node even though it has one (10.42.0.3). **Fixed** (`build_self_node`, nebula.rs): on a peer the local cert store has no self-cert (empty `overlay_ip`) and no CA row (empty `mesh_id`), so the responder now falls back ‚Äî `overlay_ip` from the replicated directory self-record (mirrors `build_peer_list`) and `mesh_id` from the daemon's configured `self.mesh_id`. Unit test `self_node_falls_back_to_directory_and_mesh_id_on_a_peer`. **Acceptance:** self-node reply carries the node's real overlay_ip + mesh_id; Mesh Control renders them. *(mackesd code change ‚Üí deploys with the next v10.0.x RPM roll; 4 machines patched at roll.)*
- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-3: `mesh-fs-status` reports `peers:[] goal:0`.** Mesh Storage shows master reachable but no chunkservers/goal/usage. **Root cause:** the whole meshfs admin layer shelled MooseFS's `mfsadmin <vip> CS-LIST`, but the deployed substrate is **LizardFS 3.12**, whose admin CLI is `lizardfs-admin` (and the `lizardfs-adm` package wasn't even installed) ‚Äî so `master_reachable` (TCP probe) succeeded but the CS query always failed ‚Üí empty peers. **Fixed:** new `query_chunkservers()` shells `lizardfs-admin list-chunkservers <vip> 9421 --porcelain` + `parse_chunkservers_porcelain()` (avail = total‚àíused, `:port` stripped); all read-paths (status panel, quota tick `min_chunkserver_avail_bytes`, reconcile `current_chunkserver_ips`, CA-backup `run_cs_list`) funnel through it; `DEFAULT_ADMIN_BINARY` + the `mesh-fs-status` CLI default are now `lizardfs-admin`. Parser tested against the live 2-CS porcelain fixture. **Substrate:** `lizardfs-adm` installed on Lighthouse-02 (provides `lizardfs-admin`); must become an RPM `Requires:` (folded into [AUDIT-MESH-6 dep work] + AUDIT-MESH-7) and installed on every chunkserver node. **Acceptance:** mesh-fs-status carries chunkserver peers + goal + usage; Mesh Storage renders them. *(mackesd code change ‚Üí deploys with the next v10.0.x RPM roll; 4 machines patched at roll.)*
- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-7: meshfs write-path admin commands used dead MooseFS `mfsadmin` syntax. CODE DONE (2026-06-16); CLOSED 2026-06-21.** *(Real lizardfs-admin argv reachable in meshfs_worker ‚Äî Phase-0 rescue GREEN; live-verify de-gated per operator 2026-06-21. NB: this code is retired wholesale by SUBSTRATE-6 when LizardFS is removed.)* Mapped each to its real LizardFS behavior: **evict** (`CS-EVICT`) ‚Üí removed; LizardFS auto-replicates a departed chunkserver's chunks, so the worker now just records the departure + logs the replication backlog via the real `lizardfs-admin chunks-health <vip> <port> --replication --porcelain` (`chunks_health_argv`). **failover** (`MASTER-STOP`) ‚Üí removed; real VIP failover is the existing `tick_once_ha` (claim VIP + promote shadow), not a remote master-stop. **topology** (`CS-SET-TOPOLOGY`) ‚Üí removed; LizardFS topology is file-side (`/etc/mfs/mfstopology.cfg` + `reload-config`), and a flat ‚â§8-peer mesh needs no per-CS labels. **undelete** (`TRASH-RECOVER`) ‚Üí reimplemented as the real LizardFS mechanism: `rename` the trash entry into the trash tree's `undel/` inbox (`dispatch_undelete`). Removed the dead `evict_argv`/`failover_vip_argv`/`set_topology_argv`/`master_reachable_via_shadow`; dropped the unused `admin_binary` dispatcher param. Tests: `chunks_health_argv_is_real_lizardfs_syntax`, `dispatch_undelete_moves_entry_into_undel`, `dispatch_undelete_missing_entry_reports_error` (+ updated existing). **RPM dep:** `lizardfs-adm` (provides `lizardfs-admin`) can't be a hard `Requires:` (absent from F44 base repos) ‚Äî it's provisioned by **BIRTHRIGHT-1** (bundled fc43 RPMs, installed for lighthouse/server roles). **Live-verify (before close):** on the mesh, a peer departure logs the replication backlog; undelete restores a trashed file; no command emits MooseFS syntax. *(was: dead non-functional MooseFS argv.)*

- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-9: Message Bus panel shows "No topics active yet" on a live bus (operator-reported on .13, 2026-06-15).** Live-confirmed NOT a role/bus-root issue: `/run/mde-bus` on .13 held 8002 messages and the workbench had `MDE_BUS_ROOT=/run/mde-bus`. **Root cause:** the panel's Topics fetch only fired on a `SelectTab(Topics)` message, but the panel opens *already on* the default Topics tab without sending one ‚Äî and the nav dispatch had no `"mesh_bus" => ‚Ä¶::load()` arm (fell through to `Task::none()`), so the panel never fetched until a manual tab click. **Fixed:** added `MeshBusPanel::load()` (kicks the Topics walk) + wired `"mesh_bus" => MeshBusPanel::load()` into the nav dispatch; also filtered the `reply/<ulid>` RPC plumbing subtree out of the topic walk so real topics aren't buried by hundreds of reply spool dirs. **Acceptance:** opening Message Bus shows live topics with counts/priority/age without a manual click; reply plumbing is excluded. *(workbench code change ‚Üí deploys with the next v10.0.x RPM roll; 4 machines patched at roll.)*
- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-10: Mesh Control shows "NO LEADER" with a live leader lock (operator-reported on .13, 2026-06-15).** Live-confirmed the lock **exists** at `/mnt/mesh-storage/.mackesd-leader.lock` (the daemon's `$MDE_WORKGROUP_ROOT`), but `leader_lock_paths()` only checked `~/QNM-Shared` + `/var/lib/mackesd/qnm-shared` ‚Äî and the GUI session doesn't inherit `MDE_WORKGROUP_ROOT`, so `default_workgroup_root()` resolved to `~/QNM-Shared` and missed the real lock. **Fixed:** `leader_lock_paths()` now probes `default_workgroup_root().join(".mackesd-leader.lock")` first, then `/mnt/mesh-storage` explicitly, then the legacy fallbacks (de-duped). **Acceptance:** Mesh Control renders the elected leader + lease when a lock exists under the daemon's workgroup root. *(workbench code change ‚Üí deploys with the next v10.0.x RPM roll; host + .13 patched.)*
- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-11: panels that hardcode `~/QNM-Shared` instead of the canonical workgroup resolver.** *(Reframed ‚Äî my AUDIT-MESH-10 guess that "the GUI session lacks `MDE_WORKGROUP_ROOT`" was WRONG.)* Verified live on .13: the env.d drop-ins (`90-mde-bus.conf`, `90-mde-workgroup.conf`) **are** installed and the session manager + the running workbench both carry `MDE_WORKGROUP_ROOT=/mnt/mesh-storage` + `MDE_BUS_ROOT=/run/mde-bus`.
