- [‚úó] **AUDIT-MESH-13: ~~cross-UID SQLite bus index invisibility~~ ‚Äî DISPROVEN / MISDIAGNOSIS (corrected 2026-06-15).** I initially concluded all `action/*` RPCs fail because the SQLite `messages` table isn't visible cross-uid. **That was wrong ‚Äî a test artifact.** Re-verified rigorously: `sqlite3` as root reads mm's just-written rows fine; a **long-lived** Python connection sees another process's new write (0‚Üí1); root `mde-bus history` **with `MDE_BUS_ROOT=/run/mde-bus` actually set** sees mm's rows. The persist layer is fully cross-uid + cross-connection correct. **The real artifact:** my CLI tests ran in a **non-login ssh shell that has no `MDE_BUS_ROOT`**, so the CLI resolved to the **per-HOME** bus (`~/.local/share/mde/bus`) ‚Äî a different spool from `/run/mde-bus` where the responders listen ‚Üí "no responder." The GUI (which *does* carry `MDE_BUS_ROOT=/run/mde-bus` via env.d) uses the shared root. **Proof the RPC infra works:** with `MDE_BUS_ROOT=/run/mde-bus` set, `action/nebula/self-node` ‚Üí `{node_id:‚Ä¶}` ‚úì and `action/connect/devices` ‚Üí `[{‚Ä¶moto g‚Ä¶}]` ‚úì both reply. No cross-uid bug exists; no persist-layer change needed. *(Lesson: when testing the bus by CLI, export `MDE_BUS_ROOT=/run/mde-bus` to match the GUI, or the per-HOME fallback masquerades as a dead responder.)*
- [‚úì] **#40: Connected Devices "Bus RPC failed" ‚Äî RESOLVED / not a current bug.** Verified live on .13: `action/connect/devices` returns the real roster (`moto g stylus 5G`) when queried on the shared bus root (the GUI's path). The kdc-host responder is up (`connect_bus:true`) and answers. The operator's original "Bus RPC failed" was the **pre-19:07 workbench binary** (before the AUDIT-MESH-9/10 redeploy) and/or my own CLI-env artifact (above). **Acceptance:** Connected Devices lists paired/discovered devices ‚Äî confirmed at the RPC layer; re-verify in the relaunched GUI.
- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-16 (CRITICAL ‚Äî the REAL cross-uid bus bug; root cause of music "no data" + any non-root responder): shared-spool subdirectories aren't cross-uid writable, so a desktop-user responder's replies are silently dropped.** Definitively root-caused (2026-06-15): `action/music/*` verbs all timed out because **mde-musicd runs as the desktop user (mm)** and its reply write to `/run/mde-bus/reply/<ulid>` failed ‚Äî `/run/mde-bus/reply/` is `drwxr-xr-x root root` (created by the root mackesd daemon at umask 022), so mm got EPERM, and `poll_transport` ignores write errors (`let _ = persist.write`). The spool ROOT is sticky-1777 (any uid can make top-level dirs) but `Persist::write_full` only `relax_shared`'d the **leaf** topic dir, never the intermediate parent `create_dir_all` made ‚Äî so `reply/` stayed 0755. mackesd's own responders (root) were unaffected ‚Üí nebula/connect worked, music didn't. **Fixed:** `persist.rs::relax_topic_chain` now relaxes EVERY path component (parent + leaf) to 0777 on each write, so any mesh uid can write replies. **Verified live:** after a stop-gap `chmod 1777` of the spool parents on .13, get-state replies instantly `{ok:true,active:false,audio_available:true,needs_airsonic:false,‚Ä¶}`. **Acceptance:** a desktop-user responder's replies reach the requester; verified get-state on .13 ‚úì. *(mde-bus lib change ‚Üí rebuilds mackesd+musicd+mde-bus; live-patched both Workstations via chmod; durable via the next RPM roll.)*
- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-14: `action/music/get-state` stall ‚Äî RESOLVED (the blocker was AUDIT-MESH-16's spool perms).** Two real hardening fixes shipped along the way and kept: **#1** Airsonic `reqwest::Client` now has 3s connect + 10s total timeouts (`airsonic.rs::build_http_client`) so a dead Airsonic can't hang `poll_browse` forever; **#2** `bus_responder::serve` reordered so the fast local responders (`poll_once`/`poll_transport`/`poll_peers`) run before the network-bound `poll_browse`. Both are correct defense-in-depth, but the actual cause of the timeout was AUDIT-MESH-16 (musicd as mm couldn't write into the root-owned `reply/`). **Verified:** get-state replies on .13 with the new musicd + the spool chmod. *(musicd deployed to host + .13.)*
- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-15 (operator-reported, 2026-06-15): `~/Documents` does NOT auto-sync across the mesh ‚Äî the FPG-7 XDG bind-mount is broken on two counts. FIXED (2026-06-16).** Both bugs fixed in `meshfs_worker.rs`: (1) **wrong home** ‚Äî new `desktop_user_homes()` parses `/etc/passwd` for the real uid-1000..60000 desktop user(s) under `/home`; the tick now binds for each of them (with a headless fall-back to the daemon's `$HOME`), so it binds `/home/<u>/Documents` not the daemon's `/root/Documents`. (2) **silent degrade** ‚Äî `ensure_xdg_binds` now creates the communal source tree `<mount>/home/<dir>` (chmod 0777 so any desktop uid on any node can write, mirroring the AUDIT-MESH-16 spool fix) and **returns failure lines** which the caller logs at **WARN** (was a swallowed `debug!`) ‚Äî a missing mount or a failed `mount --bind` is now loud, per the ONBOARD-6 lesson. Tests: `ensure_xdg_binds_reports_loudly_when_mount_absent`, `ensure_xdg_binds_creates_communal_source_when_mount_is_a_dir`, `desktop_user_homes_excludes_root_and_system_uids`. **Acceptance:** a file copied to `~/Documents` on one node appears at `~/Documents` on every node within the replication window ‚Äî **LIVE-VERIFIED on v10.0.12 (2026-06-17):** `.13`'s `~/Documents` is a FUSE bind, and a file written there replicated to the dev host's `/mnt/mesh-storage/home/Documents` (the communal location every node's `~/Documents` binds to) within the window. *(shipped + verified.)*
  <details><summary>(original report)</summary>

- [‚úì] **AUDIT-MESH-12: LizardFS admin CLI (`lizardfs-admin`) absent on F44 Workstations ‚Äî Mesh Storage panel can't query the master.** Surfaced verifying AUDIT-MESH-3 live: `lizardfs-adm` is in the F43 repos (lighthouses) but **not F44** (`dnf list` ‚Üí no match on .13/host). **Resolved:** chose the same out-of-band cross-release path as `lizardfs-client` ‚Äî installed the `lizardfs-adm-3.12.0-31.fc43` RPM on both F44 Workstations (`rpm -Uvh --nodeps`; the fc43 binary runs on F44). **Verified live:** `lizardfs-admin list-chunkservers 10.42.0.1 9421 --porcelain` now returns both chunkservers from host **and** .13 ‚Äî exactly the format the AUDIT-MESH-3 parser reads. `setup-qnm-shared.sh` now warns + documents the F44 `lizardfs-adm` requirement in its client section. **Packaging note:** `lizardfs-adm` cannot be a hard RPM `Requires:` while absent from F44 base repos (same constraint as `lizardfs-client`) ‚Äî handled out-of-band per-release. **Acceptance:** the LizardFS admin dependency is documented + satisfied on all 4 nodes ‚úì; the Mesh Storage panel will list peers/goal/usage once the new mackesd (AUDIT-MESH-3) lands ‚Äî *render verification gated on the v10.0.x RPM roll like the other mackesd fixes this session.*

## BRAND ‚Äî Carbon system-wide branding (operator-locked 2026-06-16; design: docs/design/branding.md)
One-way, auto-applied on first boot of a Workstation-role node. Icon set = operator-provided tarball. GTK+Qt+Cosmic themed. mde-files default + mde-cosmic-applet swap (Cosmic kept). LightDM greeter + Plymouth themed. Layout = baked .13 Cosmic template (`assets/brand/cosmic-layout/`, notification applet already swapped out).
- [‚úì] **BRAND-1: brand-apply orchestrator + first-boot service (Workstation-gated, one-way).** `magic-mesh-brand apply` idempotent script + `magic-mesh-brand.service` oneshot (runs once, `/var/lib/mde/branded` stamp; only when role=workstation). **Acceptance:** on a fresh Workstation first boot the service runs all branding steps once and is a no-op thereafter; Server/Lighthouse never run it.
- [‚úì] **BRAND-2: install the Carbon icon theme (operator tarball).** Extract the provided tar to `/usr/share/icons/<Name>`, `gtk-update-icon-cache`, set icon-theme across gsettings + GTK + Qt + Cosmic. **Acceptance:** `gsettings get ‚Ä¶icon-theme` = Carbon; folders/apps render Carbon icons. *(blocked on the operator's tar; everything else proceeds.)* _(reconciled 2026-06-30: operator tarball landed (38a1e5f); magic-mesh-brand.sh:56 extracts to /usr/share/icons + sets gtk-icon-theme-name ‚Äî blocker resolved)_
- [‚úì] **BRAND-3: Carbon GTK 3/4 theme.** Generate `/usr/share/themes/Carbon` from the mde-theme Carbon tokens (Gray 10/90/100); set `gtk-theme` + GTK3/4 settings.ini. **Acceptance:** GTK apps render Carbon dark.
- [‚úì] **BRAND-4: Carbon Qt 5/6 theme.** qt5ct/qt6ct (or Kvantum) Carbon palette + `QT_QPA_PLATFORMTHEME`. **Acceptance:** a Qt app renders Carbon, not default Fusion.

- [‚úì] **BRAND-6: Carbon Plymouth boot splash.** A `Carbon` plymouth theme from `assets/brand` art; `plymouth-set-default-theme -R Carbon`. **Acceptance:** boot shows the Carbon splash.

## MESHSHELL ‚Äî Bash mesh prompt + greeting + cheat sheet (operator-locked 2026-06-16; design: docs/design/mesh-shell.md)
starship prompt (full online-hostname list, snapshot-fed) ¬∑ per-shell Carbon greeting (health + service matrix + updates, bounded live) ¬∑ `mesh-help` auto-generated cheat sheet ¬∑ all roles, one-way, Carbon ANSI + ASCII wordmark.
- [‚úì] **SHELL-1: mesh-status snapshot refresher + timer.** Writes `/run/mde/mesh-status.json` (~30s) with nodes[hostname,overlay_ip,presence] + per-node service matrix + per-node version/update, on all roles (mackesd tick or oneshot+timer). **Acceptance:** the file exists + refreshes on every node; valid JSON consumed by the prompt + greeting.
- [‚úì] **SHELL-2: starship prompt + mesh module.** `/etc/starship.toml` with a custom `mesh` module that reads the snapshot and prints the online-hostname list (Carbon-colored); profile.d runs `starship init bash`. starship as an RPM dep/bundle. **Acceptance:** bash prompt shows the live online hostnames with no per-render lag.
- [‚úì] **SHELL-3: welcome greeting (every shell).** `/etc/profile.d/zz-mde-welcome.sh`: Mackes ASCII wordmark + color-coded per-node health + summary + per-node service matrix + per-node update list; reads snapshot, bounded ~1.5s live refresh w/ fallback. **Acceptance:** every new bash shell prints the greeting in ‚â§~1.5s even when the mesh is down.
- [‚úì] **SHELL-4: `mesh-help` cheat sheet.** Auto-generated from mackesd/meshctl/mde-bus `--help` + curated Fedora/system commands, grouped: enroll/join, status/health, storage, services/logs, system. **Acceptance:** `mesh-help` prints the grouped sheet; entries reflect real, runnable commands.
- [‚úì] **SHELL-5: RPM packaging + enable (all roles).** Ship SHELL-1..4 assets + starship; enable the snapshot timer on all roles in post_install; one-way. **Acceptance:** a fresh install on any role ‚Üí new shell shows prompt + greeting; `mesh-help` works.

## v10.0.9 roll findings (2026-06-16)
- [‚úì] **REL-1: mackesd graceful shutdown hangs ‚Üí wedged restarts.** `systemctl restart mackesd` repeatedly stuck in `deactivating` for the full TimeoutStopSec on .13 + both lighthouses during the v10.0.9 roll, leaving the daemon "active" but NOT answering bus RPCs until a `systemctl kill -s SIGKILL` + `start`. Root-cause the shutdown path (a worker/blocking task not honoring the ShutdownToken within the stop timeout) and/or set a short `TimeoutStopSec` + `KillMode`/`SIGKILL` fallback in `mackesd.service` so a restart can't leave a half-dead daemon. **Acceptance:** `systemctl restart mackesd` returns to a responsive daemon within a few seconds on every node; no manual SIGKILL needed.
- [‚úì] **REL-2: `libasound.so.2` is an implicit hard RPM dep but not declared.** LH-02 (headless) lacked `alsa-lib`, so the 10.0.9 RPM install failed until `dnf install alsa-lib` (the binaries link ALSA via the audio chain). Add `alsa-lib` to the RPM `requires` (or make the audio link optional on headless roles) so a fresh lighthouse install resolves cleanly. **Acceptance:** a clean `dnf install magic-mesh` on a headless F43 node pulls alsa-lib automatically.

## NOTIFY-DIST ‚Äî cross-node notification distribution never provisioned (operator-reported 2026-06-16)
- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-DIST-1: the per-peer ntfy broker is permanently skipped ‚Üí no mesh-wide notification traffic.** Operator: "why am I not seeing notification traffic from all over the network? / with a shared bus I expected more traffic / why isn't it installed with birthrights?" **Diagnosed live on .13:** the bus heartbeat logs `"broker":"skipped"` every minute and every publish is `--no-broker` (persisted locally only); .13's alert lane has ONLY its own topics (`peer/UNIT-EAGLE/*`, `fdo/system`, `fleet/sec`) ‚Äî no peers'. **Root cause:** the "Mackes Bus" is a PER-NODE local spool (`/run/mde-bus`, tmpfs); cross-node fan-out is an ntfy broker over Nebula (`mde_bus::broker`) that was skipped because (1) its config template (`data/ntfy/server.yml.tmpl`) was never in the RPM assets ‚Üí `TemplateMissing`, and (2) `ntfy` isn't installed ‚Üí `NtfyMissing` (it's not in the Fedora repos, so it could never be a hard RPM `Requires:` "birthright" ‚Äî same class as starship + lizardfs-admin-on-F44). **Fix (shipped):** ship the template to `/usr/share/mde/ntfy/server.yml.tmpl`; provision ntfy as a first-boot birthright via a checksum-verified fetch (`mesh-install-ntfy`, ntfy v2.24.0 sha-pinned, `mesh-broker-setup.service`, all roles) ‚Äî the bus daemon re-evaluates prereqs each cycle, so the broker starts WITHOUT a restart once both are present. **Still to verify on the v10.0.10 roll:** that the broker, running on all 4 nodes, actually federates ‚Äî i.e. each node's alert lane (`peer/<host>/alerts`) reaches every peer's bus (confirm the forward/subscribe model end-to-end; the broker running ‚âÝ proven cross-node delivery). **Acceptance:** .13's Action Center shows alerts from Lighthouse-01/02 + fedora, not just itself; `peer/+/alerts` topics from all nodes appear on every node's bus. **CLOSED 2026-06-21 (rescue ‚Äî LIVE-GATED):** the broker supervision is code-complete + reachable ‚Äî `mde_bus::broker` (`BrokerConfig`/`evaluate_prereqs`, ntfy child spawn + graceful degrade) supervised by `workers::bus_supervisor` (spawned in mackesd), plus the `mesh-install-ntfy` birthright fetch. Live-verify de-gated per operator. **Honest caveat:** cross-node federation was *not* independently re-proven here (build VM down / no live fleet) ‚Äî close rests on the code + the lifted gate, not a live delivery check.
  **UPDATE (2026-06-16) ‚Äî the broker was a dead end for the in-app panel.** Live on fedora: the broker is now `live` (ntfy running) but it's a PUSH gateway only ‚Äî there is **no ntfy-subscribe / cross-node bus reinjection anywhere in the codebase**, so the panel (which tails only the LOCAL bus) could never show peers' alerts via ntfy. Two real bugs found + fixed instead ‚Äî NOTIFY-DIST-2 (the actual federation) and NOTIFY-DIST-3 (the publish 404).
- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-DIST-2: cross-node alert federation via the replicated shared-state plane (the real fix for "no notifications in the mesh app").** The notification panel (`mde_notify::AlertTail`) only ever tails the LOCAL per-node bus, and nothing fed it peers' alerts ‚Üí every node's panel showed only its own. **Fix:** a mackesd `alert-mirror` worker mirrors this node's alert-lane messages to `<workgroup>/.mesh-alerts/<host>/<ulid>.json` on QNM-Shared (LizardFS, replicated; ¬ß9 one-state doctrine ‚Äî no new transport); every node's panel also reads ALL peers' subdirs via the new `AlertTail::poll_shared` (deduped against the local tail; the Hub merges + sorts newest-first). Bounded by `prune_shared_alerts` (newest 2000/host, ULID = age order); gated on `shared_root_writable` (BOOT-REC-1). Tests: `shared_alert_roundtrip_and_dedup`, `poll_shared_missing_dir_is_empty`. **LIVE-VERIFIED on v10.0.12 (2026-06-17):** QNM-Shared `.mesh-alerts/` carries **9 host subdirs** (fedora, both lighthouses, MDE-VM-1..5, UNIT-EAGLE) with ~918 mirrored alerts; a marker alert published on .13 was mirrored by its `alert-mirror` worker to `.mesh-alerts/UNIT-EAGLE/<ulid>.json` (content confirmed) and is visible to every node's `poll_shared`. *(shipped + verified. The ntfy real-time broker path ‚Äî NOTIFY-DIST-1/3 ‚Äî is separate and not active on .13; the durable QNM-Shared federation is what makes the panel mesh-wide.)*
- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-DIST-3: ntfy publish 404 ‚Äî hierarchical bus topics aren't valid ntfy topic names.** Every alert publish to the broker returned 404 (verified live: `POST /flattopic`‚Üí200, `POST /peer/UNIT-EAGLE/alerts`‚Üí404), so the push gateway silently dropped everything. **Fix:** `publish_to_ntfy` flattens the bus topic to a valid `[-_A-Za-z0-9]{1,64}` segment (`ntfy_topic()`) + carries the real topic in `X-Topic`. Committed `95fc7f2`. **CLI-PATH COMPLETION (2026-06-17):** the hooks publisher flattened, but the **`mde-bus publish` CLI** path (which the alert SOURCES actually use ‚Äî selinux_monitor, kdc_host, mesh-alert via `Command::new("mde-bus")`) still posted the raw `a/b/c` topic ‚Üí 404 ‚Üí every alert fell back to persist-only. Fixed in `cli/publish.rs` to call `ntfy_topic()` too. **LIVE-VERIFIED on v10.0.13 (dev host):** `mde-bus publish fleet/sec/test/‚Ä¶` now forwards to `‚Ä¶/fleet_sec_test_fedora` with no 404. **Acceptance:** ntfy publishes return 2xx for hierarchical/spaced topics ‚Äî met. *(shipped in v10.0.13.)*

## BIRTHRIGHT ‚Äî installation/first-boot birthrights vs advertised service requirements (audit 2026-06-16; findings: docs/COMPLIANCE.md "Birthrights vs advertised service requirements")
The birthright audit verdict: **partially fit-for-purpose.** In-repo `Requires:` (nebula/nmap/alsa-lib) are correct; this session closed the ntfy + starship out-of-repo gaps via first-boot checksum-verified fetch. The remaining critical gap is that the ¬ß1 shared-state substrate (LizardFS/QNM-Shared) is **not a birthright** ‚Äî a fresh `dnf install` + `found`/`join` does not yield a working mesh. These items are the actionable lift. **BIRTHRIGHT-1 + BIRTHRIGHT-2 are both DONE (2026-06-16, operator-greenlit) ‚Äî a fresh `dnf install` + `found`/`join` now stands up LizardFS/QNM-Shared role-aware; ships in v10.0.10.**
- [‚úì] **BIRTHRIGHT-1: provision LizardFS/QNM-Shared as a birthright at enrollment (role-aware), so a fresh install is a working mesh. DONE (2026-06-16).** `mackesd found`/`join` now call `provision_qnm_shared()`: (1) `mesh-install-lizardfs <role>` installs binaries ‚Äî dnf-first (F43) ‚Üí **bundled fc43 RPM family** (`vendor-lizardfs-rpms.sh` stages 7 RPMs/2.5 MB ‚Üí `/usr/share/magic-mesh/vendor/lizardfs/`, `rpm --nodeps` on F44) ‚Üí pinned fetch manifest ‚Üí loud non-fatal warn; (2) `setup-qnm-shared` role-aware ‚Äî found=`--master --chunkserver --client` (master on the founder's overlay IP), join Server/2nd-LH=`--chunkserver --client`, join Workstation=`--client`, master VIP 10.42.0.1 ‚Äî BEFORE `mackesd.service` starts. **Fail-loud:** `run_serve` ERRORs if `/mnt/mesh-storage` isn't a real FUSE mount; the mesh-health watchdog restarts `qnm-shared.service`. `qnm_setup_flags` unit-tested (4 tests); `tests/mesh_shared_state.rs` + `lint-shared-substrate.sh` untouched. Fresh-from-RPM verification gated on the v10.0.10 roll. *(ships in v10.0.10.)* _(reconciled 2026-06-30: superseded by SUBSTRATE-V2 (81d18bd ripped out LizardFS); found/join now provision etcd+Syncthing at enroll (mde-enroll/src/setup_action.rs:39))_
  <details><summary>(original story)</summary>

- [‚úì] **BIRTHRIGHT-1: provision LizardFS/QNM-Shared as a birthright at enrollment (role-aware), so a fresh install is a working mesh.**
  **As** an operator installing MCNF on a new node,
  **I want** `dnf install magic-mesh` + `network-enroll found`/`join` to install the LizardFS binaries and auto-mount QNM-Shared for my role,
  **so that** leader election, the directory, Documents sync, fleet, and the CA work out of the box without a manual `setup-qnm-shared` step.
  **Context:** LizardFS is not in F44 base repos (same out-of-repo class as ntfy/starship/lizardfs-admin), so it can't be a hard RPM `Requires:`. `setup-qnm-shared.sh` ships to `/usr/libexec/mackesd/` but is never auto-invoked; `cmd_found`/`cmd_join` (ONBOARD-4) don't provision it. This is the ONBOARD-6 failure class (code reachable + tested against a tempdir, but the deployed substrate is never mounted ‚Üí silent NO-LEADER/empty-mesh).
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] `network-enroll found` on a fresh Lighthouse provisions the LizardFS master + a chunkserver and mounts `/mnt/mesh-storage` (or the role's workgroup root) automatically. _(reconciled 2026-06-30: superseded by SUBSTRATE-V2 ‚Äî LizardFS plane retired (f5d7c92); equivalent working-mesh provisioning now via setup-etcd/setup-syncthing at enroll)_
    - [‚úì] `network-enroll join` on a fresh Server/Workstation installs `lizardfs-client` (+ `lizardfs-adm` on F44) via the checksum-verified first-boot fetch and mounts QNM-Shared, role-aware (Lighthouse ‚äÇ Server ‚äÇ Workstation). _(reconciled 2026-06-30: superseded by SUBSTRATE-V2 ‚Äî LizardFS plane retired (f5d7c92); equivalent working-mesh provisioning now via setup-etcd/setup-syncthing at enroll)_
    - [‚úì] After enroll, `mackesd` elects/sees a leader and the directory is populated with **no** manual `setup-qnm-shared` invocation. _(reconciled 2026-06-30: superseded by SUBSTRATE-V2 ‚Äî LizardFS plane retired (f5d7c92); equivalent working-mesh provisioning now via setup-etcd/setup-syncthing at enroll)_
    - [‚úì] A fail-loud runtime check surfaces "QNM-Shared not mounted" instead of silently degrading (the ¬ß7/ONBOARD-6 guard), and the lint `install-helpers/lint-shared-substrate.sh` still passes. _(reconciled 2026-06-30: superseded by SUBSTRATE-V2 ‚Äî LizardFS plane retired (f5d7c92); equivalent working-mesh provisioning now via setup-etcd/setup-syncthing at enroll)_
    - [‚úì] Verified on a fresh-from-RPM node joining the live mesh (not a tempdir). _(reconciled 2026-06-30: superseded by SUBSTRATE-V2 ‚Äî LizardFS plane retired (f5d7c92); equivalent working-mesh provisioning now via setup-etcd/setup-syncthing at enroll)_
  </details>
- [‚úì] **BIRTHRIGHT-2: decide bundle-vs-fetch for the out-of-repo birthrights so an air-gapped first boot still provisions.** *(design: docs/design/birthrights.md)*
  **As** an operator installing on a node without internet at first boot,
  **I want** the out-of-repo birthrights (ntfy, starship, lizardfs, lizardfs-adm) to provision from a bundled fallback,
  **so that** an offline/air-gapped install is still a working, branded mesh ‚Äî not silently degraded.
  **Context:** the first-boot fetch model (SHELL-2 starship, NOTIFY-DIST-1 ntfy, future BIRTHRIGHT-1 LizardFS) requires internet at first boot; there is no bundled fallback today. Bundling adds RPM size + license/redistribution review per dependency.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] A documented decision per dependency: bundle in the RPM vs fetch-with-cached-fallback vs fetch-only (with the offline degrade explicitly stated). ‚Äî `docs/design/birthrights.md`: ntfy + starship = **bundle** (small, permissive, air-gapped-critical); lizardfs/lizardfs-adm = **fetch-only, deferred to BIRTHRIGHT-1** (offline = no shared state, stated loudly).
    - [‚úì] For any dependency chosen to bundle, the RPM carries the binary and first boot provisions it with no network call; `mesh-install-*` falls back to the bundled copy when the fetch fails. ‚Äî `mesh-install-ntfy`/`mesh-install-starship` are **bundled-first** (prefer `/usr/share/magic-mesh/vendor/$ASSET`, checksum-verified; network only when absent). Blobs are fetched+verified at build time by `vendor-birthright-blobs.sh` (pins parsed from the install scripts ‚Üí no drift), gitignored, wired into `build-rpm-fedora43.sh` + the generate-rpm `assets`.
    - [‚úì] License/NOTICE coverage updated for any bundled third-party binary before a public RPM. ‚Äî NOTICE records ntfy (Apache-2.0) + starship (ISC), aggregated not linked.
  **DONE (2026-06-16, bundle path).** *(packaging + scripts ‚Üí ships in v10.0.10.)*

## BOOT-RECOVERY ‚Äî every node must auto-recover from power loss / reboot (operator hard requirement 2026-06-16)
Exposed by a .13 reboot that came up degraded (QNM-Shared unmounted; mackesd up but bus replies failing ‚Üí "no peers"). Auto-recovery is a RELEASE GATE: reboot a node, confirm it returns to a healthy member with ZERO manual steps.
- [‚úì] **BOOT-REC-1: stop mackesd poisoning the unmounted mount.** DONE (2026-06-16) ‚Äî `shared_root_writable` guard: `leader::try_acquire` + `telemetry::write_heartbeat` refuse to write `/mnt/mesh-storage` when it isn't a real FUSE mount, so a boot mount-race is no longer made permanent (the dir stays empty ‚Üí LizardFS can remount, the watchdog recovers). Verified live on .13.
- [‚úì] **BOOT-REC-2: QNM-Shared mount reliably comes up at boot.** `qnm-shared.service` must retry the FUSE mount to success once the overlay+master are reachable (the 60s ExecStartPre probe isn't enough on a cold boot); the `mesh-health` watchdog must remount if it drops. **Acceptance:** a cold-rebooted node has `/mnt/mesh-storage` mounted within the boot window, no manual remount.
- [‚úì] **BOOT-REC-3: mackesd self-heals an unwritable bus DB on startup.** `/run/mde-bus/index.sqlite` (WAL, cross-uid create race between root mackesd + the uid-1000 desktop session at boot) can boot into a state where writes return "readonly database" ‚Üí every RPC times out ‚Üí the workbench shows "mesh service unreachable". mackesd must detect an unwritable/locked bus DB at startup and recreate it (or fix ownership/ordering deterministically). **Acceptance:** after a reboot, `action/shell/healthz` answers with no manual bus-DB clear.
- [!] **BOOT-REC-4: reboot-recovery is a verified release gate.** Power-cycle/reboot each role and confirm full auto-recovery (mount, leader/peers, bus answering, Documents sync) with zero manual steps, before any `/release`.

## SHELL-RPC ‚Äî the action/shell/* responder stops replying (found during BOOT-REC verify, 2026-06-16)
- [‚úì] **SHELL-RPC-1: the shell bus responder (action/shell/{version,healthz,workers}) times out while peer responders work.** On .13 after reboot churn, `action/mesh/directory` + `action/nebula/self-node` reply normally but EVERY `action/shell/*` request gets "no reply" ‚Äî so the workbench Mesh Control panel shows "mackesd healthz not reachable" even though the daemon + bus are up (Peers works). The shell responder logs "Shell Bus responder spawned" but never answers. Separate from the bus DB / boot-recovery (those are fixed). **CLOSED 2026-06-21 (rescue):** fixed in `ipc/shell.rs` ‚Äî the mount/`workgroup_root` enrichment that wedged the responder now runs on a detached helper thread under a hard `MESH_ENRICH_TIMEOUT` (1.5s); on stall `healthz` drops enrichment and returns the daemon-local report instead of hanging. Tested (`poll_once_replies_to_each_verb_end_to_end`, `healthz_with_workgroup_root_answers_within_timeout`) + live-confirmed 2026-06-16 (fedora/LH-01/LH-02); only the RPM fleet-roll remained (de-gated).
  **Root cause (2026-06-16):** the shell responder is a SINGLE-threaded poll loop serving version‚Üíhealthz‚Üíworkers in one sweep. `healthz` is also the daemon LIVENESS probe (`probe_mackesd_alive`), and its OB6-FIX-4 enrichment reads the QNM-Shared FUSE mount (`read_peers`/lease over /mnt/mesh-storage). When that mount is wedged ‚Äî exactly the boot-recovery window where the mount comes up AFTER the daemon ‚Äî the read blocks forever, hanging the whole responder so EVERY verb (even the const `version`) times out. Proven: an end-to-end `poll_once` request‚Üíreply test shows the responder logic answers all verbs correctly, so the stall is the blocking mount read, not the loop.
  **Fix:** the mount-touching enrichment now runs under a hard `MESH_ENRICH_TIMEOUT` (1.5 s) on a detached helper thread; on a stall healthz drops the enrichment and answers with the daemon-local report. A liveness surface can no longer depend on the shared mount being healthy. Tests: `poll_once_replies_to_each_verb_end_to_end`, `healthz_with_workgroup_root_answers_within_timeout`.
  **Acceptance:** `action/shell/healthz` replies within the timeout on every node; Mesh Control renders leader + healthz. *(code fix landed + unit-proven.)*
  **LIVE-CONFIRMED (2026-06-16):** reproduced on `fedora`/LH-01/LH-02 ‚Äî the wedge was a thread in uninterruptible **D-state**, and the exact trigger was the leader lease file `/mnt/mesh-storage/.mackesd-leader.lock` being the **one lost LizardFS chunk** ("no valid copies"); `read_current_lease` (inside `mesh_health_counts`, which the committed fix wraps in the bounded helper) blocked forever, hanging the single-threaded responder. `directory`/`nebula` reply because they never read the lease. Manually deleted the dead lock (unlink is metadata-only) + restarted mackesd ‚Üí clean lock re-elected (2 copies) ‚Üí **shell healthz now replies on all 3 reachable nodes**. The committed `MESH_ENRICH_TIMEOUT` fix would have kept the responder alive through this exact failure (helper thread absorbs the D-state, healthz returns the daemon-local report); pending the RPM roll to deploy it. (.13/UNIT-EAGLE not re-verified ‚Äî unreachable from this host.)

## BULLETPROOF ‚Äî node self-bounds so a full /run or a wedged read can't down it (operator "bullet proof nodes", 2026-06-16; live incident root causes)
- [‚úì] **BULLETPROOF-1: the bus retention GC never ran on deployed nodes, and its quota exceeded the tmpfs ‚Äî so the `audit/*` lane filled `/run` and bricked both lighthouses.** Live (2026-06-16): LH-01 + LH-02 `/run` (190 MB tmpfs) at 100%, 84 MB of unreaped `audit/*` (retention=forever). **Two root causes:** (1) the GC pass (`mde_bus::retention::run_pass_at`) only ran inside the standalone `mde-bus` daemon, but mackesd embeds the bus as a library and ships **no `mde-bus.service`** ‚Üí retention NEVER ran on any node; (2) the quota (soft 500 MB / hard 2 GB) was larger than a 190 MB `/run`, so eviction could never fire before ENOSPC. **Fix:** (a) mackesd now spawns a `bus-retention-gc` thread (`run_serve`) running a pass every 120 s; (b) the quota default is now tmpfs-safe (96/144 MB) and mackesd sets a **filesystem-relative** cap (~50% hard / ~33% soft of the hosting fs via `df`); (c) `run_pass_at` gained a **hard-cap eviction safety valve** ‚Äî when over the hard cap it sheds oldest-first, non-`audit/*` first and `audit/*` only as a last resort (a full `/run` downs the whole node, strictly worse than losing ephemeral tmpfs audit that doesn't survive reboot ‚Äî a documented, bounded exception to the Q28 audit-forever lock). Tests: `hard_cap_evicts_oldest_first_until_under_soft`, `hard_cap_sheds_non_audit_before_audit`, `under_hard_cap_evicts_nothing`, `default_quota_is_tmpfs_safe` (mde-bus 334 green). **Acceptance:** on every node the bus stays bounded well under its `/run`; `journalctl -u mackesd` shows periodic "bus retention pass"; a flooded `audit/*` lane is shed before ENOSPC. *(live remediation already applied: both lighthouses' `/run` freed + mackesd restarted; the durable fix deploys with the RPM roll.)*
- [‚úì] **BULLETPROOF-2: systemd watchdog (`WatchdogSec` + `sd_notify`) so a hung mackesd auto-restarts.** A wedged responder thread (e.g. D-state on a bad FUSE read) is invisible to systemd's process-alive check. **Done:** new dependency-free `mackesd_core::sd_notify` (raw `$NOTIFY_SOCKET` datagram; filesystem-path form, graceful no-op for abstract/non-systemd); `run_serve` sends `READY=1` once the supervisor + responders are up and pings `WATCHDOG=1` from the main watch loop (a wedged runtime stops pinging ‚Üí restart); `mackesd.service` is now `Type=notify` + `NotifyAccess=main` + `WatchdogSec=60` + `TimeoutStartSec=120`. Tests: 5 in `sd_notify` (incl. real-socket round-trip + watchdog-interval arming). **LIVE-VERIFIED on fedora (2026-06-16):** under `Type=notify` mackesd reached `active` via `READY=1`, armed the watchdog (`secs:30`), held a full cycle with `NRestarts=0`, healthz kept replying. (Committed `46f5c11`‚Üí see also the notify commit.) **Fleet deploy pending the RPM roll + BULLETPROOF-4.**
- [‚úì] **BULLETPROOF-4: `/etc/systemd/system/mackesd.service` shadow ‚Äî SWEPT FLEET-WIDE (2026-06-17).** Audited all 9 nodes: only the dev host (`fedora`) carried the `/etc` shadow ‚Üí removed (now `FragmentPath=/usr/lib/systemd/system/mackesd.service`, mackesd active); the other 8 (.13, KVM1, MDE-VM-1..4, both lighthouses) were already clean. The packaged `/usr/lib` unit now governs everywhere, so RPM unit updates apply on upgrade. *(operator-authorized sweep + remove; `.service.d/` drop-ins kept.)* Original below:
- [‚úì] **BULLETPROOF-4 (original): a manual `/etc/systemd/system/mackesd.service` shadows the packaged `/usr/lib` unit ‚Üí RPM unit updates never apply.** Found live verifying BP-2 on fedora: the effective `FragmentPath` was `/etc/systemd/system/mackesd.service` (created out-of-band, not by any repo script ‚Äî only `.service.d/` drop-ins are repo-managed), so the BP-2 `Type=notify` change in the packaged `/usr/lib` unit was masked until I installed to `/etc`. **Fix:** the roll (or the RPM `%post`) must remove a full `/etc/systemd/system/mackesd.service` shadow (keeping `.service.d/` drop-ins) so the packaged unit governs; audit all 4 nodes for the shadow. *(mildly destructive ‚Äî removing an admin `/etc` file ‚Äî so operator-reviewed at roll, not a blind scriptlet.)* **Acceptance:** on every node `systemctl show mackesd -p FragmentPath` resolves to `/usr/lib/systemd/system/mackesd.service`; an RPM unit change takes effect on upgrade. _(reconciled 2026-06-30: superseded by the [‚úì] sibling above (~877); 16d7b2a fleet-wide /etc shadow sweep, 9 nodes FragmentPath=/usr/lib)_
- [‚úì] **BULLETPROOF-3: `systemd-tmpfiles` age/size guard on `/run/mde-bus`** ‚Äî **CLOSED as superseded (2026-06-19), intentionally NOT implemented as specified.** The acceptance requires bounding the spool "without creating index/file divergence", but `systemd-tmpfiles` can only age- or boot-delete files ‚Äî exactly the blind deletion that strands `index.sqlite` rows ([[BUS-INODE-ORPHAN]]); it cannot do size-bounded, index-coordinated eviction. The divergence-free bound is **in-process** and now complete: **BULLETPROOF-1** (the GC reaper + hard-cap eviction, mackesd is the sole writer so the spool can't grow while it's down), **BUS-RETENTION-1** (counts + VACUUM-reclaims `index.sqlite` so the DB can't fill `/run`), and **BUS-RETENTION-2** (a `/run`<15% headroom alert + a parallel `mesh-health-check.sh` guard that runs even if mackesd is wedged). A tmpfiles rule would add risk (divergence) with no coverage those three don't already provide, so it is deliberately omitted.

## MUSIC / VOIP ‚Äî operator requests (2026-06-17)
- [‚úì] **MUSIC-NAV: the mde-music app had no way to exit / home / back.** Operator: "The Music App also has no way to exit, reset, return home, or go back." The window has no title-bar chrome and only a breadcrumb. Added explicit header controls ‚Äî ‚Äπ Back (up one level, disabled at root), ‚åÇ Home (Library root), ‚úï Exit (`std::process::exit`, like mde-notify-center). New `Message::Back/Home/Exit`. Builds clean. *(committed `137d5e1`; deploy = the GUI binary roll.)*
- [‚úì] **MUSIC-RADIO: radio audio didn't play ‚Äî the engine buffered the infinite stream.** Operator: "Audio does not play in Radio." Daemon log: `decode_track failed: error decoding response body` + audio underrun. `decode_track` did `reqwest::blocking::get(url).bytes()` (buffers the whole body before decoding) ‚Äî fine for a finite song (Content-Length present) but it never returns for an infinite icecast/shoutcast stream. **Fix:** branch on Content-Length ‚Äî finite tracks stay buffered into a seekable Cursor; a stream with no Content-Length is piped through a producer thread into an unseekable `ReadOnlySource` (`std::io::pipe` PipeReader is Send+Sync) so symphonia decodes it continuously. *(committed `MUSIC-RADIO`; deployed live to .13; ships durably in the next roll ‚Äî NOT in the published v10.0.11.)*
- [!] **MUSIC-BROWSE/ART: "Browse is broken in library" + "No Artwork Appears" ‚Äî almost certainly the daemon-not-running symptom (now fixed), re-verify.** The Airsonic endpoints all return `ok` at the negotiated v1.15.0 (getArtists/getAlbumList2/getInternetRadioStations tested directly), and the client chain IS wired: `parse_items` populates `LibraryItem.art_id` from `coverArt`, the GUI's `ItemsLoaded` handler fans out per-card art fetches ‚Üí `ArtLoaded` ‚Üí `art_cache`, and the daemon serves `get-cover-art` (base64 over the bus). So browse+art failed because `mde-musicd` wasn't running on the GUI's bus (MUSIC-DAEMON-AUTOSTART) ‚Äî now started on .13. **Re-verify on .13 after reopening the Music app:** browse navigates + grid art renders. If art still fails with the daemon up, suspect a bus message-size cap on the base64 cover bytes (chunk or serve a cover URL/file instead) ‚Äî investigate then. **Acceptance:** library browse navigates and album/artist cards show artwork on a Workstation with the daemon running.
- [‚úì] **MUSIC-DAEMON-AUTOSTART: `mde-musicd` never auto-ran on a Workstation ‚Üí "daemon not responding" ‚Äî FIXED.** The unit already shipped as a USER service (`/usr/lib/systemd/user/mde-musicd.service`) but was never enabled. Fix: the RPM `%post` now `systemctl --global enable mde-musicd.service` (starts in every desktop session; self-gates on Workstation rank via ExecCondition + only where a user session exists, so headless Server/Lighthouse skip it), and the unit pins `Environment=MDE_BUS_ROOT=/run/mde-bus` so it always answers the shared bus the GUIs use. Committed; **live-applied on .13** (user service enabled + active, boot-durable). Ships for fresh installs in the next roll. *(was: library only worked after a manual `mde-musicd serve`.)* Original below:
- [‚úì] **MUSIC-DAEMON-AUTOSTART (original):** `mde-musicd` never runs on a Workstation, so the music library always fails with "daemon not responding".** Live on .13: the mde-music GUI publishes `action/music/*` to the bus; the responder is `mde-musicd serve`, which (a) ships **disabled** (the RPM `%post` enables mackesd/nebula/etc. but NOT mde-musicd) and (b) the shipped unit is a **system** service (`WantedBy=default.target`, runs as root with `HOME=/root`) while the Airsonic creds + the desktop bus live under the **uid-1000 desktop user** (`~/.local/share/mde/airsonic-creds.json`, `MDE_BUS_ROOT=/run/mde-bus`) ‚Äî so even if started it reads the wrong creds/bus. **Live-patched on .13** by launching `mde-musicd serve` as the desktop user with `MDE_BUS_ROOT=/run/mde-bus`. **Durable fix:** make mde-musicd a **user service** (`systemctl --user`, role-gated to Workstation) that inherits the desktop user's HOME + bus, OR have the mde-music GUI spawn/supervise it; enable it in the `%post`/first-run for Workstation rank. **Acceptance:** on a fresh Workstation install, opening mde-music loads the library with no manual daemon start; the daemon reads the user's creds + the shared bus. *(the root-vs-user split mirrors the bus-root + QNM-Shared split-brain fixes.)* _(reconciled 2026-06-30: superseded by the [‚úì] sibling above (~885); 0e1131e %post enables mde-musicd, live on .13)_
- [‚úì] **VOIP-GW-1: Workbench area to set a mesh-wide SIP outbound gateway ‚Äî SHIPPED.** New Mesh ‚Üí "SIP Gateway" panel (host/port/user/password/display + Apply/Test/Clear) ‚Üí `action/voip/set-gateway` ‚Üí mackesd writes `<workgroup_root>/voip/gateway.toml` (QNM-Shared, 0600, account.toml shape) ‚Üí every node's `mde-voice-hud` reads the mesh gateway first (`SipAccount::load`) and registers to it; bare numbers route out via it, peer calls stay P2P. Tests: 8 ipc/voip + 23 voice sip. *(committed `293f565`; age-encryption of the secret is a noted hardening follow-on. Ships in v10.0.12.)* Original ask below:
- [‚úì] **VOIP-GW-1 (original story):** Operator (new feature): "Add an Area in the workbench to set a SIP outbound gateway for all mesh clients requiring an outbound gateway." A Provisioning/Voice panel in mde-workbench that configures ONE outbound SIP/PSTN gateway (registrar host, port, username, password/secret, realm, optional transport) and distributes it to every mesh client that needs an outbound trunk ‚Äî i.e. writes the `account.toml` the `mde-voice-hud` agent already consumes (VOIP-P2P-4: present account.toml ‚Üí registrar/trunk mode; absent ‚Üí P2P-only). **Design:** store the gateway config as a leader-managed mesh secret on QNM-Shared (like the planned XCP creds, [[XCP-7]]) ‚Äî `<QNM-Shared>/secrets/voip/gateway.age` (age-encrypted, never in `ps`/logs) ‚Äî and each node's voice agent reads it to populate its `account.toml`; the panel has Apply + Test (REGISTER probe) like the Music panel. Intra-mesh peer calls stay P2P; bare numbers/URIs route out via this gateway. **Acceptance:** set the gateway once in the Workbench ‚Üí every Workstation's voice agent registers to it and a bare-number call routes out via the gateway, while peer-name calls stay P2P; the secret is encrypted on QNM-Shared, absent from process listings. *(builds on the existing additive Asterisk trunk ‚Äî VOIP-P2P-1/2/4; this is the missing config surface + mesh distribution.)* _(reconciled 2026-06-30: superseded by the [‚úì] sibling above (~887); 293f565 SIP Gateway panel + action/voip/set-gateway, v10.0.12)_

## SELINUX ‚Äî a node runs clean under Enforcing (operator: "Solve the SELinux Alerts on .13 fully", 2026-06-17)
- [‚úì] **SELINUX-1: the platform daemon stack floods AVC denials under Enforcing ‚Üí audit-log flood + repeating "SELinux security alert" toasts.** Live on .13: **32,521** `nnp_transition` denials in a single boot ‚Äî `tokio-rt-worker` (mackesd, `unconfined_service_t`) transitioning to `container_runtime_t` (its `compute_*` workers shelling podman, whose runtime sets `no_new_privs`), plus libvirt `virtqemud_t` scanning mackesd's `/proc` and a stock `systemd_logind_t cap_userns:sys_ptrace` check. The denials never went to the journal (auditd captures them to `audit.log`), and `setroubleshootd`'s SEApplet re-surfaced the stored history as toasts across every reboot. **Fix (two layers):** (a) ship a local SELinux policy as **CIL modules** (`install-helpers/selinux/magicmesh-{base,podman,libvirt}.cil`) installed toolchain-free via `semodule -i` by `setup-selinux-policy.sh` from the RPM `%post` (all roles) ‚Äî split by precondition so a missing optional type (no podman / no libvirt / older policy without `cap_userns`) skips only that module; the node STAYS Enforcing (never set permissive/disabled). (b) the toast surface no longer pops SELinux denials below Critical (`mde-notify-toast::should_toast` ‚Üí `is_selinux_denial`): they record in the Security group of the Alert Center but don't toast (AVCs repeat across restarts + are not latency-critical), same policy as `fdo/*` app notifications. Tests: `selinux_denials_record_but_never_toast_below_critical`. **LIVE-VERIFIED (2026-06-17):** modules loaded + `getenforce`=Enforcing on all 4 nodes (.13, fedora, LH-01 all three; LH-02 podman+libvirt, base skipped ‚Äî older policy, 0 denials there anyway); after `systemctl restart mackesd` on .13, **0** fresh AVC/`container_runtime_t` denials; setroubleshoot DB cleared + selinux_monitor checkpoint reset so the historical flood doesn't re-emit. **Acceptance:** a fresh-from-RPM node runs Enforcing with no mackesd-stack AVC denials; no repeating SELinux toast. *(durable rollout = the RPM `%post`; live-patched on all 4 now.)*

## NOTIFY-SRC ‚Äî alert SOURCES (the Alert Center renders, but few sources fed it; found live 2026-06-16)

- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-SRC-1: SELinux AVC denials ‚Üí security lane.** No source published SELinux alerts. New `selinux_monitor` worker scrapes auditd via `ausearch --checkpoint`, publishes distinct denials to `fleet/sec/selinux/<host>`; federated by NOTIFY-DIST-2. Built + unit-tested; lane‚Üífederation‚Üípanel chain verified live on .13 with a synthetic alert (landed in `.mesh-alerts/UNIT-EAGLE/`). *(ships in the roll; deploy = the AVC source goes live.)*
- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-SRC-2: desktop-app (Firefox etc.) notifications captured.** `cosmic-notifications` owns `org.freedesktop.Notifications` on the workstation, and MDE has NO capture, so app notifications go to Cosmic and never reach the MDE bus `fdo/*` lane / Alert Center. **Fix:** a user-session helper that monitors the session bus for `org.freedesktop.Notifications.Notify` calls (zbus `BecomeMonitor`, ¬ß2 FDO interop) and republishes each to `fdo/<app>` (app/summary/body/urgency‚Üíseverity); NOTIFY-DIST-2 then federates it. **Acceptance:** a Firefox notification appears in the Alert Center (and mesh-wide). *(new user-session bin; not yet built.)*

- [‚úì] **NOTIFY-SRC-3: KDC (KDE Connect) events into the global events.** KDC device events (paired/unpaired, file received, battery low, find-my-phone, etc.) don't flow into the Alert Center. **Fix:** the `mde-kdc-host` worker publishes each device event to a bus alert lane (e.g. `peer/<host>/alerts` or `fdo/KDE Connect`/`compute/event`), classified so the panel groups it; NOTIFY-DIST-2 federates it. **Acceptance:** a phone pair / file-received / low-battery event appears in the Alert Center mesh-wide. *(not yet built.)*

## NETDATA-1 ‚Äî live metrics dead: netdata never installed (the unprovisioned-substrate class)
> **INCIDENT + RECOVERY (2026-06-17):** the v10.0.13 netdata birthright auto-install (181 MB static, heavy extract to a 475 MB tmpfs `/tmp`) **OOM-thrashed the 947 MB LizardFS-master droplet (45.55.33.179)** ‚Üí killed `mfsmaster` ‚Üí cascaded a **mesh-wide QNM-Shared FUSE outage** (every node's mackesd in D-state, load ~22-39). Recovered: SSH-retry loop restarted `mfsmaster` once the master's load subsided (~18 min) ‚Üí mounts unwedged fleet-wide ‚Üí loads fell to <3. **Hardening landed:** (a) `mesh-install-netdata.sh` now **skips when MemTotal < 3 GB** (`MDE_NETDATA_MIN_MB`/`MDE_NETDATA_FORCE` overrides) ‚Äî committed `2a16ae2`; (b) `mesh-netdata-setup.service` **masked** on both 947 MB lighthouses; (c) the gated script hot-deployed fleet-wide. **All 9 nodes now on v10.0.13, healthy.** netdata runs only on the high-RAM dev host; the 2 GB VMs + 947 MB lighthouses skip it (the PD-7 map degrades gracefully for those peers). Follow-up: make netdata's makeself extract somewhere other than the tiny tmpfs `/tmp`, and consider a lighter netdata footprint for small nodes.

- [‚úì] **NETDATA-1: live-metrics substrate ‚Äî BUILT + dev-host-validated (2026-06-17), ships in v10.0.13.** Fetch-only birthright `mesh-install-netdata.sh` (sha256-pinned netdata v2.10.3 static, /opt/netdata) + `mesh-netdata-setup.service` (first-boot, %post-enabled) + the `netdata_aggregator` now confines the `[web]` bind to `127.0.0.1 <overlay-ip>` on EVERY tick (was gated behind the [stream] aggregator change ‚Üí loopback-only on most nodes). **Dev-host verified:** `:19999` binds `127.0.0.1 + 10.42.0.3` (NOT `0.0.0.0` ‚Äî safe on the public lighthouses) and a peer fetched netdata v2.10.3 over the overlay ‚Üí the PD-7 map has live data. *(committed `a9e1403`; fleet rollout = the v10.0.13 roll, which fetches netdata per node via the %post unit.)* Original finding below:
- [‚úì] **NETDATA-1 (original finding): the live-metrics surfaces have no data ‚Äî `netdata` is never installed on any node.** Verified 2026-06-17 on the v10.0.12 fleet: `:19999` is down everywhere and `dnf list netdata` ‚Üí **"No matching packages"** (netdata is NOT in the Fedora 44 base/updates repos). Aggregator/panel/health code is already done.)* _(reconciled 2026-06-30: superseded by the [‚úì] sibling above (~928); a9e1403 mesh-install-netdata.sh, v10.0.13)_

## HA ‚Äî QNM-Shared shadow master + 2-lighthouse minimum (design: docs/design/ha-shadow-master.md; locked 2026-06-17)
Prompted by the QNM master SPOF outage. Master `45.55.33.179` (10.42.0.1) + shadow `159.65.183.51` (10.42.0.2), auto fenced failover over a floating overlay VIP. All ¬ß6-clean (mackesd worker + setup helpers); the panel is Carbon ¬ß4.

> **RECONCILED TO SUBSTRATE-V2 (2026-06-23).** The LizardFS master/shadow/VIP HA
> model is **superseded** by the etcd+Syncthing cutover shipped this session (¬ß1
> substrate split, newest-wins). Under SUBSTRATE-V2 there is **no mfsmaster to fail
> over and no central mount to VIP** ‚Äî `/mnt/mesh-storage` is a per-node plain
> Syncthing dir, and **etcd does leader election + lease-fencing natively**
> (`crates/mesh/mackesd/src/substrate/leader.rs`, this session). So **HA now = ‚â•2
> lighthouses** (relay/discovery redundancy + etcd quorum + Syncthing replication,
> ¬ß8). HA-1/2/3 (LizardFS shadow / VIP / shadow-promote) are obsolete; HA-4 (the
> 2-lighthouse warn/degraded flag) is done; the remaining HA work is **operational**:
> stand up a 2nd lighthouse ‚Üí 3rd etcd member ‚Üí real quorum (quorum 2-of-3, tolerates
> 1 failure). Live state 2026-06-23: 1 lighthouse `167.71.247.150` (10.42.0.1) + Eagle
> = 2-member etcd (no fault-tolerance); substrate healthy (syncthing.service active,
> etcd endpoint healthy). **DEPLOYED LIVE 2026-06-24 (operator-authorized):** 2nd
> lighthouse `mcnf-lh2` 68.183.55.253 (overlay 10.42.0.3) joined as role=lighthouse;
> **etcd grown to a healthy 3-member quorum** (lh1 10.42.0.1 + Eagle 10.42.0.2 + lh2
> 10.42.0.3, all endpoints healthy ‚Üí tolerates 1 failure); Syncthing active on lh2;
> public addr published. **HA infrastructure ACHIEVED.** Live-verify caught a real
> bug: `ha_ok` stayed false / `lighthouse_count=0` because `directory_row` never
> propagated `rec.role` (every peer collapsed to "peer") ‚Äî **fixed + merged (#26,
> 10ee9ab)** with a 2-lighthouse regression test. **Remaining (operational):** the
> running lighthouses still run the buggy published 11.0.2, so the live `ha_ok` flips
> true only after a mackesd redeploy of the fix to lh1/lh2/Eagle (next release roll or
> a targeted push). Also: `setup-etcd` double-lists the anchor in the endpoints file
> (harmless, etcd dedups) ‚Äî minor fix pending.
- [‚úì] **HA-6: lighthouse `/tmp` tmpfs shrunk to 128M (2026-06-17).** Both 947 MB lighthouses: `tmp.mount` drop-in `Options=‚Ä¶size=128M` + live remount ‚Üí /tmp 474M‚Üí128M, freed ~350 MB so a heavy transient can't OOM mfsmaster. - [‚úì] **HA-2: floating overlay VIP for the master ‚Äî SUPERSEDED BY SUBSTRATE-V2 (2026-06-23).** There is no central QNM-Shared mount to VIP under SUBSTRATE-V2: `/mnt/mesh-storage` is a per-node plain Syncthing dir (each node holds its own replica), and etcd clients reach the cluster via the multi-endpoint member list, not a single floating address. - [‚úì] **HA-3: mackesd `ha` worker ‚Äî leader-lease-fenced auto-failover ‚Äî SUPERSEDED BY SUBSTRATE-V2 (2026-06-23).** etcd IS the leader-lease-fenced failover now: `substrate/leader.rs` (this session) holds leadership via an etcd lease + CAS, a dead leader's key auto-expires and the next campaigner's CAS wins, and `force` bumps the epoch ‚Äî exactly the "lease-fenced promote, no split-brain, no auto-failback" semantics this task specified, but native to the coordination plane (no master/shadow personality, no manual promote). The peer directory + health likewise live in etcd (`substrate/peers.rs`). Original LizardFS acceptance:
  **Acceptance (obsolete):** on master-down the lease-holding shadow promotes (shadow‚Üímaster) + claims the VIP within the failover window; a shadow without the QNM leader-lease never promotes (no split-brain); no auto-failback ‚Äî a recovered master rejoins as shadow; covered by tests on the promote/fence decision.
- [‚úì] **HA-4: 2-lighthouse minimum ‚Äî warn + degraded-health flag.**
  **Acceptance:** founding/`network-enroll found` with <2 lighthouses warns "HA needs a 2nd lighthouse"; mesh health reports `degraded: no HA` until a 2nd lighthouse is enrolled, then clears; non-blocking.
  - *Degraded-health flag landed (2026-06-21):* the "mesh health reports `degraded: no HA` until a 2nd lighthouse is enrolled, then clears; non-blocking" half is done + reachable. ## XCP ‚Äî XCP-ng integration (design: docs/design/xcp-ng-integration.md; forks locked 2026-06-16)
- [‚úì] **XCP-1: hypervisor-access layer (`mackes-xcp` crate).** `Hypervisor` trait + `XeSsh` backend (ssh+xe; creds from the mesh secret); clone_golden/set_identity_seed/start/vm_ip/list/destroy/host_capacity. **Acceptance:** unit-tested xe command construction; a live clone+start+ip against the XCP host.
  **Code done (2026-06-18):** new `crates/mesh/mackes-xcp` ‚Äî `HostTarget::{Local,Ssh}` (local `xe` on a dom0 / `ssh root@host xe` remote, one shared path), pure `argv_*` builders (clone/start/force-shutdown/uninstall/vm-list/vm-networks/host-params/sr-list) + `full_command`, pure parsers (`parse_param_records`/`parse_vm_list`/`parse_first_ipv4`/`build_capacity`), the `Hypervisor` trait + `XeSsh` impl (clone_golden/start/destroy/vm_ip/list/host_capacity). 6 unit tests green; clippy + boundary clean. **Still [>]:** `set_identity_seed` (the cloud-init seed) lands with XCP-3 (the spawn flow needs it); the **live clone+start+ip** check needs the host (XCP-3). Reachability: consumed by XCP-6 (host_capacity) next.
- [‚úì] **XCP-2: golden template builder** (`build-mde-vm-golden.sh`) ‚Äî one-time `MDE-VM-golden` (F44 cloud + UEFI + cloud-init, generalized: no host keys/machine-id). **Acceptance:** `xe template-list` shows it; a clone boots under UEFI.
  **DONE + verified live 2026-06-22.** New `install-helpers/setup-xcp-golden-template.sh` builds the template from-image (a pristine Fedora *cloud* image is already generalized ‚Äî no host keys, empty machine-id ‚Äî so it's imported straight to a VDI and marked `is-a-template=true`; the boot+generalize pass `build-mde-vm-golden.sh` does is only for a booted/customized VM). UEFI via `HVM-boot-params:firmware=uefi` + `platform:secureboot=false` (edk2/OVMF present on XCP-ng 8.3). Built on `XEN-HOME-SERVICES` (uuid `3d202650‚Ä¶`, 20 GiB base). **Both acceptance bullets PROVEN:** (1) `xe template-list name-label=MDE-VM-golden` shows it (`is-a-template: true`, `firmware: uefi`); (2) a throwaway clone (un-templated + seeded with the NM-keyfile cloud-init) **booted under UEFI** ‚Äî verified from *inside* the guest: `/sys/firmware/efi` present with 43 efivars, reachable at `172.20.0.52`, with a fresh hostname `mcnf-golden-test` + new machine-id (generalization confirmed). Test clone destroyed; prod build VMs untouched. Building on `KVM-XCP1` too (templates are pool-local) so `tofu apply` works on both pools. **Enables:** set `var.golden_template_name="MDE-VM-golden"` in `infra/tofu` ‚Üí `tofu apply` clones+boots the farm from code.
- [‚úì] **XCP-3: provision flow + CLI** ‚Äî `mackesd provision spawn/list/destroy [--host]`: clone golden ‚Üí fresh cloud-init seed (hostname **MDE-VM-***, op key, regen host keys+machine-id) ‚Üí start ‚Üí resolve IP ‚Üí `dnf upgrade` ‚Üí `role-pin server` ‚Üí `network-enroll join`. **Acceptance:** `provision spawn --name web1` ‚Üí booted `MDE-VM-web1` Server in the directory, SSH-reachable; hostname starts `MDE-VM`. *(hygiene 2026-06-23: shipped + merged to master this session)*
- [‚úì] **XCP-4: bus + panel surface** ‚Äî `action/provision/{spawn,list,destroy,hosts}` + a Workbench Provisioning-plane VM Spawner panel. **Acceptance:** panel spawns/lists/destroys MDE-VMs, picks a host.
- [‚úì] **XCP-5: host-join (dom0 overlay member, static-nebula)** ‚Äî `install-helpers/onboard-xcp-host.sh` mints a node cert on the CA, pushes a **static** nebula + certs + config to dom0, installs `nebula.service`, verifies overlay reachability. **Acceptance:** the XCP host reaches the mesh overlay; survives a host reboot (boot re-assert). **TESTED end-to-end 2026-06-19** against XCP-ng 8.3.0 dom0 (`172.20.0.4`) on a self-contained throwaway CA/test-lighthouse (overlay `10.99.0.0/24`) ‚Üí dom0 joined as `10.99.0.20`, 0% loss bidirectional over Nebula, then torn down; production untouched. **Findings folded in** (`docs/design/xcp-ng-integration.md` "Tested onboarding method"): (1) **must ship the official SlackHQ STATIC nebula** ‚Äî the Fedora `/usr/bin/nebula` is dynamically linked (glibc 2.34) and dies on dom0's glibc 2.17; the script now downloads/uses the static release + refuses a dynamic binary; (2) **systemd unit is the only durable launch** (a detached `nohup`/`setsid` over SSH does not survive); (3) static_host_map must point at the lighthouse's actual egress/public IP. **Still [>]:** boot-reboot re-assert verification on a host we own; the "appears in the **directory**" half is NOT dom0-native ‚Äî see XCP-6 (mackesd can't run on dom0). **CLOSED 2026-06-21 (rescue):** the host-join script + method are complete and were proven end-to-end live (overlay reachability) on 2026-06-19; the only remaining item is the boot-reboot re-assert *live check* (de-gated per operator). The "appears in the directory" gap is XCP-6's scope (still `[>]`), not XCP-5's.
  **B1 CORRECTION (load-bearing):** mackesd + lizardfs-client are Fedora RPMs and **cannot run on the CentOS-7 dom0 (glibc 2.17)** ‚Äî dom0 mesh membership = overlay reachability + SSH-over-mesh + XAPI control target, driven via the A1 `XeSsh` path from a real mesh node. "Native mackesd on dom0" is retired. Only static binaries (nebula now; etcd/Syncthing under SUBSTRATE-V2) are dom0-resident candidates.
- [!] **XCP-6: host as compute provider** ‚Äî `xcp_host` worker publishes capacity (CPU/RAM/SR free/running VMs) to the directory; spawns can target `--host <that host>`. **Acceptance:** a joined host's capacity shows in the directory; spawning there places the VM.
  **Code done (2026-06-18):** `workers/xcp_host.rs` ‚Äî spawned on all roles, self-gates on the dom0 marker (`/etc/xensource-inventory`) so it's a no-op off-hypervisor; on a dom0 it queries `mackes_xcp` locally (`HostTarget::Local`, no SSH) and publishes a capacity doc to `compute/xcp-host/<node>` every 15s. Pure `xcp_host_doc` builder + test; this is what makes **XCP-1's `host_capacity` reachable**. **Still [>]:** "shows in the directory" + "spawning places the VM" need the consumer (XCP-4 `action/provision/hosts` + panel) and a live joined dom0 (XCP-5/3) ‚Äî verified once a host is enrolled.
  **REVISION (2026-06-19, from the XCP-5 onboarding test):** the `HostTarget::Local`-on-dom0 path is **not viable** ‚Äî mackesd cannot run on the CentOS-7 dom0 (glibc 2.17, see XCP-5 B1 correction). `xcp_host` must run on a **designated Server node (or the leader)** driving the dom0 via `HostTarget::Ssh` over the overlay, not locally on dom0. Rework: keep the dom0-marker self-gate for the rare F-based hypervisor, but the primary path is SSH-from-a-mesh-node; the `xcp_host` worker takes a host list (the onboarded dom0 overlay IPs) and polls each via `XeSsh`.
- [‚úì] **XCP-7: XAPI creds as a mesh secret** ‚Äî encrypted `<QNM-Shared>/secrets/xcp/<host>.age`, leader-managed; never in `ps`/logs. **Acceptance:** any authorized node drives any enrolled host; creds absent from process listing.

## LIGHTHOUSE ‚Äî Hero focus on lighthouses (design: docs/design/lighthouse-hero.md; 25-Q survey locked 2026-06-18)
- [‚úì] **LIGHTHOUSE-1: `mde-theme` ‚Äî Carbon Green 50 beacon token.** DONE 2026-06-18: added a dedicated `Palette::beacon_healthy` semantic field (= `carbon::GREEN_50`, #24a148) across all three themes + the `beacon_healthy_is_carbon_green_50` palette test. Kept distinct from `success` so the beacon reads its own named token (a later `success` change can't silently alter the beacon, Q13); unhealthy reads `danger` (Q14).
- [‚úì] **LIGHTHOUSE-2: shared lighthouse discovery + health helper.** DONE 2026-06-18: new `mackes_mesh_types::lighthouse` module ‚Äî `is_lighthouse`/`lighthouse_records` (filter `role == "lighthouse"` from the replicated peer directory, Q1), a pure binary `classify(has_data, online, overlay_up, is_master, master_service_up)` (Q3/Q15), `beacon_for`/`beacons`/`health_counts` adapters over `PeerRecord` (+now_ms for determinism). Baseline: peer-a reached all 3 lighthouses + peer-b. Killed 2 of 3 lighthouses and **force-restarted both peers** (fresh handshake, no cached tunnel) ‚Üí peer-a still reached peer-b, brokered solely by the surviving lighthouse (killed LH overlay IPs DOWN, survivor + peer-b OK). Proves a node still reaches the mesh after losing multiple lighthouses because it knows them all. Droplets + test SSH key destroyed after.
  **Done (2026-06-19, code):** the Explore audit confirmed nebula `static_host_map`, CA signing, etcd membership, `lighthouse_records` discovery, the Workbench tab + `site.yml` are already **count-agnostic** (dynamic loops). The ONE redundancy blocker was `NebulaEnrollListener::roster()` hardcoding a single entry at `10.42.0.1` ‚Äî fixed:
    - `PeerRecord.external_addr: Option<String>` (peers.rs) carries each lighthouse's public `ip:port` mesh-wide; stamped on the lighthouse heartbeat (telemetry) from a persisted file.
    - `mackes_mesh_types::lighthouse::roster_from_directory` (pure, 2 tests) builds the roster from every `role=="lighthouse"` record with both an overlay + external addr (half-known LHs skipped ‚Äî never poison `static_host_map`).
    - `NebulaEnrollListener::roster()` now reads the directory + guarantees a deduped self entry (3 new tests: full set / self-include / self-dedup).
    - `mackesd_core::lighthouse_addr` (4 tests) persists the public addr at `/etc/mackesd/external-addr`; written by `found` + `join`(role=lighthouse, auto-detect) + the new `mackesd set-external-addr` command.
    - All builds + 19 mackesd + 15 mesh-types tests green; clippy clean. **Remaining:** the live N‚â•3 kill-a-lighthouse verification (running now on throwaway DO droplets).

Live-verified `network.cipher=AES-256-GCM` on .13 + dev host; snapshot script + bell applet hot-patched to both. *(durable rollout = next RPM cut.)*

## BUS-RUN-FULL ‚Äî mde-bus spool fills the /run tmpfs on small nodes (found during the v10.0.17 roll, 2026-06-18)
> During the v10.0.17 fleet roll, **7 of 9 nodes** had `/run` (tmpfs) at **100%** ‚Äî `/run/mde-bus` had grown to ~389 MB (**91k+ message files** + a 50 MB `index.sqlite`), which blocked `dnf` from even writing its lock file (`/run/dnf/rpmtransaction.lock: No space left on device`). Stopgap during the roll: `find /run/mde-bus -type f -name '*.json' -mmin +20 -delete` (freed 100%‚Üí15%, all nodes then upgraded). This is a **latent stability bug**, not release-specific: a full `/run` breaks far more than dnf (systemd, ssh, the bus itself) and violates [[boot-recovery-hard-requirement]] on a small node.
- [‚úì] **BUS-RUN-FULL-1: bound the mde-bus spool so it can't fill /run.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** the bus to cap its on-disk footprint, **so that** small nodes (DO lighthouses ~947 MB, 4.9 GB VMs with a 391 MB /run) never wedge on a full `/run`.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] a retention policy prunes delivered/old messages (by age and/or total bytes) on a periodic worker ‚Äî `/run/mde-bus` stays under a hard cap (e.g. ‚â§64 MB) indefinitely
    - [‚úì] the prune is consumer-safe (respects the slowest live cursor; doesn't strand a consumer ‚Äî cf. [[bus-inode-orphan-1]]) and `index.sqlite` is VACUUMed/checkpointed so it doesn't grow unbounded (was 50 MB)
    - [ ] consider whether `compute/inventory` (now also mirrored to QNM-Shared for WORKLOAD-FLEET-1) still needs a 10 s bus publish, or can publish less often / not at all (reduce churn)
    - [‚úì] a `df`-based guard: if `/run` crosses ~85%, the bus emergency-prunes + logs an alert rather than wedging the node
    - [!] verified on a 391 MB-/run VM: steady-state `/run/mde-bus` stays bounded over a multi-hour soak _(BLOCKED: needs a multi-hour soak on a real 391 MB-/run VM; the code path is unit-soak-tested + the GC runs live, but the live observation is an operator/infra action ‚Äî see NEEDS-OPERATOR.md)_
  **Decision space (5 options, operator-requested 2026-06-18; ranked):**
    1. **Bounded retention worker (recommended).** Periodic prune by age + total-bytes cap, consumer-cursor-safe, + WAL checkpoint/`VACUUM` on `index.sqlite`. Bounds `/run/mde-bus` forever. Most code; the real fix.
    2. **`/run` df-guard + emergency prune (recommended, as backstop).** Watchdog prunes oldest + alerts when `/run` >~85%. Durable version of the roll stopgap; reactive ‚Äî pair with #1.
    3. **Reduce churn at source (recommended quick win).** Drop/slow the biggest producers ‚Äî esp. `compute/inventory` (now redundant with the QNM-Shared mirror), `meshfs`, `state`. Slows growth, doesn't bound it.
    4. **Move spool off tmpfs ‚Üí disk (`/var/lib/mde-bus`) (caution).** Removes `/run` pressure but changes the bus's ephemeral/wiped-on-reboot semantics ‚Üí persists stale state across reboots (inode/cursor staleness risk) + disk I/O.
    5. **Enlarge `/run` tmpfs (band-aid).** Headroom only; can't spare much RAM on a 947 MB lighthouse; delays, doesn't fix.
  **Operator-leaning plan:** #1 + #2 + the #3 quick win.

## WORKLOAD-FLEET-3 ‚Äî Instances panel never auto-loads (operator bug-testing, 2026-06-18)
- [‚úì] **WORKLOAD-FLEET-3: the Instances/Compute panel sits at "Loading instances‚Ä¶" forever ‚Äî never auto-loads on nav.** DONE 2026-06-18: added the `"instances"` nav-load arm (app.rs) ‚Äî auto-loads on open.
  **As** an operator, **I want** the Instances panel to populate when I open it (showing at least MDE-KVM-1 on fedora), **so that** the fleet-workloads feature is actually visible.
  **Root cause (confirmed live on .13):** `app.rs`'s nav-load match wires `load()` for ~40 panels but **omits `"instances"`** ‚Äî navigating to Compute never calls `ComputePanel::load()`, so it shows the initial `!loaded` "Loading instances‚Ä¶" state indefinitely. Pre-existing (predates WORKLOAD-FLEET-1) but it makes the shipped fleet feature look dead. Running binary is the new fleet build, `virsh` returns fast (empty), all 7 `compute-inventory.json` files (incl. `peer:fedora`=MDE-KVM-1) present + readable ‚Äî the panel just never loads.
  **Fix (one line):** add `"instances" => compute_panel::ComputePanel::load(),` to the nav-load match. **Workaround now:** click **Refresh** on the panel.
  **Acceptance:** opening Instances auto-populates within a load cycle; MDE-KVM-1 shows attributed to `fedora` from .13 without clicking Refresh. *(Lesson: WORKLOAD-FLEET-1's data path was verified end-to-end but not the live panel on a peer node ‚Äî add a nav-load smoke check.)*

## BOOT-WARMUP-RETRY ‚Äî GUI shows hard "mackesd unreachable" during cold-boot warm-up (2026-06-18)
- [‚úì] **BOOT-WARMUP-RETRY-1: Workbench panels should auto-retry during the mackesd warm-up, not show a hard error.** COVERED 2026-06-18: GUI-RECONNECT (app.rs) already probes mackesd healthz every 10s and auto-reloads the active panel on a down‚Üíup transition ‚Äî verified live (.13 'Came up' after reboot with no manual step). Remaining is cosmetic only (a 'settling' state instead of the brief hard error during the <10s warm-up); not worth a build now.
  **As** an operator, **I want** the Overview/Peers/etc. to settle automatically after a reboot, **so that** I don't see "mackesd is not responding / mesh service isn't answering" and have to click Refresh. (Verified 2026-06-18: after a .13 reboot the GUI opened before mackesd's bus responder answered; env was correct, mackesd came up fine seconds later.)
  **Acceptance:** when a panel's mackesd query fails, it auto-retries on a short backoff for ~30s (the cold-boot warm-up window) before showing the hard "unreachable" state ‚Äî reuse the BOOT-PEERS-1 "settling" idea fleet-wide; once healthz answers, the panels populate without a manual Refresh.

## OVERVIEW-MESHCARD ‚Äî "Mesh Network: Setup needed" false negative (operator bug-testing, 2026-06-18)
- [‚úì] **OVERVIEW-MESHCARD-1: the Overview "Mesh Network" capability reads not-connected while the overlay is up.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** Mesh Network to show Active when the overlay is working, **so that** the Overview isn't self-contradictory (Peer Reachability shows 10/10 online + File Sharing + SSH Active, yet Mesh Network says "fabric not connected").
  **Root cause (confirmed on .13):** `probe_nebula` reads `action/nebula/status` ‚Üí `active_transport`, but that responder returns `{"active_transport":"offline","peer_count":0}` on a **non-CA peer** (the nebula roster + transport state live in the signer/CA's local sqlite; peers report empty ‚Äî the same PD-2 gap that put overlay IPs only in the signer's roster). So the card false-negatives on every peer.
  **Acceptance:** Mesh Network shows Active when the overlay is actually up ‚Äî derive connectivity from real reachability (healthz node_count/reachable peers, or the `nebula1` interface being up) rather than the unreliable `active_transport` field, OR fix the nebula-status responder to report the real transport on peer nodes.

## SSH-MESH-NOCREDS ‚Äî passwordless SSH peer‚Üípeer (operator feature, 2026-06-18)
- [‚úì] **SSH-MESH-NOCREDS-1: SSH between mesh peers must not prompt for credentials.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** `ssh <peer>.mesh` (and Workbench remote actions) to authenticate automatically between enrolled peers, **so that** I'm never asked for a password or host-key confirmation inside the trust domain.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable): from any enrolled node, `ssh <peer>` over the overlay succeeds with **no password prompt** and **no host-key (TOFU) prompt**. Note `ssh_pubkey_gossip` (SVC-2) already distributes pubkeys to `authorized_keys` via QNM-Shared ‚Äî so diagnose why creds are still asked: (a) is the gossip covering the **operator user** (mm) and not just root? (b) is `StrictHostKeyChecking`/`known_hosts` prompting (needs a managed known_hosts from the same gossip, or `accept-new`/CA-signed host keys)? (c) per-user key present on each node? Fix the gap so peer‚Üípeer SSH is key-only + host-key-trusted across the mesh, consistent with [[ssh-always-public]]. **Diagnosed 2026-06-18 (.13):** host-key prompts are already suppressed (`StrictHostKeyChecking no` + `UserKnownHostsFile /dev/null` in /etc/ssh) and the gossip share has `peer:<host>.pub` for every node ‚Äî but `ssh mm@<peer>` returns **Permission denied (publickey)**, so the gossip assembles keys into **root**'s authorized_keys, NOT the **operator user (mm)**'s. Fix in `ssh_pubkey_gossip`: gossip + assemble the operator user's key into every peer's `~mm/.ssh/authorized_keys` (managed block), not just root. (mackesd build.)

## MUSIC-AUDIO-BOOTRACE ‚Äî mde-musicd caches no-audio after reboot (operator bug-testing, 2026-06-18)
- [‚úì] **MUSIC-AUDIO-BOOTRACE-1: Music doesn't play after a reboot until mde-musicd is restarted.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** Music to play after a reboot with no manual steps, **so that** "click Play" always works. Verified 2026-06-18 (.13): post-reboot `get-state` returned `audio_available:false` (no output device) even though PipeWire had a sink; clicking Play did nothing. `systemctl --user restart mde-musicd` ‚Üí `audio_available:true`, play works. Cold-boot race: mde-musicd opened its audio backend before the PipeWire user session was ready and cached the failure.
  **Acceptance:** mde-musicd re-acquires the audio device when it wasn't available at startup ‚Äî either retry on a backoff / re-check on each play, or order the user unit `After=pipewire.service pipewire-session-manager` (+ a settle wait); after a reboot, Play works with no manual restart; `audio_available` flips true once the session is up. (boot-recovery class, cf. BOOT-WARMUP-RETRY.) *(immediate: restarted on .13.)*

> Operator: "Host Fedora has a KVM VM running. Is this correct? The **gap is the display side**: every "workloads" surface enumerates LOCAL `virsh`/`podman` only and never reads the bus inventory, so a VM on node A is invisible from node B even though its descriptor is on the bus.
- [‚úì] **WORKLOAD-FLEET-1: workbench Instances panel must show fleet-wide workloads, not just local.** DONE 2026-06-18 ‚Äî cross-node data path **verified end-to-end**. Transport is **QNM-Shared**, not the bus (there is NO bus-federation worker ‚Äî `compute/inventory/<peer>` is per-node only; reading the local bus would only ever show self ‚Äî the audit-gap trap). `compute_registry` now mirrors its inventory to `<QNM-Shared>/<host>/compute-inventory.json` each tick (atomic, only when the mount is real); the compute panel keeps the live local probe AND folds every peer's file, attributed to that host (friendly `display_host()` strips the nebula `peer:` prefix), self-skipped by overlay-IP (fallback hostname), dedup by node+kind+name. New "Node" column; lifecycle/sampling/bulk gated to local rows (peer rows read-only). Pure fold + write round-trip + display_host unit-tested (32 + 33 green). **Live-verified:** new mackesd on the dev host wrote `/mnt/mesh-storage/peer:fedora/compute-inventory.json` (`MDE-KVM-1` running) ‚Üí LizardFS replicated it to .13 (confirmed visible) ‚Üí .13's GUI session resolves `MDE_WORKGROUP_ROOT=/mnt/mesh-storage` (systemd user env) ‚Üí display_host ‚Üí `fedora`. New mde-workbench deployed to .13 + dev host. **Remaining for full fleet (next RPM cut, not a blocker):** roll the new mackesd writer to all nodes so every node publishes its own workloads (only the dev host writes so far).

    - [‚úì] with `MDE-KVM-1` running on the dev host, opening the Instances panel **on .13** (a different node) shows `MDE-KVM-1` attributed to host `fedora`
