### BUGS ‚Äî live demo QA (2026-07-03, Eagle/.13 on 12.0.0 Quazar)
- [>] **BUG-STORAGE-1: Storage surface has no local disk info on a Workstation.** **As** a workstation user, **I want** my own disks/partitions in the Storage surface, **so that** it's useful on a single node. **Root cause:** `crates/mesh/mackesd/src/bin/mackesd.rs:6539` gates the `StorageWorker` behind `worker_role::runs("storage", role_rank)`, which excludes the **workstation** rank ‚Äî so a workstation never publishes `state/storage/<node>`, and the surface shows "No peer has published a storage mirror yet." **Acceptance:** the storage worker runs on the workstation role too (a workstation publishes its own `state/storage/<node>` from UDisks2); the Storage surface on a solo workstation shows its local disks/partitions; unit test that `worker_role::runs("storage", workstation_rank)` is true; verified live on Eagle (Storage shows local disks). *(alt/also acceptable per ¬ß7: the surface reads local disks directly as a fallback ‚Äî but the worker-on-workstation fix is cleaner + matches the mesh-mirror architecture.)* *(code fix landed 5f2f3d2 ‚Äî the real defect was that `"storage"` was **missing from the `WORKER_TIERS` census**, so the `mackesd role-workers` diagnostic omitted it (read as "excluded from Workstation"); now an explicit `("storage", 0)` entry + tested 13/13. ‚öÝÔ∏è NOTE: runtime behavior was already correct (2-role model, rank is a floor ‚Üí the worker already spawned on Workstation), so this alone won't change the live `.13` symptom. Root cause of the demo symptom is almost certainly that **`.13`'s deployed mackesd predates the E12-20 storage worker** ‚Äî STAYS `[>]` pending a 12.x mackesd redeploy to `.13` + live-verify (`mackesd role-workers` lists `storage` AND `state/storage/<node>` present on the Bus).)* *(‚úÖ CONFIRMED via live-verify 2026-07-03: `.13` runs **11.4.5**; `strings $(command -v mackesd)` finds NO `state/storage`/`StorageWorker` ‚Äî the storage worker is absent from the deployed binary. `role-workers` on 11.4.5 lists 30 workstation workers, none `storage`. FIX = deploy a **12.x** mackesd/RPM to `.13` (also lands BUG-BRIGHTNESS-1 properly), then re-verify. Tracked as the `.13` 12.x redeploy follow-up.)*
- [‚úì] **BUG-BRIGHTNESS-1: backlight brightness fails for the non-root session shell (`Permission denied os error 13`).** **As** a user, **I want** the brightness slider to work, **so that** I can dim my panel. **Root cause:** `crates/desktop/mde-seat/src/backlight.rs:129` does a raw `std::fs::write` to `/sys/class/backlight/<name>/brightness` (root:root 0644); the DRM shell runs as the non-root session user ‚Üí EACCES. **Acceptance:** brightness set goes through **logind `org.freedesktop.login1.Session.SetBrightness(subsystem,name,value)`** (the privileged session API ‚Äî no root needed), with the direct sysfs write as a root fallback; PLUS the RPM ships a `video`-group udev rule (`ACTION=="add", SUBSYSTEM=="backlight", chgrp video + chmod g+w brightness`) as belt-and-suspenders; the shell user is in `video`. Verified: the brightness slider changes the panel on Eagle without a permission error. *(Eagle got an immediate udev+chmod workaround 2026-07-03.)* *(done: 1427cbd ‚Äî logind `SetBrightness` via the existing zbus SysBus seam + sysfs fallback + `packaging/udev/90-mde-backlight.rules` shipped in the RPM; farm gates green (mde-seat 76/76); operator confirmed the slider works live.)*
- [>] **BUG-VIDEO-1: Media/video player won't play a local video on Eagle.** **As** a user, **I want** to open a video file from my home dir and have it play, **so that** the Media surface is usable locally. **Root cause (live-verified 2026-07-03):** `.13` runs magic-mesh **11.4.5**, whose RPM ships **no `mde-media-egui` binary** (the MEDIA player epic is a 12.x feature; `command -v mde-media-egui` = absent). The local files are `~/Downloads/*.mkv` = **AV1 video (libdav1d) + Opus audio in Matroska**; `libmpv.so.2` + gstreamer + ffmpeg are all present on the box. **Acceptance:** deploy a **12.x** build to `.13` so the Media surface/player exists; the player opens a local `~/Downloads/*.mkv` and plays it (video + audio); confirm the player's decode path handles **AV1+Opus/Matroska** (libmpv-backed ‚Üí uses system dav1d) ‚Äî if the 12.x player can't decode AV1, that's a follow-on codec task. Verified live on Eagle: a local .mkv plays. *(Same old-build root cause as BUG-STORAGE-1 ‚Äî folded into the `.13` 12.x redeploy; also recon `crates/desktop/mde-media-egui` decode backend to confirm AV1 before deploying.)* *(‚öÝÔ∏è RECON VERDICT 2026-07-03 ‚Äî a straight 12.x deploy will NOT play it; the codec is a red herring (mpv+dav1d on `.13` decodes AV1+Opus/mkv fine). TWO build/wiring blockers: **(A) shipped player is `FakeMpv`** ‚Äî the `mpv` feature (`mde-media-core/Cargo.toml` `mpv=["dep:libmpv2"]`, default off) is never enabled in any build path (`xcp-build.sh:448` builds `--features drm`; `build-rpm-fedora43.sh:100` default features), so the embedded player simulates playback (flips to Playing, 0:00 frozen, no A/V). FIX: add `media-mpv=["mde-media-egui/mpv"]` to `mde-shell-egui/Cargo.toml`, build `--features drm,media-mpv`, and provision **`mpv-libs-devel`** on the farm build VMs (links system libmpv at build ‚Äî farm lacks it, honest-gated). **(B) video stage is a placeholder** ‚Äî `mde-media-egui/src/app.rs:1324` `player_stage` paints a dark rect; no mpv-render-API‚Üíegui-texture upload and no DRM overlay-plane scanout (MEDIA-2 shipped only as a seam). FIX: implement the frame‚Üídisplay path. ‚öÝÔ∏è **DESIGN FORK (operator): render via mpv render-API ‚Üí egui `TextureHandle` upload, vs a DRM overlay plane beneath the egui shell.** Local-file open + surface mount are FINE (MEDIA-18 done; Open-URL/Index-folder accept `~/Downloads/*.mkv`). Storage+brightness are unaffected by this ‚Äî the `.13` 12.x deploy still fixes those two.)*
- [‚úì] **BUG-BLUETOOTH-1: Bluetooth had no controls in the Workbench.** **As** a user, **I want** to scan/pair/connect/manage Bluetooth from the shell, **so that** the System surface is usable for BT. **Root cause:** the `mde-seat` BlueZ backend (`bluez.rs`) is complete, but the shell's `system.rs` BT section was **read-only** ‚Äî pair/connect/disconnect/trust/scan/forget were never wired to buttons. **Acceptance:** the BT panel drives the real backend verbs + a pairing dialog; no mockups. *(done: dd16142 (worker 461c23c) ‚Äî adapter Power/Discoverable/Pairable/Scan toggles + per-device Connect/Disconnect/Pair/Forget/Trust; a `PairingBridge`/`bt_pairing.rs` modal (PIN/passkey/confirm/authorize) blocking off the egui thread; errors‚ÜíBLUETOOTH toasts; + 3 backend gaps folded (BtDevice.address/rssi, BtAdapter.discoverable/pairable). Farm-gated: mde-seat 76/76, shell 330/330, clippy clean. Live pair/connect needs a real adapter (headless farm has none) ‚Äî D-Bus round-trips tested as typed-error paths.)*
- [‚úì] **BUG-CHAT-1: Chat surface looked incomplete.** **As** a user, **I want** a finished chat, **so that** it feels complete. **Root cause:** the panel was real + live-wired but had four visible edge holes (no message timestamps, no self presence-picker, no status editor, no mute). **Acceptance:** the four holes closed with real worker round-trips (not local-only UI). *(done: f297611 (worker 66656bc) ‚Äî `HH:MM`+hover timestamps with day separators; ICQ presence ComboBox (Free-for-Chat/Available/Away/DND/Invisible) + inline status editor via new `ACTION_CHAT_PRESENCE`; per-contact/room Mute via new `ACTION_CHAT_MUTE` + `STATE_CHAT_NOTIFY` mirror. Round-trips proven: presence/status republish `state/chat/roster` + reload from `presence.json`; mute mutates `NotifyPrefs`, persists `notify.json`, silences a muted Critical alert. Combined chat+BT+nav shell re-gated green (336 tests). Dead Clipboard/File/Call/Remote message-cards left as a follow-on.)*

## POWER ‚Äî battery indicator + full power settings (operator 2026-07-03; recon+3-fork survey; design: docs/design/battery-power.md)

Live "battery does not show" + "include power settings". Backend (UPower/logind) is real; gaps = no chrome battery slot + missing settings. Operator locked FULL scope: native mde-seat power-profiles client, DRM-native idle+lid honorer, charge thresholds + rich telemetry. mde-seat backend adds serialize on snapshot.rs/upower.rs; push backend before the panel.

- [‚úì] **POWER-1: battery indicator in the chrome status bar.** **As** a laptop/Surface user, **I want** battery % at a glance, **so that** I don't open System to check charge. **Acceptance:** a `battery_view` `SlotView` in `chrome.rs` over the polled `SeatSnapshot.batteries` ‚Äî system-pack %, charging bolt, severity dot (OK/WARN under ~20% / DANGER critical), honest "No battery"/"unavailable"; tooltip = kind+state; token-styled; unit-tested. *(done: fc6cfc5 ‚Äî `battery_view` slot (Signal¬∑BT¬∑Vol¬∑Batt), system-pack %, ‚ö° bolt, OK/WARN(<20%)/DANGER(‚â§5%/Empty) dots, "No battery"/"unavailable"/pre-poll dash, tooltip=kind¬∑state¬∑%; token consts BATTERY_LOW/CRITICAL; standalone SlotView (folds cleanly into NAVBAR-4 tray). Farm-gated; combined shell re-gated green 339 tests.)*
- [‚úì] **POWER-2: mde-seat Hibernate verb + on-AC source.** **As** a user, **I want** Hibernate + to know if I'm on AC, **so that** power management is complete. **Acceptance:** `PowerVerb::Hibernate` + `PowerCaps.hibernate` (CanHibernate probe); `SeatSnapshot` carries on-AC/on-battery folded from the UPower LinePower `Online` prop (currently dropped); real D-Bus, honest None, unit-tested. *(done: 45b4412 ‚Äî `PowerVerb::Hibernate` (Manager.Hibernate, CanHibernate) + `PowerCaps.hibernate`; `SeatSnapshot.on_ac: Probe<Option<bool>>` folded from LinePower `Online` (honest None when absent). mde-seat 79 tests. Integration: shell SeatSnapshot literals got `on_ac: absent()` ‚Äî combined shell re-gated green.)*
- [‚úì] **POWER-3: mde-seat power backend v2 (profiles + thresholds + telemetry + lid).** **As** the shell, **I want** local power hardware access, **so that** the settings panel drives real hardware. **Acceptance:** a native `net.hadess.PowerProfiles` zbus client (get active + list available + set), folded to `SeatSnapshot.power_profile: Probe<..>` (honest "unavailable" when the daemon is absent); charge thresholds via sysfs `charge_control_end_threshold` (read+write); rich `Battery` telemetry (time-to-empty/full, energy-rate draw W) folded from UPower; an evdev **`SW_LID`** lid-switch watch ‚Üí `SeatSnapshot` lid state. All real, honest None, unit-tested. *(done: 6d05ec3 ‚Äî `powerprofiles.rs` (net.hadess.PowerProfiles get/list/set ‚Üí `SeatSnapshot.power_profile: Probe<ProfileState>`), `charge_threshold.rs` (sysfs read/write ‚Üí `charge_limit: Probe<Option<u8>>` + `set_charge_threshold`, EACCES surfaced honestly), `Battery` telemetry (time_to_empty/full + energy_rate W), `lid.rs` ‚Üí `lid: Probe<LidState{Open/Closed/Unknown}>`. Drive: `set_power_profile`/`set_charge_threshold`. ‚öÝÔ∏è lid uses the `/proc/acpi/button/lid` read (evdev not farm-vendored + crate forbids unsafe ‚Üí no raw SW_LID ioctl); revisit if a richer lid signal is needed. mde-seat 100 tests, shell 339; combined re-gated green. Charge-write + lid Open/Closed are HW-gated (need a real laptop).)*
- [‚úì] **POWER-4: Power Settings panel (System surface).** **As** a user, **I want** power settings in one place, **so that** I can tune power. **Acceptance:** extend `system.rs` "Power & Battery" + a new `power_settings.rs`: a profile segmented control (Performance/Balanced/Power-saver, honest "unavailable" when absent), a caps-gated Hibernate row, an on-AC/on-battery line, a charge-threshold slider (writes sysfs), the time-to-empty/draw telemetry, and idle-timeout + lid-action settings (persisted); each drives the real backend/honorer ‚Äî no inert controls (¬ß7); ¬ß4 tokens. *(done: 69b4f53 ‚Äî `power_settings.rs` + extended `power_section`: profile segmented control (SetPowerProfile‚ÜíSeat), caps-gated Hibernate, on-AC line, 50‚Äì100% charge-threshold slider (SetChargeThreshold‚Üísysfs), time-to-empty/full + draw-W telemetry. Honest Absent/unsupported/EACCES states, no inert controls. shell 351 tests; combined re-gated green. Idle-timeout + lid-action UI moved to POWER-5 with the honorer, so they're not inert.)*
- [‚úì] **POWER-5: DRM-native idle + lid honorer (shell).** **As** a user, **I want** idle-suspend + lid-close to actually work, **so that** the settings aren't inert. **Acceptance:** a shell-owned idle timer (last-input ‚Üí configured timeout ‚Üí `seat.power(Suspend)`) + a lid-close handler reading POWER-3's `SW_LID` watch ‚Üí the configured action, both driven by POWER-4's persisted settings; works on the DRM shell (no Wayland/swayidle); live-verify suspend-on-idle + lid-close on real hardware. *(done: 18a7b32 ‚Äî `power_honor.rs`: idle timer (last-input reset from egui events ‚Üí Suspend once, no re-fire w/o activity, default Never) + lid Open‚ÜíClosed edge handler (default Suspend, debounced, unarmed-if-closed-at-start, desktop-no-lid=no-op); config `power-honor.json` via `client_data_dir` (atomic write), edited by the POWER-4 panel's new idle-timeout + lid-action pickers; tiny 2-line main.rs tick hook (auto-merged clean with EDITOR-9). shell 364 tests; live suspend/lid HW-gated. **POWER epic COMPLETE (1..5).**)*

## NAVBAR ‚Äî bottom nav taskbar (relocate the shell dock, Carbon icon-first) (operator 2026-07-03; 15-Q `/plan`; design: docs/design/workbench-navbar.md)

Moves the surface launcher from the left vertical rail to a **full-width bottom taskbar**, redrawn Carbon icon-first, folding the separate status chrome into the same bar. Tasks NAVBAR-1..3 are the visible relocation + look (dispatch first); NAVBAR-4..8 largely **serialise on `dock.rs`/`chrome.rs`/`main.rs`** (same-file ‚Äî follow the core in sequence, don't parallel-edit).

- [‚úì] **NAVBAR-1: relocate the rail to a full-width bottom taskbar.** **As** a user, **I want** the nav along the bottom, **so that** it reads like a desktop taskbar. **Acceptance:** `dock.rs` renders via `TopBottomPanel::bottom("shell-taskbar")` (48px) with a **horizontal** entry layout; the left `SidePanel` rail is removed; the surface body fills the `CentralPanel` above it; flat Carbon `layer` fill + hairline top divider (¬ß4); shell tests green + renders.
- [‚úì] **NAVBAR-2: grouping, dividers + tray-style order.** **As** a user, **I want** the surfaces sectioned, **so that** the bar is scannable. **Acceptance:** entries partition into **mesh-control ‚à£ apps ‚à£ system** with thin Carbon dividers; apps pack left, the **system** group (System/Storage/About) is pushed hard-right beside the tray; a declarative `group_of(Surface)` classifier drives it; `Surface::Editor` is in the apps group.
- [‚úì] **NAVBAR-3: icon-first glyph cell (label, two-tone tint, active mark, hover).** **As** a user, **I want** clear per-surface glyphs, **so that** I can tell them apart at a glance. **Acceptance:** each cell = `brand::icons` Carbon glyph + a tiny always-on label; **active glyph filled / idle outline** (two-tone, tokens); **accent top-border + brighter tint** on the active cell; hover shows the `hint` tooltip + a cell highlight; all via `mde-egui::Style` (no raw hex). *(done: NAVBAR-1/2/3 in 303cc78 (worker f43d4a5) ‚Äî 48px `TopBottomPanel::bottom`, grouped mesh‚à£apps‚à£system w/ system tray-ordered hard-right, icon-first cells, accent top-border active mark, left rail deleted, body fills above. Farm-gated build+test (merged BT+nav tree re-gated on .130: 332 tests pass). NOTE lock #9 approximated: the `brand::icons` set has no separate outline artwork, so "filled vs outline" is done via tint intensity (active=solid ACCENT / idle=dim) ‚Äî a true outline variant is a follow-on if wanted.)*
- [ ] **NAVBAR-4: unified status tray (fold `chrome.rs` in).** **As** a user, **I want** one bottom bar, **so that** status + nav aren't split. **Acceptance:** the status widgets (clock, peer count, health, quick-toggles, role badge, version tag) render in a right-aligned tray segment of the taskbar; the separate status strip is retired; no regression in what `chrome.rs` showed. *(serialises after NAVBAR-1)*
- [ ] **NAVBAR-5: live badges (unread / peers / health).** **As** a user, **I want** at-a-glance status on glyphs, **so that** I see activity without opening a surface. **Acceptance:** `badge_for(Surface,&ShellState)` paints a Chat unread badge (from `chat::total_unread`), a Mesh Map peer count, and a health-tinted node/System dot; badges are token-styled + only shown when meaningful. *(serialises after NAVBAR-3)*
- [ ] **NAVBAR-6: keyboard + right-click context menu.** **As** a keyboard user, **I want** to drive the bar without the mouse, **so that** nav is fast. **Acceptance:** `Super`+1‚Ä¶9/0 jump to the Nth visible surface (reuse `hotkeys.rs`); arrow keys traverse focus; right-click a glyph opens a context menu (pin, info, close-if-closable). *(serialises after NAVBAR-3)*
- [ ] **NAVBAR-7: overflow 'More' (‚ãØ) tray.** **As** a user on a narrow panel, **I want** every surface reachable, **so that** none is lost. **Acceptance:** when grouped glyphs + tray overflow the width, trailing/low-priority surfaces collapse into a `‚ãØ` popup (`egui::menu`); nothing is silently dropped; measured before painting. *(serialises after NAVBAR-2)*
- [ ] **NAVBAR-8: tie the bar to the compact‚Üîexpand mode.** **As** a user, **I want** the bar to match the shell density, **so that** compact mode reclaims space. **Acceptance:** the locked compact/expand mode selects the bar variant ‚Äî expand = 48px + labels; compact = a shorter icon-only bar; one mode drives the whole shell (reuse the control-surface enum). *(serialises after NAVBAR-1/3)*

### NAVBAR-UNION ‚Äî merge the Nav Bar + Desktop Chooser into one picker (operator 2026-07-03 follow-up survey; design: docs/design/workbench-navbar.md "one picker")

The bar and `chooser.rs` (the Picker) become one picker system sharing one `ChooserState`. Rides **after NAVBAR-1..3**; touches `dock.rs`/`chooser.rs`/`main.rs` ‚Äî serialise on those files.

- [ ] **NAVBAR-U1: Desktop entry as a split button.** **As** a user, **I want** one click to return to my desktop, **so that** reconnecting is instant. **Acceptance:** the Desktop cell renders as a split button ‚Äî main click reconnects the last/active remote desktop (from `ChooserState`), or opens the picker if none; a caret opens the source flyout (U2). Token-styled; keyboard-reachable.
- [ ] **NAVBAR-U2: source flyout in the bar.** **As** a user, **I want** to pick a desktop source from the bar, **so that** I don't have to enter the full grid first. **Acceptance:** the caret opens a bar popup listing discovered + pinned sources (reuse `connect_picker`/a slim `chooser_grid` reading the shared `ChooserState`); selecting one connects; reuses the NAVBAR-7 flyout/overflow machinery.
- [ ] **NAVBAR-U3: active sessions as temporary bar entries.** **As** a user, **I want** my open desktops in the bar, **so that** I can switch like a taskbar. **Acceptance:** each connected remote desktop shows a live glyph in the bar (a 'desktops' run), appearing on connect + removed on disconnect; click focuses that session; a session/count badge (reuse NAVBAR-5).
- [ ] **NAVBAR-U4: one state, two faces.** **As** a user, **I want** the bar picker + the chooser surface to agree, **so that** there's no split brain. **Acceptance:** the bar flyout (compact) and `chooser_panel` (expanded) read/mutate the SAME `ChooserState` (single source of truth for sources/pins/sessions); the compact‚Üîexpand mode (NAVBAR-8) selects which face shows; no second store.

## CURTAIN ‚Äî the secure login/lock curtain (operator 2026-07-04; 10-Q `/plan`; design: docs/design/lock-curtain.md)

The missing login gate for the DM-less DRM shell: a full-screen Carbon lock/login curtain (slide+settle-bounce), giant clock, PAM auth, lock-screen media transport. All in `mde-shell-egui` ‚Äî CURTAIN-1 establishes `curtain.rs`; 2/3/4 serialize behind it (and behind the in-flight W10-2 on main.rs/hotkeys).

- [‚úì] **CURTAIN-1: the curtain surface + motion + clock.** **As** a user, **I want** a lock screen, **so that** the seat is coverable. **Acceptance:** `curtain.rs` full-screen top layer with the state machine (Unlocked/Dropping/Locked/Revealing/Verifying/Lifting/Backoff); slide-down + settle-bounce drop, lift-up unlock (Motion tokens); giant digital HH:MM + date face; idle-dim to faint; while not Unlocked ALL input routes to the curtain only; Super+L drops it; tested state transitions + input-exclusivity. *(done: e88f31a ‚Äî curtain.rs (1310) + main.rs; state machine + settle-bounce motion + giant clock + idle-dim; 4-layer input exclusivity (pointer whole-screen Foreground area, per-frame focus-steal, hotkey/edge/chyron gates, and closed the vdi::forward_input raw-drain leak that would reach a live guest under lock); injectable Verifier seam (default NotWired CANNOT grant ‚Äî CURTAIN-2 fills PAM) + face_extras seam for CURTAIN-4; 388 combined shell tests, 0 new warnings.)*
- [‚úì] **CURTAIN-2: PAM auth + two-stage reveal + backoff.** **As** the operator, **I want** real auth, **so that** the lock is secure. **Acceptance:** `pam_auth.rs` runs a real PAM conversation for the seat user OFF the render thread (channel bridge); any key reveals the password field (Esc returns to the face); wrong password ‚Üí honest error; 5 fails ‚Üí 30s cooldown with countdown (field disabled); farm-probe libpam bindings EARLY; unit-test the state/backoff logic via an injectable auth seam (the live PAM leg verified on real hardware).
- [‚úì] **CURTAIN-3: triggers ‚Äî boot-gate, idle/lid Lock, logind signal.** **As** a user, **I want** locking everywhere it should happen, **so that** coverage is complete. **Acceptance:** persisted `require_login_at_boot` (default ON once shipped) starts the shell Locked before any surface; POWER-5's honorer gains a **Lock** idle action + lid-Lock routes to the curtain in-process; a logind Lock/Unlock listener drops/lifts it; `loginctl lock-session` works live; tested trigger routing. *(touches power_honor.rs/main.rs/hotkeys.rs ‚Äî serialize)*
- [‚úì] **CURTAIN-4: lock-screen media transport + status row.** **As** a listener, **I want** playback on the curtain, **so that** music doesn't need an unlock. **Acceptance:** the unified now-playing strip (active player's title/artist, play/pause/next/prev, volume) drives the REAL music/media transport seams while locked ‚Äî the ONLY interactive elements besides unlock; a status glanceables row (battery/mesh/date) reuses the tray folds; no message content anywhere; tested transport-while-locked + content-privacy.

## VDOCK ‚Äî the left vertical auto-hide dock (operator 2026-07-04; 25-Q `/plan`; design: docs/design/vertical-dock.md)

REPLACE the horizontal Win10 bottom bar with a left-edge, full-height, auto-hide vertical dock. Clock removed ‚Üí Timers&Alarms; status icons ‚Üí stacked 2√ó2 quads; Settings/Show-Desktop ‚Üí a 2√ó2 system quad. Super toggles + pin, slide-from-left, ~48px solid dark panel. A re-layout of the grouped-picker/tray work, not a rebuild. Serialize the dock.rs units.

- [ ] **VDOCK-1: the vertical dock frame + auto-hide.** **As** a user, **I want** a left dock I summon, **so that** the screen is uncluttered. **Acceptance:** a left `SidePanel`/`Area` ~48px, full-height, solid Carbon-dark + hairline right divider; hidden by default, **Super toggles** it (hotkeys path) with a **pin** to hold open (#9/#13), **slide-in-from-left** motion (#14); central content fills the freed width when hidden; no focus/input steal while hidden (DRM-seat safe); tested toggle/pin/slide + hidden-passthrough. *(reworks main.rs + dock.rs frame ‚Äî serialize all VDOCK)*
- [‚úì] **VDOCK-2: the vertical app picker.** **As** a user, **I want** my apps grouped vertically, **so that** I launch by section. **Acceptance:** Workbench lead pinned top; the 6 groups stacked top‚Üíbottom, **single-column** icon-only cells (#2/#11), each group with a **horizontal accent label** above + a **left-rail accent stripe** + divider (#4/#21, PICKER-2 tokens); **left-edge accent bar** on the active surface (#10); ~24px icons (#12/#23); **'‚Ä¶' overflow** popup when groups exceed height (#22); all 13 app surfaces present once (Settings/Desktop moved to the system quad); routing unchanged; tested membership + active-mark + overflow. *(after VDOCK-1)*
- [‚úì] **VDOCK-3: the status 2√ó2 quads.** **As** a user, **I want** compact status, **so that** glances are quick. **Acceptance:** the tray reworks into **stacked 2√ó2 quads** anchored bottom (#6/#8): Chat[badge]/BT/Vol/Batt, then Status/Signal/Peers/Sessions; ~18px icons; each cell **routes to its owning surface** (#15, no flyouts); Chat's badge counts CHAT-FIX-2 unread + peer messages (#19); battery-fill/dot logic carried over; tested quad layout + route + badge. *(after VDOCK-1; reworks tray.rs)*
- [‚úì] **VDOCK-4: the system 2√ó2 quad + Power menu.** **As** a user, **I want** system actions gridded, **so that** they match the status size. **Acceptance:** a 2√ó2 quad (#7/#17): Settings‚ÜíSystem, Show-Desktop‚Üíexisting route, Lock‚Üícurtain, Power‚Üía **Lock/Suspend/Reboot/Shutdown menu** (#18, reboot/shutdown typed-armed); sized to the status icons; tested each cell dispatches + the armed power menu. *(after VDOCK-1)*
- [ ] **VDOCK-5: Timers & Alarms surface (clock replacement).** **As** a user, **I want** timers/alarms, **so that** the removed clock earns its place. **Acceptance:** a clock-glyph status cell showing the time as its glyph (#20) opens a new `Surface::Timers` ‚Äî create/run countdown **timers** + set **alarms** that fire notifications via the CHAT-FIX-2 producer even when the surface is closed (a shell-side or daemon timer that survives surface switches, risk); Carbon tokens; tested a timer fires an alarm/notification. *(after VDOCK-1; new surface)*
- [‚úì] **VDOCK-6: rip out the horizontal bottom bar.** **As** the shell, **I want** one dock, **so that** the layout is coherent. **Acceptance:** the bottom `TopBottomPanel` taskbar is removed (#25); the shell body fills top-to-bottom with the vertical dock on the left; the old horizontal taskbar()/tray-flyout code retired or dormant; every surface still reachable exactly once; shell layout tests updated + green; the PICKER-3 layout harness extended to pin the vertical geometry. *(the final cutover ‚Äî after VDOCK-1..5 land)*

## KDC-MESH ‚Äî KDE Connect over the Nebula mesh (operator 2026-07-04; 16-Q `/plan`; design: docs/design/kdc-mesh.md)

Move the existing KDE Connect subsystem (`crates/kdc/` + `kdc_host` worker + the SEC-5 mesh-shunt) onto the Nebula overlay so a phone (Android Nebula client + KDE Connect app) is a full mesh member with all features across all nodes. Overlay-only transport, one mesh-wide pairing, kdc_host on every node. Android apps are STOCK ‚Äî "one Mesh device" is a host-side fanout (design note).

- [‚úì] **KDC-MESH-1: overlay transport (Nebula-only).** **As** a phone, **I want** KDC over the overlay, **so that** it works anywhere I have mesh. **Acceptance:** an `OverlayTransport` in `crates/kdc/mde-kdc-host` binds 1716 on the node's Nebula overlay IP + dials peers/phones by overlay IP; overlay-only (no LAN direct, #3); `kdc_outbound` sends over it; nothing binds the public NIC (tested ‚Äî bind addr = overlay); LAN transport retired/gated off. ¬ß7 + proto tests green.
- [‚úì] **KDC-MESH-2: directed discovery over the mesh roster.** **As** a host, **I want** to find the phone without broadcast, **so that** discovery crosses Nebula. **Acceptance:** the `kdc_host` worker consumes the mesh-shunt roster + peer directory to learn the phone's overlay IP + every host's; hosts directed-announce to the phone (no UDP broadcast, #2); the phone's overlay IP flows from the enroll/roster; tested roster‚Üíannounce.
- [‚úì] **KDC-MESH-3: mesh-wide pairing + universal role.** **As** the mesh, **I want** one pairing recognized everywhere, **so that** the phone isn't tied to a node. **Acceptance:** the `PairingStore` record replicates on the substrate so every node's `kdc_host` recognizes the phone (#5); `kdc_host` ‚Üí **rank-0** in `WORKER_TIERS` (every node incl. lighthouses/headless, #15) with the census count-tests updated; the firewall preset opens 1716 on the **overlay iface only**, never public (tested default-deny public); a node that hasn't synced the pairing honest-gates.
- [ ] **KDC-MESH-4: QR pair-to-mesh onboarding.** **As** an operator, **I want** one scan to enroll+pair, **so that** onboarding is trivial. **Acceptance:** the Phones hub renders a QR encoding the mesh enroll token + a KDC pairing token; scanning it (Android Nebula client + KDE Connect) enrolls the phone onto Nebula AND pairs it mesh-wide (#14); the RSA-4096 TOFU + fingerprint-pin completes over the overlay (#4); tested token gen + the pairing-record write.
- [‚úì] **KDC-MESH-5: bidirectional mesh notifications.** **As** a user, **I want** notifications both ways, **so that** phone + mesh talk. **Acceptance:** phone notifications appear on every desktop (all-nodes, #6) AND the CHAT-FIX-2 local-event feed pushes to the phone (#9); reply-from-desktop where supported; a de-dup/coalesce so one phone notification isn't N unpleasant desktop toasts (risk); over the overlay transport; tested both directions + de-dup. *(composes with CHAT-FIX-2)*
- [ ] **KDC-MESH-6: remote input + media control.** **As** a user, **I want** phone-as-touchpad + media keys, **so that** I control the desktop. **Acceptance:** the phone drives touchpad + keyboard input on the active desktop via the shell's evdev/input-injection seam (#10) + media play/pause/next/vol + presenter on the playing node (media surface transport seam); real events (¬ß7); tested input inject + media dispatch. *(touches mde-shell-egui input + media seams ‚Äî coordinate)*
- [ ] **KDC-MESH-7: two-way any-node files + mesh service directory.** **As** a user, **I want** files across the mesh, **so that** I reach any node. **Acceptance:** send/receive (done) + browse the phone's FS from a desktop (SFTP mount) + browse ANY node's shared files from the phone (#11); a mesh-wide **service directory** (each node publishes its KDC services to the substrate) the phone/hub browse to target any node over the overlay (#7); tested the directory + a node-targeted file browse.
- [ ] **KDC-MESH-8: run-commands incl. OpenStack lifecycle (all nodes) + battery/telephony/find.** **As** an operator, **I want** to drive the fleet from my phone, **so that** ops are pocket-sized. **Acceptance:** run-commands targetable per-node via the directory, INCLUDING a series of **OpenStack lifecycle commands** (instance start/stop/reboot/etc.) driving the QC `state/openstack` verbs across all nodes (#12); battery + connectivity report on desktops; telephony (call/SMS alerts, SMS reply done); find-my-devices both ways; **pairing is the auth** (#16, no per-command confirm) but every action appends to the KDC hash-chained audit log (`events::append_event`); tested each command ‚Üí its real seam + the audit append.
- [ ] **KDC-MESH-9: the Phones hub surface + mesh-fanout endpoint.** **As** a user, **I want** to manage my phone, **so that** the relationship is visible. **Acceptance:** a `mde-shell-egui` Phones hub: paired phone(s) with mesh identity + battery/signal, per-feature toggles, the file browser, the run-command editor (incl. the OpenStack set), unpair (fast + mesh-wide), pairing QR; a mackesd **mesh-fanout** so a designated endpoint advertises as "Quasar Mesh" (one device to stock KDE Connect, #8) relaying follow-everywhere actions + aggregating responses; Carbon tokens (¬ß4); folds in the existing phone-hub/kdc pieces (¬ß6); tested hub render + fanout.

## CONSOLE ‚Äî the Terminal's Start-Menu front door (operator 2026-07-04; 50-Q `/plan`; design: docs/design/console-frontdoor.md)

A Carbon Win10-style Start Menu that IS the Terminal's front door: a far-left terminal-glyph button opens a panel of operational entries, each launching a real TUI/CLI op as a named tab in `mde-term-egui`. Grounded in Eagle's real toolset (btop/systemctl/journalctl, nmcli/ss/mtr, dnf/rpm/flatpak, lsblk/df/smartctl, podman/virsh, mesh stack). MVP = everything at once.

- [ ] **CONSOLE-1: the Start button + panel shell + nav.** **As** a user, **I want** a terminal front door, **so that** ops are one click. **Acceptance:** a far-left Start button in `dock.rs` using the Terminal glyph toggles a new `console.rs` panel; Win10 two-pane (left rail = category jump-index + power/session + footer user@host¬∑version; right = pinned Terminal+Monitor + grouped list); slide-up Motion from the button; Esc/click-away/re-click close; full arrow-key nav + focus ring (EXPLORER-18 posture); Carbon tokens (¬ß4); tested open/close + nav + jump-scroll. *(serialise after PICKER-2 ‚Äî dock.rs)*
- [ ] **CONSOLE-2: the terminal spawn-tab seam + entry launch.** **As** a user, **I want** entries to open in terminal tabs, **so that** ops run where I can see them. **Acceptance:** a `spawn_tab(name, argv)` seam on `mde-term-egui` (reuse `TabbedTerminal`/`new_tab`, add the thin entrypoint if absent ‚Äî glue ¬ß6); selecting a Console entry closes the menu, switches to `Surface::Terminal`, opens a NAMED tab running the real command (stays-open-on-exit with a prompt); root-needing ops run under `sudo` in the tab (interactive password); tested a real command opens a named tab + sudo path. *(after CONSOLE-1)*
- [ ] **CONSOLE-3: the entry table + all groups.** **As** an operator, **I want** the real ops, **so that** the front door is useful. **Acceptance:** a const `ConsoleEntry` table for System (btop/systemctl/journalctl-f/live-dashboard), Network (mesh-status/ss/mtr/nmcli/firewall-cmd), Packages (check+apply dnf/list-installed/platform-update/flatpak), Storage (df+lsblk+ncdu/smartctl/mesh-share), Mesh (meshctl-status/peers/openstack-mirror/etcdctl), Containers&VMs (podman ps/virsh list/openstack ‚Äî **combined, with a surface link to the Cloud/Instances plane**, Q41/Q50), Shells (user/root/tmux); each row = icon + label + one-line desc + Fedora/Quasar provenance tag; a missing tool ‚Üí entry honestly hidden/greyed (¬ß7, no dead entries); tested every entry maps to a present command + the surface link routes. *(after CONSOLE-2)*
- [ ] **CONSOLE-4: Power group (armed) + custom entries.** **As** an operator, **I want** power + my own ops, **so that** the front door is complete. **Acceptance:** a Power section (Lock‚Üícurtain, Suspend, Reboot, Shut Down) via real loginctl/systemctl, destructive ones behind the platform **typed-arming** confirm; a Custom group where the operator registers their own named command entries (in-UI add + config file); tested power actions dispatch (armed) + a custom entry opens its tab. *(after CONSOLE-1)*

## CHAT-FIX ‚Äî the empty-Chat bug + local notifications (operator 2026-07-04, found live on Eagle; design: docs/design/console-frontdoor.md)

Eagle's Chat is empty. Two real defects: the chat worker never runs (census gap), and nothing produces local system notifications.

- [‚úì] **CHAT-FIX-1: register the chat worker in the census (reporting hygiene).** **As** an operator, **I want** `role-workers` to list chat, **so that** the census is honest. *(CORRECTED: live-verified on Eagle the chat worker ALREADY runs ‚Äî boot log `starting worker: chat` (rank-0 unknown-worker default). This is a REPORTING gap (`role-workers`/census omits it), NOT the empty-Chat cause ‚Äî the BUG-STORAGE-1 REPORTING half. The empty Chat is CHAT-FIX-2.)* **Acceptance:** `bin/mackesd.rs` spawns ChatWorker only `if runs("chat", role_rank)`, but "chat" is absent from `WORKER_TIERS` ‚Üí the unknown-worker default keeps it off (the BUG-STORAGE-1 class); add `("chat", 0)` (universal/rank-0) to `WORKER_TIERS` so chat runs on every node incl. Eagle; census count tests updated; live-verify the chat worker appears in Eagle's roster after deploy.
- [‚úì] **CHAT-FIX-2: the local-notification producer worker.** **As** a user, **I want** the node to tell me what's happening, **so that** Chat isn't empty absent peer messages. *(THE real empty-Chat fix ‚Äî operator reported it live on Eagle: chat worker runs but there are no peer messages + nothing produces local system notifications. Note: an ntfy broker already runs (overlay :8443) ‚Äî the producer can ride it.)* **Acceptance:** a new mackesd `notify` worker watches: mesh peer join/leave (directory), dnf/platform update availability, `systemctl --failed` + mesh/cloud health, disk-usage/SMART thresholds, and **journal WARN-or-above**; emits typed notifications on the bus (bounded/rate-limited polls); the Chat surface renders them as a scrollable timestamped feed (newest first) + the tray badge counts unread (Q46/47); census entry (rank-0); tested each event source ‚Üí a notification (fixture-driven) + the Chat feed render. *(the notify producer half of Q34; composes with CONSOLE)*
