## EXPLORER ‚Äî the Hero unit explorer (operator 2026-07-04; 25-Q `/plan`; design: docs/design/unit-explorer.md)

A cinematic full-bleed "Hero" view of every discovered unit ‚Äî mesh peers, off-mesh LAN hosts, AND every OpenStack object on any node ‚Äî folded into the Discovery surface. Daemon aggregator (¬ß6) does the scanning; shell renders. MVP = all three sources at once (lock #25). EXPLORER-1 (aggregator worker) is the spine; the shell hero fold + scan submodule serialize behind it.

- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-1: the `unit_aggregator` mackesd worker + `Unit` model.** **As** the mesh, **I want** one unit stream, **so that** the shell renders without scanning. **Acceptance:** new `workers/unit_aggregator/` publishing `state/units*` on the bus; typed `Unit { id, kind(Peer/LanHost/Instance/Volume/Image/Network), name, reachability(InMesh/OnLan/CloudObject{node}), address?, health?, telemetry?, actions[] }`; folds the mesh mirror (peers/health) + unions every `state/openstack/<node>` (QC-2) dedup-by-id host-tagged (#20); unprobed fields explicit `unknown` (#12/¬ß7); publish-on-change + rescan tick (#19); census entry (rank per the BUG-STORAGE-1 lesson); tested folds + union dedup. *(scan submodule = EXPLORER-2)*
- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-2: the active LAN scan submodule.** **As** the aggregator, **I want** off-mesh discovery, **so that** LAN units appear. **Acceptance:** mDNS/DNS-SD listen + ARP/neighbor read + a bounded ping-sweep & light port fingerprint over the local subnet (nmap-style, #3) via the bounded-proc path; runs ONLY while the scan-active flag is set (#24) with a warm cache of the last result; emits `LanHost` units with type guesses + explicit unknowns; tested against a controlled fixture (no live-net assertion in unit tests; a live smoke on the farm subnet documented). *(serialise after EXPLORER-1)*
- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-3: the Discovery-surface hero fold + navigation.** **As** a user, **I want** the hero view, **so that** each unit gets a focused presentation. **Acceptance:** the existing Discovery surface grows the full-bleed hero card + bottom filmstrip + top category chips + `/` search (#5‚Äì8); Carbon slide+fade paging (#21); adaptive cinematic‚Üîlist-detail by shell size (#22); subscribes to `state/units*`; renders self as the first unit at empty then streams (#23); sets the aggregator scan-active flag only while visible (#24); enrollment/pair purpose preserved (folds into the #16 invite action); shell tests green. *(serialise after EXPLORER-1; touches the shell ‚Äî coordinate with W10/CURTAIN)*
- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-4: the hero card content + live telemetry.** **As** a user, **I want** a rich card, **so that** I know each unit at a glance. **Acceptance:** large type glyph + live status ring (#9), name/type/reachability headline (#10), rich telemetry sparklines (load/mem/net/uptime) when reachable else dimmed-minimal card with explicit unknowns (#11/12); all Carbon tokens (¬ß4); tested reachable-vs-dimmed rendering. *(after EXPLORER-3)* *(done: `explorer.rs` ‚Äî a rolling per-unit `UnitHistory` (60-pt ring ‚âà 5 min at the 5 s poll) sampled each `refresh` from the REAL polled load/mem scalars (¬ß7 ‚Äî every point observed, never synthesised; departed units pruned); the rich card now paints a load¬∑mem¬∑net¬∑uptime metric grid where load/mem draw a live sparkline (axis expands to a real peak), net stays honestly dimmed "no source" (no wire seam yet), uptime shows its value on a neutral baseline (a scalar counter, no fake trend), and a still-filling series reads "collecting‚Ä¶"; dimmed-minimal path unchanged; all Carbon `Style` tokens; +4 tests: bounded-real-sample accrual, prune-on-depart, no-series-no-history, reachable-sparkline-vs-dimmed render.)*
- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-5: per-type action bars (armed destructive).** **As** an operator, **I want** real verbs on the hero, **so that** it's a launchpad. **Acceptance:** peer ‚Üí open-in-Fleet + live health-check + evict(typed-armed) (#14); cloud instance ‚Üí console(SPICE/VNC) + start/stop/reboot/delete (every mutating verb typed-armed) + volume/image/network inspect+delete(armed) (#15); LAN host ‚Üí invite-to-mesh(armed) kicking the existing pairing flow (#16); each drives the REAL seam (no dead buttons, ¬ß7); arming reuses the platform typed-confirm; tested each verb dispatches + arming gates the destructive ones. *(after EXPLORER-3/4)*
- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-7: edge derivation in the aggregator + bus edge stream.** **As** the mesh, **I want** relationships as data, **so that** any client can render connectivity. **Acceptance:** the `unit_aggregator` derives a typed `Edge { kind, from, to, detail }` set covering all five kinds (E2: mesh tunnels incl. via-lighthouse, cloud attachments instance‚Üínetwork/volume/image + network‚Üísubnet‚Üírouter, L2/L3 adjacency same-subnet/one-ARP-hop/same-gateway, host placement object‚Üínode, storage volume‚Üíinstance + pool/share consumption); published alongside units on `state/units*`; a typed bus read API exposes the unit+edge stream (E9); edges derived from the SAME unioned sources (no new probes); tested per edge kind + dedup. *(after EXPLORER-1)*
- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-8: hero-card edge chips (grouped by kind) + jump.** **As** a user, **I want** to see how a unit connects, **so that** I can traverse the topology. **Acceptance:** the hero card renders a grouped edge-chip region (E1/E6: Tunnels / Networks / Volumes / Same subnet / Runs on \<node\> / Storage sections) from the edge stream; each chip is a clickable related-unit that jumps the hero to that neighbor; Carbon tokens; absent-edge sections omitted (no empty headers); tested chip render + jump. *(after EXPLORER-3 + EXPLORER-7)*
- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-9: full object detail + enrichment sources.** **As** a user, **I want** deep, named facts, **so that** each unit is fully legible. **Acceptance:** instances carry full Nova/Neutron/Cinder detail (E4: flavor/state/all IPs+ports+nets/volumes+sizes/image/host/keypair/created/secgroups); enrichment folds into every unit (E5: reverse-DNS+mDNS names, offline MAC-OUI vendor, service/port fingerprint‚Üítype guess+openable actions, mesh cert/role/groups/uptime); first-seen/last-seen timestamps (E10); all honestly `unknown` where unprobed (¬ß7); tested field folds + the offline OUI lookup + fingerprint‚Üítype mapping. *(EXPLORER-1 model extension; enrichment probes ride EXPLORER-2's scan)*
- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-10: the IPAM prefix/IP table mode.** **As** an operator, **I want** a NetBox-style address view, **so that** I can see what's on my networks. **Acceptance:** a third surface mode (beside Hero) ‚Äî a live table of every discovered subnet/prefix (mesh 10.42/‚Ä¶, LAN 172.20/‚Ä¶, OpenStack tenant nets) with each address' occupant unit, free/used count, gateway (E7); rendered live from discovery (no manual allocation); rows jump to the occupant's hero unit; Carbon productive-density table; tested prefix aggregation + occupancy from the unit set. *(after EXPLORER-3 + EXPLORER-7)*
- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-11: the mosaic overview + summary strip + zoom transition + D-pad grid.** **As** a user, **I want** a whole-fleet landing, **so that** I see everything before focusing one. **Acceptance:** the Discovery surface lands on a category-clustered mosaic of mini hero tiles (O1); a slim summary/filter strip on top shows per-category counts + health rollup (green/warn/down) + total addresses, doubling as the category chips (O2/#8); picking a tile shared-element **zooms into** its full hero, Back/Esc zooms out (O3); three-mode switch Mosaic‚áÑHero‚áÑIPAM; full arrow/D-pad grid nav + focus ring (O6); Carbon tokens; tested mode switch + tile‚Üíhero zoom + grid nav + rollup counts. *(supersedes part of EXPLORER-3's scope ‚Äî EXPLORER-3 narrows to the hero-card mode; serialise both after EXPLORER-1)*
- [‚úì] **EXPLORER-12: ambient idle auto-cycle.** **As** an operator, **I want** a living wall display, **so that** an unattended screen still informs. **Acceptance:** after an idle interval the hero slowly auto-advances through units, pausing on ANY input; a toggle enables it (OFF by default), persisted; never fights user input; tested idle-advance + input-pause. *(after EXPLORER-11)*
- [ ] **EXPLORER-13: view/selection/filter persistence.** **As** a user, **I want** my place kept, **so that** re-opening is continuous. **Acceptance:** the last mode (Mosaic/Hero/IPAM), last-selected unit id, and active filter/search persist in the shell config + restore on open (O5); survives lock/unlock + restart; tested round-trip restore + graceful fallback when the remembered unit is gone. *(after EXPLORER-11)*
- [ ] **EXPLORER-14: universal search + jump.** **As** a user, **I want** to find any unit by any field, **so that** scale doesn't slow me. **Acceptance:** `/` opens a search matching across name/IP/MAC/type/node/service (O7) over a self-contained fuzzy matcher (reuse the editor's `fuzzy` idiom if shareable, else local); results jump the hero/mosaic focus; tested field-spanning matches ("5900"‚ÜíVNC host, "nova"‚Üíinstance, MAC prefix, node name). *(after EXPLORER-11)*
- [ ] **EXPLORER-15: per-category visual identity (accent + glyph family).** **As** a user, **I want** instant category recognition, **so that** I know each unit's world at a glance. **Acceptance:** Mesh/LAN/Cloud each get a distinct Carbon accent token + coherent glyph family applied to tiles/chips/status-rings (O8); tokens live in `mde-theme`/`mde-egui::Style` (¬ß4, no raw hex); tested token application per category. *(mde-theme token add + shell usage; can land early/parallel to EXPLORER-11)*
- [ ] **EXPLORER-16: pinning + Pinned cluster.** **As** a user, **I want** my key units up front, **so that** they're always one glance away. **Acceptance:** pin any unit (key/right-click); pinned sort to the front of mosaic + filmstrip + get a Pinned filter chip (O9); persisted in shell config; tested pin/unpin + ordering + chip filter. *(after EXPLORER-11)*
- [ ] **EXPLORER-17: multi-select + armed bulk actions.** **As** an operator, **I want** fleet operations, **so that** I act on many units at once. **Acceptance:** mark N units in the mosaic (shift/ctrl/D-pad-mark); the action bar offers verbs the selection SHARES (reboot instances, health-check peers) executed per-unit with a progress rollup; destructive verbs keep the typed-arming (O10, reuses EXPLORER-5's arming); no dead bulk verb (only shared+real, ¬ß7); tested selection‚Üíshared-verb set + armed dispatch + rollup. *(after EXPLORER-5 + EXPLORER-11)*
- [ ] **EXPLORER-18: accessibility ‚Äî large-type + focus ring + text-scale.** **As** any user, **I want** legibility + keyboard clarity, **so that** it works across the room + by keyboard. **Acceptance:** generous display type, a high-contrast focus ring that always shows the selection (D-pad essential, O11), and honoring the platform text-scale setting throughout; Carbon tokens; tested focus-ring presence on every navigable element + text-scale response. *(folds into EXPLORER-11's nav; verified as its own acceptance)*
- [ ] **EXPLORER-6: live smoke + wiring verify on the test bed.** **As** the operator, **I want** proof it works live, **so that** it's not just green tests. **Acceptance:** on a live node, opening Discovery shows self + real mesh peers + real LAN hosts (incl. testvm-lin 172.20.146.144) + real OpenStack objects once QC compute is up; a cloud instance console opens; the scan is surface-gated (no probe traffic when closed, verified). *(integration cap; after 1‚Äì5 + QC live)*

## TESTVM ‚Äî Spice/VNC/RDP test endpoints for the VDI bed (operator 2026-07-03; `/plan`; design: docs/design/vdi-test-endpoints.md)

Throwaway XCP-ng VMs on a dom0 (LAN-bridged, `172.20.x`) giving the shell's Desktop/VDI surface real targets. Basic connection only. AUTHORIZED (live VDI test bed + blanket op-authorize) ‚Äî provisioning is live-infra; probe the classifier before exec.

- [‚úì] **TESTVM-1: provisioning scaffold + local images.** **As** a tester, **I want** a repeatable bringup, **so that** the test VMs are easy to (re)create + tear down. **Acceptance:** a dom0 with headroom chosen by live capacity; a locally-reachable **Alpine** image mirrored (airgap) + a check for a local **Windows** ISO/template (record present/absent); an `xe`/tofu bringup path (reuse `infra/tofu/xen-xapi` where it fits) + a documented teardown (`vm-shutdown`/`vm-destroy`). *(done: eea31e0 ‚Äî install-helpers/testvm-up.sh (live capacity probe ‚Üí dom0 .9 chosen 9299MiB free; airgap sha512-verified Alpine mirror; NoCloud seed; xe assemble; IP discovery; endpoint verify; --probe mode) + testvm-down.sh (vm-shutdown --force + vm-uninstall + orphan-VDI sweep). No Windows ISO on either dom0 ‚Äî recorded for TESTVM-3 (Alpine+xrdp fallback).)*
- [‚úì] **TESTVM-2: `testvm-lin` (Alpine) ‚Äî Spice + VNC endpoints.** **As** a tester, **I want** a Linux guest serving Spice + VNC on the LAN, **so that** I can test those viewers. **Acceptance:** Alpine VM boots on the dom0, gets a `172.20.x` address, runs a Spice server (:5930) + `x11vnc` (:5900); both ports reachable from the shell host; a viewer shows its framebuffer. Basic (no/trivial auth). *(done: eea31e0 ‚Äî testvm-lin uuid 9ce6b326‚Ä¶ on dom0 172.20.0.9, DHCP 172.20.146.144. VNC :5900 (x11vnc/Xvfb) ‚Äî full RFB 003.008 handshake + 270KB framebuffer pulled; Spice :5930 ‚Äî real SpiceLinkMess/REDQ link (Xspice segfaults on Alpine 3.24 ‚Üí honest nested qemu -spice fallback, baked into script). Reboot-persistent via /etc/local.d. TESTVM-4 = point the Desktop chooser at :5900/:5930.)*
- [ ] **TESTVM-3: `testvm-win` ‚Äî RDP endpoint (fallback Alpine+xrdp).** **As** a tester, **I want** an RDP target, **so that** I can test the ironrdp path. **Acceptance:** a Windows VM boots with Remote Desktop enabled (:3389) reachable on the LAN; OR ‚Äî if no local Windows image ‚Äî an **Alpine+`xrdp`** guest on :3389 (documented degradation, operator-flagged). `mde-vdi-rdp` connects and shows the login/desktop.
- [ ] **TESTVM-4: shell Desktop-chooser connects to each endpoint.** **As** a user, **I want** the Desktop surface to connect to the test endpoints, **so that** the VDI path is proven end-to-end. **Acceptance:** the shell's Desktop chooser is pointed at each endpoint and establishes a basic session over VNC, Spice, and RDP respectively; each viewer renders the guest. (Live-verify; the DRM seat part may need real display hardware per the VDI-bed note.)

### QUASAR-CLOUD ‚Äî the mesh becomes an OpenStack cloud (design: `docs/design/quasar-cloud.md`, 90-Q `/plan` survey 2026-07-03)

**Replacement epic** (operator: "replace the methods in the platform today when possible"). Nova/libvirt replace the mesh-native VM stack; Glance+DIB replace the golden-image script; Cinder adds volumes; Neutron/OVN puts instances on one flat mesh-bridged net; Designate replaces naming; the Controller plane becomes the Cloud plane. Nebula, etcd, Syncthing, Podman, mde-bus, netdata, chat, ISO installer all KEPT. Hard per-node cutover; replaced code deleted same-epic (¬ß7). Parallel to E12; dev cloud on farm VMs.

- [ ] **QC-1: host virt foundation in the image.**
  **As** a mesh operator, **I want** libvirt/QEMU-KVM + OVN host bits baked into the one bootc image, **so that** any node can carry cloud duties without breaking immutability.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [ ] the image ships libvirt/qemu-kvm + OVN; `virsh version` + `ovs-vsctl show` work on a stock node
    - [ ] cloud-hypervisor is absent from the image (Q32); the virtio-gpu‚Üíegui path re-validated on QEMU or a blocker filed
- [‚úì] **QC-2: mackesd `openstack` worker.** *(done: ad1bef8 ‚Äî workers/openstack/{mod,catalog,fleet,podman,reconcile,testkit}; 14 ServiceKinds (Q24 MVP + foundation trio); FleetStateSource + PodmanRunner seams (reuses MV-4 argv builders ¬ß6); pure plan_converge + converge_cycle on spawn_blocking 15s tick; mirror state/openstack/<node> publish-on-change + 60s heartbeat; killed-container restart unit-tested; honest IntegrationGates ‚Üí QC-3 (kolla archives), QC-4 (doctrine record + config render); census rank-0 deliberate; mackesd 30/30+14/14, clippy 0.)*
  **As** the platform, **I want** a mackesd worker that renders Kolla config from fleet state and supervises the service containers, **so that** the cloud obeys the one-state doctrine with no deploy tool.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] worker reads etcd/Syncthing fleet state and materializes per-service Podman units + Kolla config on its node
    - [ ] per-service health published on the Bus; a killed container restarts; `[!]`-grade failures surface in chat
- [‚úì] **QC-3: Kolla image transport over Syncthing.** *(done: 734d41f ‚Äî images.rs: archive layout `<share>/kolla/<release>/<basename>-<release>.tar` + SHA256SUMS; on absent image ‚Üí check_archive ‚Üí typed ArchiveStatus; ONLY Verified (sha256 matches) ‚Üí podman load (600s); ChecksumMismatch/SumsUnavailable/ShareAbsent/ArchiveMissing/ReadFailed ‚Üí sharper Gated reason (+alert on mismatch/IO), load NEVER called on unverified (unit-asserted); share root = existing workgroup_root; openstack 44/44, clippy 0. No registry pull ‚Äî the airgap trust boundary.)*
  **As** an operator, **I want** service images distributed as archives on the mesh share and `podman load`ed locally, **so that** deploys need no registry and work offline.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] a pinned Kolla release lands on `/mnt/mesh-storage`; nodes load images from it; checksums verified; no `quay.io` pull at deploy time
- [‚úì] **QC-4: foundation services ‚Äî DB, MQ, coordination.**
  **As** the platform, **I want** leader-hosted MariaDB, clustered RabbitMQ (quorum queues), tooz on the mesh etcd, and per-node memcached, **so that** the control plane has no permanently-special node.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] MariaDB rides the etcd leader and re-places on failover; APIs recover (design acceptance #3)
    - [ ] RabbitMQ cluster survives one node down; tooz locks work against the mesh etcd
- [‚úì] **QC-5: Keystone + the identity bridge.**
  **As** a mesh member, **I want** enrollment to provision my Keystone identity and nodes to mint tokens invisibly, **so that** the mesh account IS the cloud account (Q21/62/87).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] a newly-enrolled member exists in Keystone with no manual step; the Cloud plane opens with no login
    - [ ] the CA/KDC no longer holds human cloud credentials (machine certs only)
- [‚úì] **QC-6: core APIs on every node.**
  **As** the platform, **I want** Keystone/Glance/Nova/Placement/Neutron/Cinder API containers on every OpenStack-carrying node, bound plaintext to the Nebula interface, **so that** the control plane is distributed and overlay-secured (Q5/22/23).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] `openstack endpoint list` resolves to a mesh name reaching any healthy node; APIs unreachable from non-Nebula interfaces
- [‚úì] **QC-7: Neutron/OVN flat mesh network.**
  **As** a member, **I want** instances on one flat provider network bridged into the mesh with default-open security groups and LAN floating IPs, **so that** an instance is "inside" and reachable from any peer with no per-instance certs (Q43/44/45/48/49).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] an instance is reachable from a different mesh peer with no floating IP; tenant MTU set for Geneve-over-Nebula; a LAN FIP pool exists per site
- [‚úì] **QC-8: Cinder LVM + backups.**
  **As** a member, **I want** volumes carved from each node's writable partition with cinder-backup to the object tiers, **so that** data survives instances (Q51/56/57/59).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] create/attach/detach/snapshot round-trip green; a backup lands in the object tier and restores
- [‚úì] **QC-9: Glance + DIB image pipeline.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** Glance (local store + replication) fed by a diskimage-builder pipeline, **so that** the golden-image script retires (Q36/53).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] DIB builds the platform's standard images into Glance; `build-mde-vm-golden.sh` deleted; images replicate across API nodes
- [‚úì] **QC-10: capacity-derived flavors + hard per-user quotas.**
  **As** the platform, **I want** flavors generated from real node shapes and quotas derived from real capacity divided into enforced per-user limits, **so that** guardrails are honest (Q29/39/89).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] flavor set regenerates when a node joins/leaves; exceeding a per-user quota is rejected by Keystone/Nova and surfaced in the UI
- [‚úì] **QC-11: typed verbs wrap the cloud.**
  **As** the platform, **I want** the mackesd Bus verbs (boot/stop/rebuild/volume/net/image) reimplemented over the OpenStack APIs, **so that** ¬ß9's contract holds and GUIs never speak raw OpenStack (Q40).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] every Cloud-plane action round-trips through a typed verb; verb-level integration tests (QC-16) exercise them
- [ ] **QC-12: the Cloud plane (Controller plane replaced).**
  **As** a member, **I want** the Workbench Controller plane to become the Cloud plane ‚Äî instances, volumes+snapshots, images, networks+stacks, full launch picker, per-user usage view, **so that** every member self-serves from the shell (Q70/82/83/85).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] full picker launches an instance end-to-end; all five resource kinds manageable; fleet-state template records render as launch presets (Q84)
- [ ] **QC-13: instance access ‚Äî console + keys.**
  **As** a member, **I want** a one-click SPICE console (mde-vdi-spice viewer) and automatic SSH key injection, **so that** getting into my instance is trivial (Q34/88).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] console opens from the Cloud plane row; a launched instance accepts the member's mesh-derived SSH key
- [ ] **QC-14: VDI broker overlay on Nova.**
  **As** a desktop user, **I want** the session-broker to place VDI desktops as Nova instances (flavor+metadata) while owning the display path/roaming/seat binding, **so that** one VM plane serves both worlds (Q33).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] a VDI session boots via Nova and renders through the existing viewer path; roaming = rebuild per Q38
- [ ] **QC-15: hard cutover + deletion.**
  **As** the platform, **I want** per-node cutover flags and same-epic deletion of the replaced stack (mde-kvm scheduler paths, cloud-hypervisor glue, Cockpit VM console, golden script), **so that** no dead code survives (Q72/73/66).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] a cutover node runs zero old-stack VM code; `/audit` finds no orphaned modules from the replaced stack; existing VMs rebuilt fresh (Q58)
- [ ] **QC-16: verb-level CI on the farm dev cloud.**
  **As** the platform, **I want** Rust integration tests driving boot/net/volume round-trips through the verbs against a farm-VM dev cloud, **so that** the cloud is continuously proven (Q74/75).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] IaC brings up disposable virtual mesh nodes on the farm; the test suite runs in the GitOps lane and gates regressions
- [ ] **QC-17: Designate replaces naming.**
  **As** the platform, **I want** Designate serving mesh zones fed by the peer directory, **so that** nodes, instances, and services resolve by DNS everywhere (Q46).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] node + instance records resolve mesh-wide; the peer directory can re-seed Designate from scratch
- [ ] **QC-18: object tiers + media re-platform.**
  **As** the workgroup, **I want** Swift as the hot object tier with DO Spaces off-site, and the media stack (Navidrome) re-platformed as instances, **so that** a real platform feature lives on the cloud (Q54/55/60).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] Swift serves Keystone-authed objects; cinder-backups land in it; Navidrome runs as a Nova instance serving the mesh with media on the tiers
- [‚úì] **QC-19: wave-2 services ‚Äî Heat rendered, Octavia, Horizon.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** Heat stacks rendered from fleet state, Octavia for instance load-balancing, and optional Horizon, **so that** wave 2 lands per the locks (Q25/47/61).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] a fleet-state record renders + applies as a Heat stack; an Octavia LB fronts an instance service; Horizon (if deployed) is reachable mesh-only
- [ ] **QC-20: cloud events into chat + idle nudges.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** OpenStack notifications folded into the mesh chat (services as roster contacts) and idle instances nudging their owners, **so that** the one notification surface covers the cloud (Q65/90).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] an instance failure arrives as a signed chat message from the service contact; an idle instance triggers an owner nudge
- [>] **QC-21: docs ‚Äî the four deliverables.** *(authored b9afd0a: `docs/ops/quasar-cloud-runbook.md` (services-per-node, leader failover drill, airgap Kolla mirror procedure), `docs/help/cloud-self-service.md` (ships via the existing RPM help glob), `docs/ops/quasar-cloud-cutover-map.md` (dies‚Üíreplacement + KEPT tables + verification checklist), DISCLAIMER.md ENT-12 blast-radius extension. Stays `[>]`: the acceptance's "docs match shipped behavior" can only close as QC-1..20 land ‚Äî each doc carries a status header saying it tracks the LOCKED design.)*
  **As** an operator/member, **I want** the operator runbook, the ENT-12 blast-radius update (instances are "inside"), the replaced-vs-kept architecture map, and the member how-to, **so that** the claim is operable and honest (Q77).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] all four docs exist and match the shipped behavior; the blast-radius doc covers default-open groups + hard quotas
- [ ] **QC-22: SELinux tightening.**
  **As** the platform, **I want** the initially-permissive OpenStack domains moved to enforcing with the proper policy modules, **so that** the RH-conventions claim becomes fully true (Q14).
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] OpenStack services run enforcing with zero new AVC denials over a soak; the hardening documented


## SETTINGS ‚Äî world-class Settings redesign: master-detail, tinted, Carbon (operator 2026-07-04; 5-Q `/plan`; design: docs/design/settings-redesign.md)

Locks: master-detail rail + full-width detail pane; categorical accent tint + Carbon elevation layers; grouped by domain (Devices / Personalization / Mesh & System); Carbon expressive density; rail nav only (no search). Replaces the single-column stack in `crates/desktop/mde-shell-egui/src/system.rs`. Reuse every existing section body + its `apply()`/`SysAction` seam verbatim (¬ß6) ‚Äî a presentation/routing pass, not a rewrite.

- [‚úì] **SETTINGS-1: the master-detail shell.** **As** a user, **I want** Settings to use the whole page, **so that** it stops being a cramped column. **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable): a left `SidePanel` rail lists the 3 domain groups (Devices / Personalization / Mesh & System) each with its section rows; a right detail pane fills the remaining width and renders ONLY the selected section's body (reusing the existing per-section fns); the active section is highlighted; every existing section (Mixer/Bluetooth/Displays/Power/Wallpaper/Hotkeys) is reachable exactly once and its actions still dispatch; a `SettingsNav {group,section}` selection persists in the shell config across surface switches + restart; Carbon expressive spacing; tested rail render + section route + all-sections-reachable + nav persistence round-trip. *(touches system.rs + main.rs Surface::System arm; serialize vs the browser live-helper main.rs edit)*
- [‚úì] **SETTINGS-2: categorical accent + Carbon layer elevation.** **As** a user, **I want** areas visually separated by color, **so that** I read structure at a glance. **Acceptance**: three domain accent tokens REUSED from the existing `Style::ACCENT_*` set (coordinated with PICKER-2 + EXPLORER-15 ‚Äî one shared token language, defined once, ¬ß4); rail group headers + the active detail header take their group accent; page = layer-01, cards = layer-02 with hairline borders; NO raw hex / scattered metric literals (grep-clean); tested accent-per-group application + the layer/border rendering. *(mde-egui::Style/mde-theme token use + system.rs)*
- [‚úì] **SETTINGS-3: expressive detail layouts that use the width.** **As** a user, **I want** wide sections laid across, **so that** the space isn't wasted. **Acceptance**: each section body reflows to the wide pane ‚Äî Displays lays outputs in a row of cards, Bluetooth puts adapters + devices in columns, Mixer spreads channels across, Power shows battery + profiles side by side; the section LOGIC (`apply()`/`SysAction`) is unchanged (¬ß6/¬ß7 ‚Äî presentation only); tested each section renders its controls in the wide layout + the actions still fire. *(system.rs section bodies)*
- [‚úì] **SETTINGS-4: the Mesh & System group.** **As** an operator, **I want** identity/role/pairing/network in Settings, **so that** the node's mesh facts are one place. **Acceptance**: the Mesh & System group surfaces Identity (mesh cert/name), Role (the pinned role), Pairing (folds in the existing `sync_pairing_agent` KDC pairing flow), and Network (overlay/underlay facts) from REAL node state, honest-`unknown` where unprobed (¬ß7); Pairing drives the existing agent; tested each section renders live data + the pairing action dispatches. *(system.rs + reuse the pairing/role/mesh seams the shell already reads)*
- [‚úì] **SETTINGS-5: the Personalization Theme section.** **As** a user, **I want** an appearance section, **so that** I can tune the look. **Acceptance**: a new Theme section under Personalization exposing accent choice + text-scale (reusing the EXPLORER-18 accessibility posture) + any light/dark the shell supports, all honest to what the runtime actually applies (no dead toggles, ¬ß7); persists in shell config; tested the controls apply + persist. *(system.rs + Style/mde-theme)* *(done: new `theme_section` under Personalization ‚Äî **accent choice** re-tints the live interactive `Style` accent across every surface via a new `mde_egui::Style::set_accent` (7 curated choices, each an existing `ACCENT*` token, no new hex); **text-scale** = the EXPLORER-18 whole-UI zoom in 5 steps (0.9‚Äì1.5√ó), applied as `zoom_factor` atop the seat's DPI base so it composes with hi-DPI, not clobbers it. NO light/dark switch (platform is dark-only ‚Äî no dead toggle, ¬ß7). Both apply GLOBALLY every frame from `SystemState::poll` (both runners, restored on start) + persist as `settings-appearance.json` (the SettingsNav idiom). mde-shell-egui 500 + mde-egui 116 tests green (7 new SETTINGS-5 + refactored accent test), clippy clean on the touched files, style-leak + tier lints clean.)*
- [ ] **SETTINGS-6: live smoke on the seat.** **As** the operator, **I want** the redesign verified on a real seat, **so that** it's truly done. **Acceptance**: on Eagle / the test bed the redesigned Settings renders on the DRM seat ‚Äî rail + wide detail, accent tint + layers visible, every section reachable, a real action fires (Bluetooth toggle or display mode change); captured/confirmed. *(runtime verify; ¬ß7 live-verify)*


## NODE-GRADE ‚Äî per-node A‚ÄìF capability grade in the vertical dock (operator 2026-07-04; 20-Q `/plan`; design: docs/design/node-grade.md)

Locks: a stacked A‚ÄìF grade per mesh node above the VDOCK-3 status quads; green‚Üíred; blink at D/F; four weighted factors (resources heaviest); classic 90/80/70/60 bands; each node self-grades + publishes; smoothed ~15‚Äì30s; blend health+headroom; local pinned first, peers worst-first; trend arrow; tap‚ÜíExplorer hero; worst-N overflow; notify feed on drop to D/F.

- [‚úì] **NODE-GRADE-1: the node self-grade worker (mackesd).** **As** an operator, **I want** each node to grade its own capability, **so that** the fleet's health is legible at a glance. **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable): a rank-0 `node_grade` worker computes four 0‚Äì100 factor scores (CPU load/headroom, RAM+disk free, role/worker health + no failed services, mesh reachability), each blending health + spare headroom (#17); a weighted average (resources heaviest, #13) ‚Üí an A‚ÄìF band (90/80/70/60), smoothed ~15‚Äì30s, plus a recent-slope trend; publishes `{grade,score,factors,trend}` to `<root>/node-grade/<hostname>.json` on the substrate (SEC-5 mesh-shunt pattern); on a transition into D/F emits a debounced `event/notify/*` alert (CHAT-FIX-2). Reuses the existing telemetry (¬ß6, no new probes). Census `("node_grade",0)`; tested: factor scoring, band mapping, smoothing/trend, the drop-to-D/F alert, honest-absent.
- [‚úì] **NODE-GRADE-2: the dock grade mini-list (mde-shell-egui).** **As** a user, **I want** the grades above the notification icons, **so that** a struggling node is obvious. **Acceptance:** `dock.rs` renders a stacked grade list in the bottom zone ABOVE the VDOCK-3 status quads ‚Äî the local node pinned first with a "you are here" marker (#18), peers worst-grade-first (#19); each row = the A‚ÄìF letter in the green‚Üíred `Style` token (#4) + a tiny load bar (#5) + a ‚Üë/‚Üí/‚Üì trend arrow (#14); D/F blinks hard on/off (always, #6/#16); tapping a node routes to its Explorer hero (#7); overflow shows worst-N + a "‚Ä¶" popup (#8); no header (#15); honest dim pre-poll. Reads the published grades via the dock's status-input seam (extend `set_status_inputs`). All `Style`/`Motion` tokens (¬ß4). Tested: layout above the quads, sort/pin, blink at D/F, tap-route, overflow. *(serialize on dock.rs vs the VDOCK churn ‚Äî land on the settled vertical-dock base)*
- [ ] **NODE-GRADE-3: the A‚ÄìF color-ramp tokens (mde-egui Style).** **As** the shell, **I want** one grade palette, **so that** every grade UI is consistent. **Acceptance:** `GRADE_A..GRADE_F` green‚Üíred tokens in `mde-egui::Style` (reuse the status palette where it already covers the ramp; add only what's missing), no raw hex (¬ß4), with a backing `mde-egui` test; consumed by NODE-GRADE-2. *(shared-kit; coordinate with the status/accent palette)*
- [ ] **NODE-GRADE-4: live smoke on the test bed.** **As** the operator, **I want** the grades verified live, **so that** it's truly done. **Acceptance:** on Eagle/the test bed the dock shows real per-node grades from live telemetry, a stressed node's grade drops + blinks + posts a feed notification, tapping opens the Explorer hero. *(runtime verify; ¬ß7 live-verify)*


## BROWSER-DD ‚Äî the daily-driver browser (operator 2026-07-04; 100-Q `/plan`; design: docs/design/browser-daily-driver.md)

A dual-engine (keep sandboxed Servo + ADD CEF/Chromium for compat) mesh-native, privacy-forward, Quasar-styled browser. Phased; Phase-1 pillars first. Reuses the BOOKMARKS-5/6 offscreen-render-into-egui helper architecture. Each task's full spec is in the design doc.

### Phase 1 ‚Äî the daily-driver MVP
- [‚úì] **BROWSER-DD-0: BUGFIX ‚Äî the browser never rendered any page (`run_tab` socket-protocol stub).** **As** a user, **I want** pages to actually render instead of hanging on "Loading the page‚Ä¶", **so that** the browser works at all. **Root cause:** `mde-web-preview`'s `tab` serve loop (`main.rs::run_tab`) was a STUB ‚Äî it created the shm `FrameChannel`, `println!`'d `SHM_FD` to stdout, and looped `pump_step`+sleep with ZERO socket I/O, so it never sent `AttachFrame`/`PaintReady` over the session socket. The client (`WebSession`) only reaches `Live` (clears the "Loading‚Ä¶" note) on a `PaintReady` after an `AttachFrame` maps the shm fd, so EVERY url hung ‚Äî not google-specific; the interactive browser had never worked. **Fix (landed):** (1) `run_tab` now speaks the BOOKMARKS-6 protocol in the confined child ‚Äî wraps the session socket (the shell hands it as stdin/fd 0), sends `EventMsg::AttachFrame` + the shm fd via `SCM_RIGHTS`, then loops applying `ControlMsg` nav (Load/Reload/Back/Forward ‚Üí the engine's methods; Resize/Input/verdict decoded-but-not-yet-wired), pumping a step, and signalling `PaintReady{seq}` on any delivered frame; a ~750ms first-frame watchdog force-emits so a slow/heavy SPA never hangs the shell ‚Äî delivery is keyed on a delivered frame, NEVER on `LoadStatus::Complete`. (2) new `Engine::force_emit` (the watchdog path: paint+present+read-back+emit without a fresh frame-ready). (3) client Layer-A shm fallback in `WebSession::poll` ‚Äî promotes to Live straight from the seqlock sequence, self-healing a `PaintReady` that arrived before `AttachFrame`. **Protocol sharing:** the excluded helper can't depend on the client, so it `#[path]`-includes the client's ONE `wire.rs` (single byte-exact source) + a minimal local `sock.rs` (SCM mechanism only); pinned by golden byte-compat tests on both ends. Tests: client Layer-A + early-PaintReady self-heal + golden (green, 40/40); helper wire golden + `sock` round-trips; `render-once` prints `FRAME_OK ‚Ä¶ distinct= mean_luma=` + `FORCE_OK` (force_emit live-exercise, separate process since Servo is one-instance-per-process). *(the release/RPM story unchanged: [[rpm-cut-needs-servo-build]] ‚Äî the excluded helper still builds via `--manifest-path`)*
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-1: CEF engine integration.** **As** a user, **I want** a real Chromium engine, **so that** every site works. **Acceptance:** vendor prebuilt CEF binaries on the farm (workspace-EXCLUDED like mde-web-preview); a new `mde-web-cef` helper renders offscreen into the BOOKMARKS-6 shm/texture seam; the `mde-web-preview-client` live-helper spawn launches either engine (Servo|CEF, user-selectable); a real site (e.g. Gmail) renders. *(heavy; the release/RPM story like [[rpm-cut-needs-servo-build]])*
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-2: tabs + omnibox + compat chrome.** **As** a user, **I want** normal browsing, **so that** it's usable. **Acceptance:** standard tabs (open/close/switch/reorder) with a vertical-tabs option; unified URL+search omnibox with live SearXNG suggestions; back/fwd/reload/stop; HTTPS-only-with-prompt; block-3rd-party-cookies + clear-on-close; the Quasar-dashboard new-tab (SearXNG + mesh services); tested reachable.
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-3: native ad/tracker blocking + privacy hardening.** **Acceptance:** uBlock-class native blocker on mesh-synced subscribable filter lists + custom rules + per-site toggle; anti-fingerprinting; per-site permission prompts + manager (default-deny); mesh-hosted safe-browsing blocklists; per-site data manager + forget; zero telemetry.
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-4: Widevine DRM.** **Acceptance:** the Widevine CDM fetched at first run (Firefox-style, not redistributed); DRM streaming (Netflix/Spotify web) plays on the CEF engine; the browser is fully functional (non-DRM) without it (honest gate).
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-5: WebExtensions (curated allowlist) + LastPass.** **Acceptance:** the CEF engine runs a VETTED allowlist of WebExtensions (LastPass, uBlock, password managers) from a mesh-hosted extension registry (sideload in Power mode); standard Chrome permission model; LastPass installs + autofills. *(CEF extension support is partial ‚Äî validate/host-shim as needed)*
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-6: WebAuthn / passkeys.** **Acceptance:** hardware security keys (FIDO2) + platform passkeys in a mesh-synced encrypted authenticator + phone-as-authenticator (KDC); passwordless login works end-to-end.
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-7: mesh sync + follow-me tabs + send-tab.** **Acceptance:** tabs/session + bookmarks + settings/speed-dial + downloads list sync over the Nebula+Syncthing substrate (no external account, E2E); follow-me tabs (your live set on any node); send-tab to nodes AND paired phones; startup restores the synced session.

### Phase 2 ‚Äî power + media + chrome
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-8: Power mode + power menu + downloader + scraper.** **Acceptance:** a single Power-mode toggle (off=clean; on=the Power menu) surfacing full Chromium DevTools + view-source + UA-switch + device APIs (prompted) + the native media downloader (HLS/DASH video, all-images, media sniffer, ignore-blocking, auto-rename+metadata) + the full site scraper (extract/crawl/export CSV¬∑JSON¬∑MD) + userscripts.
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-9: media + mesh conferencing.** **Acceptance:** full codecs (incl. H.264/H.265) + full WebRTC + PiP + background audio + media keys + GPU/HW video decode; block-all autoplay; a built-in MULTI-PARTY mesh conferencing app over WebRTC on the Nebula overlay (screen-share, peer-directory participants, phone ties).
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-10: browser chrome + UX.** **Acceptance:** fixed Quasar toolbar; container tabs; force-dark (Quasar-tuned) on light sites; full download manager (fixed folder); built-in PDF viewer; full print/save-as-PDF (CUPS); full capture (full-page/region/PDF-MHTML/annotate); reader mode; per-tab audio mute; page zoom; find-in-page; multi-display.
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-11: accessibility + TTS + voice + userscript library.** **Acceptance:** screen-reader (accesskit) + forced-dark + keyboard nav + a best-of-breed open-source TTS engine (Piper/Kokoro-class) + voice commands/dictation (on-device STT) + offline-hunspell spellcheck; a bundled library of ~100 curated userscripts for major sites (YouTube/NPR/Spotify/news‚Ä¶).
- [ ] **BROWSER-DD-12: platform integration + the long tail.** **Acceptance:** private offline/mesh translation; auto-suspend idle tabs; offline cache + mesh peer cache; protocol handling (mailto‚Üíemail, tel‚ÜíVOIP, magnet); web notifications + download/capture events ‚Üí the mesh notify feed; share to peer/Chat/phone/email/QR; rich bookmarks (folders/tags/search/dead-link); independent security updater.


## TMUX-FC ‚Äî first-class tmux control chrome (operator 2026-07-04; 16-Q `/plan`; design: docs/design/tmux-first-class.md)

Make tmux first-class in mde-term-egui via iTerm2-style control mode (`tmux -CC`): tmux windows‚Üínative tabs, panes‚Üínative splits, driven by full GUI chrome, mesh-aware, persistent. Reuse TERM-4 splits + TERM-5 tabs (¬ß6, no second multiplexer).

- [‚úì] **TMUX-FC-1: control-mode core.** **As** a user, **I want** tmux to drive the native chrome, **so that** it's truly first-class. **Acceptance:** a `tmux -CC` spawn + an incremental control-mode protocol parser (%output/%window-*/%layout-change/%session-changed/%begin-%end); a live sessions‚Üíwindows‚Üípanes model; each tmux window mapped to a `tabs::TabbedTerminal` tab + each pane to a `splits` leaf feeding the TERM-3 widget; GUI ops emit tmux commands and %-events reconcile the GUI; tested against a real tmux (parse + round-trip).
- [‚úì] **TMUX-FC-2: session management chrome.** **Acceptance:** a session/window/pane sidebar tree; create / attach / detach / kill / rename; a picker listing ALL sessions (attached + detached); tested each op issues the tmux command + the tree reflects %-events. *(mde-term-egui `tmux_ui.rs`: the `TmuxChrome` sidebar tree over the live `TmuxModel`; session ops via `TmuxIntent`‚Üí`command_for`‚Üí`tmux::commands` (round-trip, never a direct mutation); the all-sessions picker off the control-channel `list-sessions` reply (`TmuxController::all_sessions`). Session cmd builders + `parse_session_list` added to `tmux.rs`; the menubar tmux seam wired (`TmuxMenuChoice`) as its entry point; mounted in `panel.rs`. Opt-in per lock #16 ‚Äî no auto-attach. Pane-content mount + window/pane mutation ops remain TMUX-FC-3.)*
- [ ] **TMUX-FC-3: window & pane operations.** **Acceptance:** split/close/zoom ¬∑ break/join/swap/move ¬∑ drag-resize (‚Üíresize-pane) + drag-reorder ¬∑ rename window/pane titles ‚Äî each a GUI affordance issuing the tmux command, reconciled by %layout-change; tested.
- [ ] **TMUX-FC-4: native status bar + toolbar + palette + context menus.** **Acceptance:** a native Quasar status bar (window tabs + session + clock, ignoring tmux status config); a toolbar; a curated ~30-command fuzzy palette; right-click context menus on tabs/panes ‚Äî all issuing tmux commands; Style tokens (¬ß4); tested.
- [ ] **TMUX-FC-5: persistence + templates.** **Acceptance:** auto-reattach remembered sessions on relaunch (detached keep running); session templates ("projects") seed a layout + commands; persisted in the platform-managed config; tested reattach + template open.
- [ ] **TMUX-FC-6: mesh tmux.** **As** an operator, **I want** any node's tmux, **so that** my persistent sessions follow the mesh. **Acceptance:** extend remote.rs/roster.rs (SSH-over-overlay) to enumerate + attach `tmux -CC` on peer nodes; the same chrome controls a remote session; tested list + attach path.
- [ ] **TMUX-FC-7: the 5 mesh-styled layout presets.** **Acceptance:** Mesh Ops (meshctl+peers+logs+shell) ¬∑ Node Watch (btop+journal+disk/SMART+shell) ¬∑ Cloud/OpenStack ¬∑ Dev/Build ¬∑ AI-CLI (Claude CLI + Codex CLI + shell) ‚Äî each opens its window/pane layout + seeded commands in the Quasar style; mesh-synced; tested each preset builds its layout.
- [ ] **TMUX-FC-8: config, keys, copy.** **Acceptance:** a platform-managed Quasar tmux config (mesh-synced) + a GUI settings pane (prefix/mouse/history); the tmux prefix passes through AND remappable native GUI chords; native GUI scrollback + selection + search (not tmux copy-mode) with yank into tmux buffers + the mesh clipboard; tested.


## TERM-MENUBAR ‚Äî a top menu bar exposing all terminal features (operator 2026-07-04)

- [‚úì] **TERM-MENUBAR-1: the terminal menu bar.** **As** a user, **I want** a menu bar at the top of the terminal exposing all features, **so that** everything is discoverable without memorizing shortcuts. **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable): a top menu bar on the terminal surface (mde-term-egui) with menus covering EVERY feature ‚Äî File (new tab/window, close), Edit (copy/paste/find/select-all/clear), View (appearance/theme presets, fonts, zoom, toggle status bar), Terminal (new session, reset, broadcast-input, bell settings), Splits (split H/V, navigate, close, zoom, layouts), Tabs (new/close/rename/reorder/detach), Session (mesh/remote roster, attach a peer node), tmux (the TMUX-FC session/window/pane actions ‚Äî wired as those land), Help (shortcuts). Each item drives the REAL existing feature seam (menu.rs/tabs/splits/search/remote/appearance/presets ‚Äî ¬ß6 glue, no dead items ¬ß7); shortcuts shown beside items; Carbon Style tokens (¬ß4). Tested: the menu bar renders all menus, each item dispatches its real action, honest-disabled where a feature needs context. *(mde-term-egui; keep the panel.rs mount minimal ‚Äî coordinate with TMUX-FC-1)*


### DEVMGR ‚Äî Device-Manager hardware inspector in the About surface (25-Q survey 2026-07-04; design: docs/design/about-device-manager.md)

Turn `Surface::About` into a Windows-Device-Manager-style hardware inspector: a faithful categorized device tree in Quasar dark, host-switching across the whole mesh (nodes/Cloud/phones/LAN/VyOS), rich per-device properties, MDM problem-code parity, fleet-wide fault notify, and (P2) real device actions over the overlay. **Serialize the shell units (DEVMGR-2..6/10/11 all touch the new `device_manager.rs` + the About mount ‚Äî land on the settled base, like the VDOCK churn).**

#### Phase 1 ‚Äî read-only inspector (local + mesh nodes)

- [‚úì] **DEVMGR-1: the device-inventory worker + publish.**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** every node to enumerate + publish its own hardware,
  **so that** any host's device tree is readable across the mesh.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] extend an existing inventory worker (`legacy_inventory`/`compute_registry`, NOT a new worker ‚Äî #16) to enumerate the local host's **full Linux taxonomy** (CPU/memory/disk+storage-ctrl/network/GPU/USB/PCI/audio/input/sensors/bluetooth/power) via **sysfs/udev first** (+ `pci.ids`/`usb.ids` names) with `lshw -json`/`dmidecode` shelled out for deep DMI/firmware on demand (#4/#15)
    - [‚úì] each device carries `{name, vendor, model, ids, sysfs_path, driver/module+version, status+problem_code, resources(irq/io/mem), recent_events}`
    - [‚úì] publish the tree to `<workgroup_root>/device-inventory/<hostname>.json` via the SEC-5 mesh-shunt replication (like node_grade); periodic republish + an on-demand live-re-query seam (#7/#8); rank-0 (every node)
    - [‚úì] the shared serde schema lives in a mesh-neutral shared crate (or duplicated with a round-trip test) ‚Äî no ¬ß6 boundary crossing
    - [‚úì] tested: enumeration builds the taxonomy from a fixture sysfs tree, the JSON round-trips, the publish path writes the file
    ‚Äî DONE (2026-07-04, session 4e2f8f4c): folded into the existing rank-0 **`hardware_probe`** worker (the best "whichever fits best" home ‚Äî `legacy_inventory` is a file-catalog core module, `compute_registry` publishes VM/container workloads to the Bus; `hardware_probe` is the existing hardware producer already publishing to `<workgroup_root>` via the SEC-5 idiom, so lock #16 is honored with no new worker/census entry). New engine `mackesd::workers::device_inventory` walks the full taxonomy sysfs-first (`/sys/bus/{pci,usb}`, `/sys/block`, `/sys/class/*`, `/proc/{cpuinfo,meminfo,uptime}`) with `pci.ids`/`usb.ids` names + honest status/problem derivation (PCI no-driver ‚Üí `no-driver`, `enable=0`/de-authorized USB ‚Üí `disabled`, dmesg error ‚Üí `degraded`) + IRQ/io/mem resources + dmesg events; `lshw`/`dmidecode` are best-effort tool-availability flags (#15 honest-degrade). Publishes `<workgroup_root>/device-inventory/<hostname>.json` (atomic temp+rename, keyed on the same stem node_grade uses). **Shared schema in `mackes-mesh-types::device_inventory`** (the mesh-neutral crate that already carries `peer_probe` ‚Äî both `mackesd` + `mde-shell-egui` depend on it, no ¬ß6 crossing; DEVMGR-2 reads this). Farm-green (slot devmgr1, host .90): mackes-mesh-types + mackesd build/clippy clean on the new files; `mackes-mesh-types` 5/5 + `mackesd::workers::device_inventory` 11/11 device tests pass; layered-tiers lint clean; rustfmt clean.

- [‚úì] **DEVMGR-2: About ‚Üí Device Manager shell (local host, by-type).**
  **As** a user,
  **I want** the About surface to become a Device Manager,
  **so that** I can inspect this machine's hardware like Windows.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] a new `device_manager.rs` renders as the body of `Surface::About`; brand ‚Üí a compact `‚óà <name> v<ver>` title strip + an ‚ìò button opening license/credits/mesh-identity in a dialog (#2/#24)
    - [‚úì] the faithful MDM **by-type** device tree in `mde_egui::Style` dark tokens, **all-collapsed** default (#1/#18), reading the LOCAL published inventory (DEVMGR-1)
    - [‚úì] a full **menu bar (Action/View/Help) + toolbar** (Scan, View-mode toggle, Expand/Collapse-all) (#19)
    - [‚úì] a **rich header card** (host ¬∑ OS/kernel ¬∑ uptime ¬∑ CPU/RAM/disk totals ¬∑ device count + problem badge) (#20)
    - [‚úì] style-leak grep clean; tested: tree builds from a fixture inventory, categories group correctly, collapse state, header card fields
    ‚Äî DONE (2026-07-04, session 4e2f8f4c): new `crates/desktop/mde-shell-egui/src/device_manager.rs` (`DeviceManagerState`) is the body of `Surface::About` ‚Äî a compact `‚óà MDE Quazar v<ver>` title strip (single-sourced from `mde_theme::brand`, never a hardcoded name) + an ‚ìò button opening the canonical QBRAND-6 identity screen (`about::about_panel` reused verbatim, ¬ß6) in an `egui::Modal`; a faithful MDM menu bar (Action/View/Help) + toolbar (Scan re-reads the published snapshot, Expand/Collapse-all, the view-mode control) in `mde_egui::Style` dark tokens; the by-type `CollapsingHeader` tree **all-collapsed** by default (#18, external expand-set so Expand/Collapse-all + per-header clicks route through one store), amber-tinted category branches over problem devices + per-device status dot + honest Linux `problem` reason; a rich header card (host ¬∑ OS ¬∑ kernel ¬∑ humanized uptime ¬∑ CPU model+count ¬∑ RAM in GiB ¬∑ device count + problem badge, honest em-dashes for absent fields, lshw-missing hint) fed by `mackes_mesh_types::device_inventory::read_inventory(root, local_host)` on a 30 s cadence + on Scan; honest pre-poll dim "?" before the first read and an honest "nothing published yet" for an empty host (¬ß7). By-connection (DEVMGR-5) + by-node (DEVMGR-4) view modes are honest **disabled** seams, not stubs; the detail drawer (DEVMGR-3), host rail (DEVMGR-4) + export (DEVMGR-6) are clean seams. Farm-green (slot devmgr2, host .130): `mde-shell-egui` build clean; **510/510** tests pass incl. the **10** new `device_manager` tests (fixture tree render, all-collapsed default + expand/collapse-all + toggle, header-card fields, absent-field em-dash, honest pre-poll‚Üíempty read, disabled view modes, ‚ìò dialog render, uptime/mem formatting, status tones, partial-CPU degrade); clippy clean on both touched files (`device_manager.rs`, `main.rs`); rustfmt + style-leak grep + layered-tiers lint clean. **NOT pushed** (operator-gated).

- [‚úì] **DEVMGR-3: the device detail drawer + problem codes.**
    ‚Äî DONE (2026-07-05, session 4e2f8f4c): extended `crates/desktop/mde-shell-egui/src/device_manager.rs` with three landed things. **(a) The bottom detail drawer (#9/#10):** a tree-row click opens a resizable `TopBottomPanel::bottom` drawer (via `show_inside`, tree stays full-width above in a `CentralPanel`) with the five MDM tabs **General / Driver / Details(sysfs+IDs) / Events / Resources** as `selectable_label`s, each populated from the selected `DeviceRecord` ‚Äî honest empty-tab (`muted_note`) when a field/list is absent, em-dash for an absent scalar (¬ß7); selection is a stable `DeviceSelection{category,name,sysfs_path}` resolved against the live inventory each frame, so a re-read never freezes a stale device (a vanished device closes the drawer); a re-click on the open row closes it. **(b) Full MDM problem-code parity (#11):** `problem_code(DeviceStatus)` maps no-driver‚Üí**Code 28**, disabled‚Üí**Code 22**, degraded‚Üí**Code 10**; Ok/Unknown carry **no fabricated code** (honest). The General tab's status box reads "This device is working properly." or "Code N ‚Äî <real Linux reason>"; the tree rows carry a `Code N` badge beside faulted devices. **(c) About chrome onto the shared `mde_egui::menubar::MenuBar`** ‚Äî DEVMGR-2's bespoke Action/View/Help bar + toolbar are **replaced** by the shared component (title "About", accent `Style::ACCENT_SYSTEM`, the `‚óà Magic-Mesh Quasar v<ver>` brand strip kept beside it per #24): **Action**(Scan) ¬∑ **View**(the 3 modes as radio items ‚Äî By type live+checked, the others honest-disabled ¬ß7 ‚Äî + Expand/Collapse-all, gated on a loaded inventory) ¬∑ **Help**(the ‚ìò dialog), each item the mouse-twin of the real seam via `apply()`; right-side **status cluster** = host ¬∑ N devices ¬∑ M problems ¬∑ scanned-time (all off live state). Farm-green (slot devmgr3, host .130): build clean; **562/562** tests (22 `device_manager`, **10** new: the state‚Üícode map, `device_status_display` keeps the real reason, the 5-tab drawer renders per record, drawer prunes a vanished selection, the selection key, the MenuBar menus drive the real seams, expand/collapse gate honestly, `apply` dispatch, the status cluster reflects host/devices/problems + is honest pre-read/clean, scanned-freshness humanize); clippy clean on `device_manager.rs`; rustfmt + style-leak grep + layered-tiers lint clean. **NOT pushed** (operator-gated).

- [‚úì] **DEVMGR-4: the host rail + mesh-node switching.**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** to switch which host I'm inspecting,
  **so that** I can check any node's hardware from one panel.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] a persistent **left host rail** (rail ‚îÇ tree ‚îÇ drawer) listing mesh peer nodes with a status dot + the local "you are here" marker (#5)
    - [‚úì] selecting a host loads its published inventory instantly (**hybrid snapshot**) + a **live-refresh** button re-queries it (#7); a **Scan** action + ~30s auto-refresh (#8); honest dim/stale/offline states
    - [‚úì] tested: rail lists nodes from the peer directory, switching loads the right tree, stale/offline render honestly
    ‚Äî DONE (2026-07-05, session 4e2f8f4c): extended `crates/desktop/mde-shell-egui/src/device_manager.rs` (DEVMGR-4 only ‚Äî no other file touched). **The persistent left host rail (#5):** a full-height `SidePanel::left` reserved first so the About body is now **rail ‚îÇ tree ‚îÇ (bottom drawer)**; it lists every peer that published a `device-inventory/<host>.json` (enumerated via **`mackes_mesh_types::device_inventory::read_all(root)`** ‚Äî one dir read serves both the rail model and the selected host's tree, no second file read) as a clickable row with a freshness/health **status dot**, the **local "you are here" node pinned first** + marked with a ‚åÇ glyph, and a header **‚Üª live-refresh** button. **Host switching (#7 hybrid):** clicking a row `select_host`s it ‚Äî the device drawer + tab reset (a selection is per-host), then an instant re-read loads THAT host's published snapshot; the **tree + header card + drawer + MenuBar status cluster all reflect the selected host**, with local the default on open. **Honest dim/stale/offline (¬ß7):** a new pure `host_freshness(published_at_ms, now)` classifies **Fresh** (dot = OK/green or Danger on a fault) / **Stale** (amber ‚Äî published but older than the 180 s `STALE_AFTER`, or an unknown `published_at_ms == 0`, so its health can't be trusted) / **Absent** (dim ‚Äî nothing published, an honest "?" you can still select ‚Üí the empty-host read, never a fabricated tree); the row hover carries the real counts + freshness read-out, an absent host invents none. Scan (menu) + the ~30 s auto-refresh cadence (DEVMGR-2's `poll`) both flow through the same rebuilt-rail `refresh`. All colours/spacing via `mde_egui::Style` tokens (¬ß4). Farm-green (slot devmgr4, host .130): `mde-shell-egui` build clean; **568/568** tests (28 `device_manager`, **6** new: rail lists every published host with local pinned first, local pinned first even when it published + sorts late, `refresh` reads the rail + switching loads the right host's tree over a real multi-host dir, an unpublished selected host reads an honest empty tree, freshness ‚Üí honest dim/stale/offline dots, the rail renders headless + its hover stays honest); clippy clean on `device_manager.rs`; rustfmt + style-leak grep (zero new hits) + layered-tiers lint clean. **NOT pushed** (operator-gated).

- [‚úì] **DEVMGR-5: the By-connection view mode.**
  **As** a user,
  **I want** the bus-topology view,
  **so that** I can see what hangs off what.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] a **By-connection** view mode (the View toggle) renders the PCI/USB topology tree (host bridge ‚Üí bus ‚Üí device ‚Üí child) from the same inventory (#3)
    - [‚úì] tested: the topology tree nests devices under their parent bus from a fixture
    ‚Äî DONE (2026-07-05, session 4e2f8f4c): extended `crates/desktop/mde-shell-egui/src/device_manager.rs` (DEVMGR-5 only ‚Äî no other file touched). **The By-connection view (#3):** `ViewMode::ByConnection` is now wired (`is_available` = ByType | ByConnection; **By node** stays an honest disabled seam ¬ß7) and selectable from the shared MenuBar's View menu; the About body branches on the active mode, re-rooting the **same** devices under their **parent bus / controller** (host ‚Üí PCI/USB bus segment ‚Üí device) instead of their function category. **Topology source:** the DEVMGR-1 `DeviceRecord` schema carries **no explicit `parent`/`bus` field** ‚Äî the only topology signal is **`sysfs_path`**, so a new pure `build_connection_tree(&DeviceInventory)` reconstructs the hierarchy via `derive_bus(sysfs_path)`: a PCI address ‚Üí its `DDDD:BB` bus segment (`/sys/bus/pci/devices/0000:02:00.0` ‚Üí `PCI bus 0000:02`; a real `/sys/devices/‚Ä¶` path resolves to the device's own bus, not the bridge's), a USB path ‚Üí its bus number, any other `/sys/bus/<kind>/` ‚Üí a title-cased `<Kind> bus`. **Honest degradation (¬ß7):** a device whose path resolves no bus (or has no `sysfs_path`) falls under the **host root** as a leaf ‚Äî never dropped; a host that published **no bus/parent data at all** degrades to a **flat** list under the root with an explicit note (`flat_no_bus`), never a fabricated hierarchy ‚Äî the note flags that a richer bridge/port tree needs a `parent`/`bus` field in the DEVMGR-1 inventory. Bus branches share the one `expanded` store (Expand-all is now mode-aware: category keys in By-type, bus-branch keys in By-connection) and the **device rows + selection + detail drawer (DEVMGR-3) are reused verbatim** ‚Äî only the nesting differs, so a mode flip preserves the selected host (DEVMGR-4's rail selection still governs) and its inventory. Farm-green (slot devmgr5, host .130): `mde-shell-egui` build clean; **585/585** tests (**33** `device_manager`, **5** new: the fixture nests each device under its parent PCI bus, a parentless device stays under the host root, no-bus-data degrades flat with the note, switching to By-connection preserves the selected host + Expand-all fills bus branches + renders headless, `derive_bus` reads PCI/USB/generic paths + honest None; plus the renamed disabled-seam test now asserting By-connection wired / By-node disabled); clippy clean on `device_manager.rs` (`use_self` fix); rustfmt + style-leak grep (zero new hits) + layered-tiers lint clean. **NOT pushed** (operator-gated).

- [ ] **DEVMGR-6: export the device list.**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** to export a host's inventory,
  **so that** I can attach it to a ticket or diff it.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [ ] an Export action produces the current host's inventory as machine **JSON** and a human-readable **Markdown report**, plus copy-to-clipboard (#23)
    - [ ] tested: the JSON round-trips, the Markdown report contains every category + problem summary

#### Phase 2 ‚Äî actions, notify, By-node, non-PC hosts, reach

- [ ] **DEVMGR-7: local device actions (armed).**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** to act on this machine's devices,
  **so that** I can recover a wedged device.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [ ] **Rescan bus** (sysfs `.../rescan`), **Enable/Disable** (driver bind/unbind, `ip link up/down`, USB `authorized`), **Reload kernel module** (rmmod+modprobe), **Properties/Copy-info** (#12) fire on the LOCAL host
    - [ ] destructive actions behind **typed-arming** (type the device/host name ‚Äî reuse EXPLORER-5 arming, #14); the safe ones fire directly
    - [ ] tested: each action maps to its real seam, the arming gate blocks until typed, a rescan/disable dispatches

- [ ] **DEVMGR-8: remote device actions over the overlay.**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** to act on a remote node's devices,
  **so that** I can drive any host's hardware from one panel.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [ ] the DEVMGR-7 actions dispatch on a selected **remote** host over the Nebula overlay (reuse the mackesd run-command / QC-verb / TERM remote seam, #13), typed-armed
    - [ ] a "you may lose reach to this host" warning for network-device actions; every action appends to the KDC hash-chained audit log
    - [ ] tested: a remote action round-trips to the target's action seam + the audit append

- [ ] **DEVMGR-9: fleet-wide device-fault notify.**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** to hear when a device fails on any node,
  **so that** I catch hardware problems without watching the panel.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [ ] a device transitioning INTO a problem state (driver drop, disk I/O errors, NIC down) emits `event/notify/<source>` ‚Üí Chat + phone (CHAT-FIX-2 producer, #21), debounced against flapping (mirror node_grade)
    - [ ] tested: a simulated fault transition fires one debounced notify; a flapping device does not spam

- [ ] **DEVMGR-10: the By-node cross-fleet view.**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** every host's devices in one tree,
  **so that** I can scan the whole fleet's hardware at once.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [ ] a **By-node** view mode flattens all hosts' published inventories into one cross-fleet tree (host ‚Üí its devices), problem hosts near the top (#3)
    - [ ] tested: the By-node tree aggregates multiple fixture hosts + surfaces problem counts per host

- [ ] **DEVMGR-11: non-PC host types.**
  **As** a user,
  **I want** phones, routers, cloud instances + LAN hosts in the inspector,
  **so that** the whole mesh's hardware is visible.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [ ] the host rail also lists **Cloud/Nova instances**, **paired phones**, **LAN-discovered hosts**, and **VyOS/router devices** (#6); each renders **only the categories that apply** (router‚ÜíNetwork/System/Firmware, phone‚ÜíPower/Sensors/Radios, Nova‚Üívirtio, LAN‚Üíremotely-detectable), never an empty category (#22)
    - [ ] each source contributes what it can (Nova via the QC/compute registry, phones via KDC, LAN via probe_nmap, VyOS via SSH/API); honest partial trees
    - [ ] tested: each host type maps to its inventory source + renders only applicable categories

- [ ] **DEVMGR-12: live smoke on the seat.**
  **As** the operator,
  **I want** the Device Manager verified on a real seat,
  **so that** it's truly done.

### MENUBAR-ALL ‚Äî unified title + menu bar on every surface (15-Q survey 2026-07-04; design: docs/design/menubar-all.md)

Every primary nav-bar surface gets a slim top bar: a large UPPERCASE mono accent title (left) + the File/Edit/View/Help spine + surface menus (inline) + a live per-surface status cluster (right), all via one shared `mde-egui` MenuBar. **Governing principle (operator): the menu bar surfaces EVERY control incl. advanced/complex ‚Äî comprehensive, honestly-wired, no dead entries (¬ß7); critical for the OpenStack/IaC interfaces.** One big wave; Terminal + Editor refactor onto the shared component.

- [‚úì] **MENUBAR-ALL-1: the shared `mde-egui` MenuBar component + Terminal/Editor refactor.**
  **As** a mesh operator,
  **I want** one shared title+menu bar widget,
  **so that** every surface reads as one platform.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] a new `mde_egui::menubar` module: a slim `MenuBar` rendering an UPPERCASE mono DISPLAY-tier title (accent-tinted) + an inline menu strip + a right-aligned status-chip cluster, at one consistent height, from `Style`/`Motion`/`fonts` only
    - [‚úì] a caller-supplied menu model (`Menu{title,mnemonic,entries}`, `Item{id,label,shortcut,enabled,checked}` + `Entry::{Item,Submenu,Separator,Caption}`); dropdowns fade in on the shared motion spring; **Alt-mnemonics** (underlined, `resolve_mnemonics`) + egui keyboard nav + 2px accent focus ring; each item shows its live shortcut hint; honest disable/omit (¬ß7)
    - [‚úì] backing tests (model, mnemonic resolution, disabled-item non-activatable, status cluster, title casing, reduce-motion, headless render) in mde-egui; style-leak grep clean
    - [‚úì] **Terminal** (`mde-term-egui/menubar.rs`, incl. the TERM-MENUBAR-1 + TMUX-FC-2 Tmux menu) + **Editor** (Word-97 bar) refactored onto it ‚Äî every existing menu item + seam preserved, their menu tests green (term 290, editor 388)
    - [‚úì] renders correctly at 1.0 + a fractional scale (built on egui layout + `Style` tokens only, no hardcoded pixel positions)

- [‚úì] **MENUBAR-ALL-2..N: per-surface title+menu bars (one big wave).**
    ‚Äî DONE (2026-07-05, session 4e2f8f4c): **all 13 wave surfaces now embed the shared `mde_egui::menubar::MenuBar`** (Terminal + Editor were the MENUBAR-ALL-1 refactor), so every one of the 15 nav surfaces reads as one platform. Per-surface bars landed: Music (`mde-music-egui/menubar.rs`), Media (`mde-media-egui/menubar.rs`), Files (`mde-files-egui/menubar.rs`), Voice (`mde-voice-egui/lib.rs`), Browser (`mde-shell-egui/web.rs`), Chat + Instances + Desktop(`vdi.rs`) + System + Storage + Workbench (`mde-shell-egui/*`), Mesh-View (`mde-mesh-view/menubar.rs`, `MeshMenuBar` over the shared bar), and now **About** (`mde-shell-egui/device_manager.rs`, this unit ‚Äî DEVMGR-3) ‚Äî the **14th/last** surface onto the component. Each carries its UPPERCASE title + category accent + a live status cluster, its real File/Edit/View/Help spine (only where real) + surface-specific menus, every visible item bound to an existing seam with honest disable/omit (¬ß7). All farm-green + tested per surface; About closes the wave.

### IAC ‚Äî the "Infra as Code (IaC)" workspace / OpenStack IaaS control plane (25-Q survey 2026-07-04; design: docs/design/iac-workspace.md)

A new Workloads-group surface "Infra as Code (IaC)": an OpenStack IaaS control plane on the standard APIs ‚Äî Keystone catalog = the service directory, Heat = the native IaC engine, per-service APIs = status + comprehensive control. Lists all published services (OpenStack catalog + mesh/LAN scan, grouped by kind) under a live OpenStack-API status band. Tabbed Overview/Resources/Heat; typed-arming on all mutations; audit-all + notify-on-failure; comprehensive catalog-driven menu bar (the MENUBAR-ALL governing principle). Everything in one cut. Instances (QC-12) stays the quick VM view; IaC is the full admin.

- [‚úì] **IAC-1: the OpenStack client foundation.**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** a standard-API OpenStack client,
  **so that** the workspace speaks OpenStack natively.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] auth via `clouds.yaml` (openstacksdk standard, single default context); the **Keystone service catalog** (services + public/internal/admin endpoints + region); per-service **API health** (real ping/version probe ‚Üí up/down + latency + microversion); the standard resource + verb calls (Nova/Neutron/Glance/Cinder/Heat/‚Ä¶) ‚Äî reuse/extend the QUASAR-CLOUD / mackesd OpenStack integration (¬ß6), not a parallel client
    - [‚úì] honest absent/unreachable when a service isn't deployed; tested against fixtures + (IAC-7) a live cloud
    - **Landed (IAC-1, 2026-07-04):** the client foundation extends the QUASAR-CLOUD `mackesd::workers::openstack` worker with a new `client/` sub-tree ‚Äî `config` (clouds.yaml load + single-context select, password redacted, never on argv), `keystone` (v3 auth ‚Üí token + catalog seam), `health` (per-endpoint version/ping probe seam), `resource` (the list/show/create/update/delete REST seam ‚Äî the IAC-3 boundary) ‚Äî plus a testkit of fakes; all pure logic fixture-tested (37 new unit tests). The ¬ß6 catalog+health wire contract (`ServiceCatalog`/`ServiceHealth`) lives in `mackes-mesh-types::openstack` so IAC-2's `mde-shell-egui` consumes it off the Bus without depending on `mackesd`; runtime-reachable now via the new `action/cloud/get-catalog` read verb on the existing QC-11 Bus seam (honest `Unconfigured` gate on a node with no clouds.yaml). The live-cloud smoke is IAC-6.

- [‚úì] **IAC-2: the surface + Overview tab (status band + merged directory).**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** the API status + every published service in one grouped view,
  **so that** I see the whole infrastructure at a glance.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] `Surface::InfraCode` in the Workloads dock group, name "Infra as Code (IaC)", its Server (infrastructure) glyph; **Overview shown alone this unit** (the Resources/Heat tab bar lands with those tabs in IAC-3/4 ‚Äî no disabled-tab or "coming soon" placeholder, ¬ß7)
    - [‚úì] the **OpenStack API status band** ‚Äî rich tiles from the live catalog (health dot + latency / version + microversion / region / public-internal-admin endpoints + port), consumed off the Bus read verb `action/cloud/get-catalog`; honest "OpenStack not configured" (gated) / "unreachable" (failed) / "querying" states when the cloud/verb is absent (¬ß7). Per-tile actions (logs / restart-armed / self-test / drill) are IAC-3 (they need the Resources verb seam)
    - [‚úì] the **merged service directory** ‚Äî the Keystone catalog grouped by service type (Compute / Network / Image / Volume / Orchestration / Identity / DNS / Object Storage / Placement / Other); rich rows (name / endpoint host:port / health + latency / region). The **Mesh services** group (`descriptors` / `probe_nmap` / mackesd registries scan) + the Rescan button fold in at IAC-3 (a code-level seam here, not rendered)
    - [‚úì] all `mde_egui` tokens (¬ß4); tested ‚Äî the Overview renders from a fixture `ServiceCatalog`+`ServiceHealth`, the honest not-configured / unreachable / querying states render, the reply tri-state folds honestly, grouping-by-type, `Surface::InfraCode` in `Surface::ALL` + the Workloads group
    - **Landed (IAC-2, 2026-07-05):** `mde-shell-egui/src/iac.rs` (surface state + Overview render + the `action/cloud/get-catalog` non-blocking request/reply poll, folding the shared `mackes_mesh_types::openstack` `ServiceCatalog`/`ServiceHealth` off the Bus ‚Äî no shell‚Üímackesd dep, ¬ß6) + `Surface::InfraCode` wired into `dock.rs` (enum / `ALL` / `icon_id` / Workloads group) + `main.rs` (dispatch + in-view poll). The live-cloud smoke is IAC-6.

- [‚úì] **IAC-3: the Resources tab ‚Äî per-service CRUD via the menu bar.**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** to manage every service's resources,
  **so that** the workspace is the full OpenStack admin.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] drilling a service shows its **read-only resource tables** (sortable, row + bulk select); **every cataloged service** with a resource collection gets a section (catalog-driven, auto-covers new services via `default_collection`); honest per-service querying / not-configured / unreachable / no-resources states (¬ß7)
    - [‚óê] the **mutating verbs live in the catalog-driven menu bar** (one menu per drillable bucket ‚Äî Drill / Refresh resources, + **Compute's armed Nova lifecycle** Start/Stop/Reboot/Delete on the selected instance); **typed-arming** on every destructive mutation (#22); real Bus/API calls (no mockups). **Deferred (honest ¬ß8, omitted not faked):** the generic create/update **forms** (flavor/image/network pickers) + generic resource create/update/delete verbs beyond the Compute lifecycle ‚Äî no landed Bus seam yet, so omitted rather than a dead menu
    - [‚óê] the **linked cross-service view** ‚Äî a selected instance offers jumps to the other cataloged services (Network / Volume / Orchestration), selection follows the link (the target section highlights); honest "not cataloged" when a link target is absent. The arming gate + tab/render/menu/fold seams are unit-tested; a live create/delete round-trip is IAC-6 (needs the create/delete verbs above + a throwaway project)
    - **Landed (IAC-3, 2026-07-05):** the shared `list-resources` wire contract ‚Äî `ResourceTable`/`ResourceRow` + a pure `from_collection_json` parser + `default_collection` in `mackes-mesh-types::openstack` (6 unit tests); the real mackesd `action/cloud/list-resources` Bus verb reusing IAC-1's `ResourceApi`/`Session` client via a new `ResourceSource` seam + a `CloudClient` supertrait (`LiveOpenStack` authenticates ‚Üí REST `list` ‚Üí parses; honest `Unconfigured` gate / transport-failure degrade; 3 verb tests ‚Äî genuinely live end-to-end for Nova servers + Heat stacks on a real Kolla cloud); and `mde-shell-egui/src/iac.rs` ‚Äî the Overview | Resources | Heat **tab bar**, the **Resources** tab (per-service sortable tables off `list-resources`, row + bulk selection, non-blocking request/reply per the IAC-2 idiom), the **catalog-driven per-service menus** (MENUBAR-ALL governing principle), **typed-arming** on the destructive lifecycle verbs, the **linked jump bar**, and the **Heat** honest-empty state (IAC-4). No shell‚Üímackesd dep (¬ß6). The live-cloud verb-path tuning (per-service collection versioning) is the IAC-6 smoke.

- [ ] **IAC-4: the Heat tab ‚Äî the native IaC loop.**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** Heat stacks/templates/drift + reverse-generate,
  **so that** infrastructure-as-code is first-class.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [ ] list/show stacks; view + edit **HOT templates**; **preview-update** (dry-run diff of what would change); create/update/delete (typed-armed); **stack-check** (drift); events + resources drill
    - [ ] **reverse-generate** a HOT template from the live discovered infra (capture reality as code); tested a stack lifecycle + a drift detect + a reverse-generate against fixtures/a live cloud

- [ ] **IAC-5: audit + notify + comprehensive menu bar.**
  **As** an operator,
  **I want** every op audited + failures surfaced, via one comprehensive bar,
  **so that** ops are traceable + all controls are reachable.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [ ] the **dynamic per-service menu bar** (one menu per advertised service carrying its full standard verb set + Catalog/View/Help, auto-growing) via the MENUBAR-ALL-1 shared component ‚Äî surfaces ALL controls incl. advanced (the governing principle), honest omit/disable
    - [ ] every mutating op ‚Üí the KDC hash-chained audit log; the mesh notify feed fires **only on failure/service-down** (CHAT-FIX-2 producer); tested the audit append + a failure notify

- [ ] **IAC-6: live smoke on the test bed.**
  **As** the operator,
  **I want** the IaC workspace verified against a real cloud,
  **so that** it's truly done.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [ ] on the farm dev cloud / test bed: the status band shows the real catalog health; the directory lists real services; a real Resources op (e.g. list + an armed create/delete) round-trips; a Heat stack shows/drifts; captured/confirmed (¬ß7 live-verify). *(coordinate with QUASAR-CLOUD live cloud availability)*
